[kakawin sumanasāntaka,

#Awiǥnama astu#

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ pinakādidewa ni karas para kawi makatattwa ṅ akṣara,
saŋ saṅkan paran iŋ palambaṅ atiduṙllaƀa kahanan ira n kawīśwara,
saŋ sūkṣmê kukus iŋ tanaḥ kinikir iŋ kuku ri sĕḍĕṅ iṅ aṅrĕgĕp laṅö,
māyākāra winimba nitya sinamāđi manurunana caṇḍi pustaka*

sambanđanya k aṅaṙccanê pada nirâhyun ajar ajara milwa riŋ kawi,
yekī kāraṇa ni ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti ri sira magawe namaskrĕti,
luṅgaḥ niŋ kalaṅön sapuṅgĕl asĕkaṙ kakawin inuparĕṅgan iŋ laṅö,
puṣpāñjalya ri jöŋ nira n sumanasāntaka caritakĕnâstu sanmatan*

pūṙwwaprastuti niŋ kaŧā hana sira dwija taruṇa suśīla subrata,
śiṣyâgastya sira prakāśa karĕṅö kasutapan ira nora tan wruha,
ꝁyātîŋ rāt trĕṇawindu nāma pinakesi niṅ ujar ujar iŋ kadewatan,
sakweḥ niŋ hyaṅ anaṅśayê hyuna nirâṅadĕha ri paṅadĕg surāđipa*

ndan saŋ hyaŋ suranāŧa muꝁya pinakādi niṅ awĕdi manaṅśayê hati,
lwiṙ tan duḥka sira ndan i twas awiweka riṅ aṅĕnana de niṅ olaha,
gūḋākāra nira n wikalpa kadi tan hana panaha nahā nirâlaha,
prāyê saŋ suyaśa n tĕka ŋ ƀaya sakêŋ musuh awĕdi kaciry-anâwĕdi*

wwantĕn rakwa warāpsarī linĕwih iŋ sa haripada wagĕd wicakṣaṇa,
prajña dyaḥ hariṇīṅaranya tuwi waṅśaja wĕka wĕka dewaputrikā,
sākṣāt hrū nikaṅ indracāpa suƀagêṅid iṅidan i hayunya dug siṅī,
Aṅhiŋ sāra hiḍĕp hyaṅ indra śaraṇāśraya paṅalaha śakti niŋ tapa*

yekī rakwa kinon hyaṅ indra marĕkâṅucap ucapa rahasya riŋ taman,
śīǥrânĕmbah acum wulat nika sinuṅsuṅ iṅ ujar amanis priyambada,
Om putrī saṅ anĕmwa kāṣṭaguṇan aṅhilaṅakĕna kaśaktin iŋ tapa,
Aṅhiŋ māsku sinamƀawâsiha paṅöbana niṅ aśaraṇêŋ kadewatan*

wwantĕn brāhmaṇa sidđiśakti magawe tapa katĕka tĕkêŋ surālaya,
maṅde saṅśaya ni ṅhulun ndan alĕmĕḥ katĕṅĕra ri wikalpa niŋ hati,
saŋkṣepanya lumampahânaku mamañcana maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
Eñjiŋ māsku lumakwa wörakĕna riŋ hima sumiliba tan hana wruha*

nāhan de nira mojar asru paṅutus nira lumarisa tan wruh iŋ ƀaya,
kepwan dyaḥ hariṇī katon gĕgĕh i suṅsut ira yadin apakṣa laṅǥana,
rĕs lāwan pagĕh iŋ kaƀaktin ika kāraṇa niki n uƀaya n lumampaha,
paṅgil paṅhwata janma liŋnya sĕḍĕṅanya karahatana riŋ pamañcanan*

mantuk dyaḥ hariṇī manĕmbah i surendra ri wijila nikā madandana,
Eñjiŋ maṅkat akañcugâdarupa ƀūṣaṇa nika pinasaŋnya tūt hĕnū,
tan kwâmbĕknya lumampa lampah aṅĕliḥ kasusu laku nikâṅhade hade,
denyâđaṙmma ri de nirâṅutus amiǥnanana tapa tatan hanâṅrwaṅi*

ṅūni n pamwit i jöŋ surendra mamĕgĕŋ taṅis inimur imuṙ kinölakĕn,
maṅke n sāmpun adoḥ lakunya wĕnaṅ aṅlĕpasakĕna taṅisnya riŋ hawan,
lagy-ânambatakĕn laranya kasihan pati sĕsĕl anĕsĕl purākrĕta,
tūt māṙggāmbara luḥnya tan papĕgatan drawa kadi titis iŋ maṇik bañu*

kāṅĕn denya katuhwan iŋ giṇa mamiǥnani tapa wipaŧâgawe hala,
yadyastun kawaśā pira ŋ suꝁa tĕmun yan amuhara hala ndya don ikā,
mwaŋ yan tan kawaśā katon tĕtĕp i śāpa nira paṅawaśanya tan wuruŋ,
kodāsīnan irêka ta pwa pinalaṙ palar ika siha saŋ hyaṅ īśwara*

mampĕḥ mātra laranya luḥnya pinakembuh i manis i matanya yan wulat,
luṅsuṙ luṅsur ikaŋ tapiḥ pinakatambĕh i raras i tĕṅaḥ nikâlaris,
hrĕknyâlwan ya samaṙ samaṙ tuna tunâmuwuhi manis i de nikâṅucap,
Aśrī waṙṇna nikâṅĕliḥ wĕnĕs ikâṅhalĕpi kadi wĕnĕs niṅ abrata*

luṅhā lampah ikânĕlat ri hirĕṅ iŋ gagana hanan awās hanan samaṙ,
rĕp mukṣânusup iŋ rĕmĕŋ kadi wulan lumaku kasaputan lamad lamad,
lwiṙ wintaŋ sumurup katonan ika riŋ wĕkasan asĕmu maṙmmakê kapö,
rĕm niŋ meǥa tinūtakĕnya manicip nicipi jawuh awaṙṇna cātaka*

rāmyanya n pamĕgat laṅit lĕpas adoḥ tĕka ri sadawatā nikaŋ limut,
Agyā de ni panas hyaṅ aṙkka karaṇanya n alisuh atawĕŋ tawĕŋ hima,
prāpta ŋ truḥ sumaput praƀāwa ni lakunya wahu mari huyaŋnya kāṅinan,
tūt gaṅgâhawan indracāpa tumurun lari nika suꝁa mampir iŋ wukiṙ*

watw-ânuṅgul amaṙwwatâhrit aguhâtupis atiba tiban latāṅkura,
ṅkā teka n dumunuŋ lukaṙ ni darupanya pinahayu lugas siniṅsĕtan,
tistis tan hana tīṙŧayātra wiku śakty-atapa katĕmu śūnya kewala,
Aṅhiŋ handiwa handiwâgarawalan katĕmu marĕk anuṅsuṅ iŋ guyu*

priṅgâtyanta ruhuṙnya mānuṣa paran wĕnaṅa mara ri doḥnya duṙggama,
ṅhiŋ saŋ paṇḍita saŋ huwus tumĕmu ṅ aṣṭaguṇa sira wĕnaŋ marêrika,
hetu dyaḥ hariṇī wĕnaŋ mara kajanman ika saꝑala dewakanyakā,
lĕṙ denya n tumurun sawaŋ garagatī tumurun ahawan antih antihan*

tiṅhalnyâbayaṅan mamet i patapan saṅ atapa parananya bañcanan,
riŋ winđyācala rîndrakīla salĕbak wukir ika pinaran katuṅkulan,
mwaŋ riŋ rewatakāgra ganđamadanādri masamun apa tan hanâtapa,
hetunya n ƀramitâpĕgâkuliliṅan kadi pakalaṅan iŋ niśākara*

lambuŋ niŋ himawān kidul hana ta paṙwwata śuci patapan hañaṙ katon,
tumraŋ teja nika praƀāwa nira saŋ sutapa tilaka niŋ jitendriya,
Aṅlīlâṅililan pahoman ira söḥ kukus ika maṅadĕg nirantara,
lwīr oṅkāra mawindunāda kadi hĕnwa nira hĕlĕm anĕmwa śūnyatā*

budđi dyaḥ hariṇī tumiṅhal irikaŋ patapan asĕmu haṙṣa niścaya,
byaktâwās trĕṇawindu ta pwa makapājaran iki liṅ ikânĕhĕṙ marĕk,
līlâṅambah i hambal iŋ jalada saṅsaya samar asamun hibĕk jawuḥ,
miṅsoṙ lwīr ahawan turun turunan iŋ gupura suꝁa hanan kadînuluṙ*

prāptêŋ paṙwwata śūnya kaywan ika pakṣa wukir asĕgĕh iŋ hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ,
haṙyyan mwaŋ hujuṅan sakêŋ pisaṅ alasnya rumarasah amet kalālatā,
sakweḥ niŋ wulakan sumaṅgraha bañunya walahar ika pakṣa sāgara,
jaṅgâṅambĕki pakṣa kasturi waṅinya hinaturakĕn iŋ drĕs iŋ barat*

wahw-âron anak iŋ pakis haji katon sukĕt i pasusupanya duṙggama,
sakweḥ niŋ kayu nora tan pagati de niṅ anila tĕka riŋ trĕṇāṅkura,
ndan trāsâsĕpi tan paron kapanasan paḍa ragas amalaṙ malaṙ jawuḥ,
waṅkal seṅwan alīt alīt bataṅ agöṅa hĕlĕm i paṅadĕgnya riŋ juraŋ*

lwiṙ tan pahyaṅ ikāṅ alas hana giraŋnya wahu linawad iŋ warāpsarī,
tapwan maṙmma dahat panuṅsuṅ ika kewala kusuma yayā maweḥ suꝁa,
lumrâkweḥ tumibêŋ gĕluŋ kadi tinap sawaṅ aṅit aṅitan sĕkaṙ taji,
kady-âṅĕmbaṅ akon aṅantya pakamaṅgala nika tanĕmĕn ya dewatī*

lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ talagânamaṙ tasik anak tuna tuna kawi nora maṅlĕṅĕŋ,
paṅgaŋ wwadnya kakumbah iŋ bañu suluṙnya wahu mĕtu satuŋtuṅ iŋ tanaḥ,
I groŋ groṅ i pasiṙ pasiṙnya mawatu dyan aniru niru piṇḍa niŋ karas,
līlâṅanti darā putiḥnya kadi śaṅꝁa madulur aṅurambat iŋ hĕnī*

ṅkā ta dyaḥ hariṇī marâdyus amĕḍaṙ tĕṅah abuṅah amawwahan gaḍiŋ,
māliḥ ṣaṭpada niŋ saroruha maliwran i wĕtis ika kesisan tapiḥ,
romanyâwilĕtan marê susu nikâniru niru rakĕt iŋ lumut lumut,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ kumudâṅliliṙ kadi tinaṅhi winulatan ikâṅdadak mĕkaṙ*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

ri sāmpun ika mĕntas aṅliga ligā kadi taman aśarīra dewatī,
titis titis ikaŋ wĕhaŋ satitis iŋ bañu wulakan anumbĕr iŋ paras,
lumöṅ amiluluk gaḍiŋ kahudanan susu nika kasarambahan bañu,
sirat ni bañu niŋ gĕluŋ kinirab aṅhiribi kukus i sāri niŋ puḍak*

titis ni mađu niŋ mađubrata baṅun lĕṅa waṅi humaḍaŋ hanêŋ śilā,
pawitra hana tīṙŧa niṙmmala sumaṅgraha ri harĕp awaṙṇna pahyasan,
hrĕbuk hrĕbuk i kĕmbaṅ iŋ sarasijâsĕmu hawu hawu muṅgu riŋ cupu,
hirĕŋ ni kucup iŋ trikañcu sumĕlat kadi sipat awawan puḍak puḍak*

lumampah aṅĕliḥ kaṅelan apa tan tahu mahas ahas iŋ wanāśrama,
sĕkaṙ niṅ asanâmayuŋ kuniṅ apiṇḍa mamayuṅana kāla niŋ panas,
paḍâṅrĕs atatā ŋ wuluḥ kadi harĕp tĕkĕnakĕna tan intar aṅhaḍaŋ,
gaḍuŋ kadi kamāsihĕn paḍa lumuŋ baṅun aharĕp anuntunêŋ hĕnū*

huwus tĕka riṅ āśramâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ry-ulaha nika mĕne n panĕmbaha,
nĕhĕṙ lumaku muṅgah iŋ gupura saṅśaya manaha nahā marê dalĕm,
Aluṅguh irikaŋ bukuṙ paṅaraṅanya nĕhĕr asidĕhâṅure gĕluŋ,
cĕcĕk masahuran sakê wuri pinakpak ika pinakadūta niŋ hala*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

ƀagawān trĕṇawindu sĕḍĕṅ ajapa nitya śiwasmaraṇa,
Asamāđi kumöl katĕmu hĕniṅ i budđi nira n humĕnĕŋ,
dwija śukla suśīla sira pinakadaṙśśana riŋ patapan,
kadi wꜽṣṇawawimba pawulatan ira n pamutĕṙ guduha*

I rare nira ṅūni hati nira hibĕk sukĕt aṅrahabi,
Inĕnö ni rajaḥ tamah ira karaṇanya n aron asĕwö,
Atuha pwa sira wruh aṅaji guṇa niŋ guru nora kari,
hana sattwaguṇâmaṅani sukĕt i budđi nira n patapa*

wijayêŋ patapan dwijawara makasāđana yoga nira,
Anukūla ri jöŋ nira sahana niṅ indriya nora wani,
Aṇimā laǥimādi kakaratala de ni samāđi nira,
kamumukṣuhan aṅhaḍa marĕk akĕliṙ swaśarīra nira*

ri huwus ni samāđi nira linĕsu rakwa harĕp mijila,
Anĕlat rarab iŋ rĕrĕb aṅuraṅi tan panĕlĕs harĕpan,
larap iŋ kilat iŋ gagana kadi dinĕmwan aganti lumöŋ,
paṅapö ni gĕrĕḥnya kadi mamisiki n hana wāhu ḍatĕŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

mijil muniwarâhawan hĕniṅ i budđi nira laku nirâṅhade hade,
pijĕṙ mulat i posik iŋ jalađi rāmya tĕpi nika katuṅku tuṅkulan,
ri tiṅhal ira riŋ bukuṙ saṅ araras winulatan ira maṅligā ligā,
ya kāraṇa nira n parâgarawalan saṅ ahayu tumuluy madan tapiḥ*

saṅ ugratapa niṙwīkara tamūyan wĕkas iṅ ahayū riŋ kādĕwatan,
salaḥ sĕmu manis manis nira baṅun manis iṅ anĕmu mitra riŋ hĕnū,
dudū suꝁa nira n mulat paḍa lawan suꝁa niṅ atamuyan kadaŋ kadaŋ,
Ikaŋ turida rāga sāmpun amatĕḥ milu milu mamiratyakĕn manaḥ*

Aniṅsĕti hĕniŋ ni budđi nira śudđa ni basahan ira n siniṅsĕtan,
subadđa daluwaŋ siṅī pinakabadđa nira pamađa riŋ rajaḥ tamaḥ,
samaṙ tura turaḥ ni ƀasma nira paṅgĕsĕṅ ira wiṣayâtĕmaḥ hawu,
jamaŋ kadi mahā taraṅtaṅĕn i sampĕt ira huwus anampĕtîndriya*

marĕk sira sulakṣaṇâdara maṅakṣama kamĕna nira n paluṅguha,
katon upaśamâtalaṅkup aṅagĕm kayu kanaka supattralepana,
tamuy nira masewa đaṙmma pakatonan i manah ika ƀakti kewala,
prasidđa guru śiṣya rūpa nira kālih i papupul irêrikaŋ bukuṙ*

Anĕmbah ikaṅ apsarī mĕtu rarasnya tan asarag aṅambĕk ambĕki,
lĕmĕs ni luṅayanya kālih ajajaṙ kadi pĕpĕsa kahambĕṅ iŋ susu,
laris ni jarijinya sāmpun atalaṅkup inayat inamĕṙ marêŋ muꝁa,
Amatyakĕn i raśmi raśmi ni liriŋnya n api miṅay aṅīrakĕn wulat*

lanâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt dwijeśwara tumon hayu nika winiweka riŋ hati,
tulis kanaka wahw-inuṅkaban aṅāśraya ri buṅah ika n paƀūṣaṇa,
Ahadyan ahĕnĕŋ nĕhĕṙ masidĕhâsĕmu taruban i kāla niŋ gawe,
yadin haliwatêŋ saƀā tan alaraŋ halĕpakĕna maḍampa mās tatuṙ*

sinaṅśaya nirâlumâluñuta mađya nika kulayĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,
suśūnya winaliŋ nirêmwa gamĕlĕn ri kahiḍĕpan ikôṇḍuh oṇḍuhan,
wĕtisnya kadi maṙwwi maṅgarita paṅkwakĕna kahiḍĕpanya de nira,
muꝁanya gumawaŋ ya rakwa tinahâlwaṅa hilaṅa ri kāla niŋ tilĕm*

hyaṅ iŋ nagara kālasan pawulatanya n anuruni rikaŋ wanāśrama,
mađubrata baṅun pinañjiṅan ikâṅidĕri salaga mĕtta riŋ sĕkaṙ,
puḍak kadi panĕmpa nĕmpahan ikâsĕmu maniliha lambay iŋ ṭikā,
Amānuṣa hayunya kenaka nikâmulaṅunakĕna riŋ jitendriya*

kayogyan iṅ apiṇḍa ratna liniṅiṙ saparana nika ta pwa hĕmbanĕn,
hade kumĕḍapa n wulat yan aṅadĕg tĕhĕr aṅadĕga tan paluṅguha,
yadin lukara kenya tan wruh amahaywa kahalĕp ika denya n aṅligā,
sawaŋ sawaṅ iṅ aṅhĕmū guyu kapantĕs ika pamapaganya riŋ wulat*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

Āścaṙyya budđi ƀagawān trĕṇawindu denya,
ndātan hana hyun ira mātra sumöṅa riŋ twas,
kewalya susŧira manaḥ nira tan prapañca,
maswāgatâmanis ujaṙ nira sāṙjjawâtwaŋ*

rakryan kṣamākĕna kamîbu paran kitâri,
strī tan wruh iŋ ƀaya ri duṙggama niŋ wanādri,
Aṅhiŋ katon kita wĕnaŋ mara niṙwīkāra,
prāptâṅĕnĕs maniluman baṅun indrajāla*

Āsĕṅka ni ṅhulun i māsku tĕkanta maṅko,
strī niŋ wiśeṣapuruṣa praƀu cakrawaṙtti,
tan saḥ kinuṇḍaṅ i sĕḍĕŋ niṅ aburwa burwan,
ndā ṅke n katĕmwa samayanta lawan priyanta*

strī tan pađaṙmma ta kunaŋ kita kāri śoka,
swāminta tan pahamĕṅan kawi tan pawasŧa,
Ambĕkta wikwa manusup nusupêṅ alas göŋ,
sambin hiḍĕpta wulikĕn palarĕn katĕmwa*

Anwam kunaŋ kita katuṅhapan iŋ bapebu,
muṅgw-iŋ kadaŋ maṅupapīra maweḥ larâmbĕk,
māṙgganta lampus aṅusiṙ wanadeśa śūnya,
Ahyun lumakwa wiku kilya rarā wiratya*

hyaŋ hyaŋ niṅ āśrama kunaŋ kita diwyacakṣuḥ,
wruḥ riŋ jitendriya sadābrata tan kĕnêŋ strī,
budđinta moǥa mawĕlas mulat iŋ daridra,
prāptânurun paran ikā paṅanugrahanta*

rakryan hiḍĕpku ri hayunta sakêŋ wanādri,
Ambĕt ni sinwam iṅ aśoka marê tĕṅaḥta,
molaḥ kadînĕluk ĕluk luṅ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ mrik,
tan saḥ katon i luṅayanta lĕmĕs lĕmĕsnya*

Amraŋ baṅ iŋ katirah aṙjja hanê laṭinta,
tuñjuŋ birū mĕkar alurw-akusū suganđa,
māliḥ lurunya mamanis kawawê matanta,
mimbâmarāśraya tikĕlnya hanê halista*

polaḥ nikaŋ kusumasāri hanê wiwalta,
maṅgiṣṭa wāhu rinĕmĕk tumibê kĕcapta,
paṅhrĕŋ nikaŋ ƀramara muṅgw-i taṅis taṅista,
hīs niŋ tusāra rumarab makajanma luḥta*

sandeha budđi mami de ni halĕpta māsku,
dūra n manuṣya kita kewala dewaputrī,
de niŋ manaṙkka ri ḍatĕŋta mahāpraƀāwa,
saṅkê hyaṅ indra mapa donta waraḥ kamîbu*

nāhan panaṙkka nira maṙmma dahat rasanya,
mambö tilam kadi huwus wruh i rumrum iŋ strī,
śrĕṅgāra dewaduhitā kawĕlad hatinya,
maṅgĕḥ ri budđi ƀagawān kĕna bañcananya*

<Akrĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

suraputrikā sumahur ādara mulat awiraŋ tumuṅkul anaṅis,
ƀagawān rĕṅön pawarah i ṅhulun aṅusir aṅāśrayê kadi kita,
taha tan sakê surapati n ḍatĕṅ aṅĕnĕs amet pradeśa wĕgilĕn,
mwaṅ asamƀawa n hyaṅa niṅ āśrama panaha nahā dwijeśwara hade*

tuwi tan manuṣya maniwi praƀu madulur aburwa burwa riṅ alas,
hayu ni ṅhulun taha tan antuk iṅ aṅalap alap sakêŋ giriwana,
riṅ apa n rarâharĕpa wikwa manusupa manĕmbahêŋ wiku talun,
pisaniṅw-ajalwa kawi mūṙcꞓita layat alaṅö manambaṅ anadin*

ƀagawān manĕḥta huniṅan humulunakĕn awaknya tan patĕbusan,
tuwi hetu niŋ mara ri jöŋ dwija taruṇa ƀaṭāra đaṙmma maṅutus,
I ratĕŋ nikaŋ brata samāđi kakawaśa tĕkapta sāmpun amatĕḥ,
mĕtu tan pasaṅkan inucap wulatana tariman ṅhulun ꝑala nika*

hyaṅĕn i ṅhulun ri pada saŋ dwija taruṇa kaśudđyanôtus utusĕn,
pisanīṅw-anĕṅgaha mĕne n pasuruhana sĕkaṙ lawan bañu damu,
marĕkêŋ paturwan aṅisapwakĕna suku munīndra riŋ pakasutan,
tan asamƀawa n hulun anaṅhuluna yan apuyĕŋ dwijaṙṣi majapa*

Arĕnaḥ tĕkapnya n aṅucap kama riṅ ujar amiǥnani brata tapa,
mata mesi luḥ saha taṅis winulatakĕn ikā wineh amanisa,
Ajajaṙ pasaṅgraha nikā susu waṅi ni pipinya lāgi sumaji,
kadi pādapâṅlih alaris tĕṅah ika pasĕnāha ri dwijawara*

Umĕnĕŋ dwijaṙṣi rumase wacana nika tĕkā waśâṅhamu hamu,
smaradūta kewala manisnya n aṅucap ataṅis lanâmĕlas arĕp,
wĕkasan dwijendra wihikan ry-aƀimata nika yan pamiǥnani tapa,
mĕtu kadwijātyan ira nora kawĕdi nira sāhasânapaŧani*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

Aḍā wipaŧa ko pakojar iku đūṙtta tan aharĕp i haywa niŋ tapa,
huwus wruh aku yan pakona suranāŧa karaṇamu ḍatĕŋ mamañcana,
Ikaŋ hala gawemu tan wuruṅ amaṅsulana malĕsanêri ko mĕne,
manuṣya tĕmahamwa tan waluya riŋ surapada wĕkasamwa dewatī*

yadin śatasahasraƀāgan i suꝁaṅku n ataki taki niṣparigraha,
taŧāpi kapana n samaṅkana suꝁaṅkwa k aṅusira suꝁêŋ surālaya,
hana pwa suꝁa niŋ manuṣya masamāgama mapa ta gawe nikâđama,
lĕhĕŋ juga ṅ anĕmwa pātaka sakêŋ katuduhana kabañcanâtapa*

nahan liṅ ira sāhasâṅḍawuhi śāpa nĕhĕr anudiṅî kiwâṅdĕlö,
prapañca surakanyakā kahilaṅan hurip apĕga ri tan sih iŋ wiđi,
ri doṣa nika rāga rāga n aṅusiṙ sutapa pisaniṅūn kabañcana,
Alum kadi gaḍuŋ pinuṅgĕl aṅayuḥ sĕkar iṅ asana tan wuruŋ pĕjaḥ*

tumuṅkul i harĕp dwijaṙṣi makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ nira,
hanan kadi waśâṅdĕlö nĕhĕr aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ surālaya,
mĕhāḥ salahasâtĕpak jaja manĕmbah aḍĕkuh amalaṙ kasanmata,
Apan harĕp iṅ antaśāpa karaṇanya n aṅucap amanis maṅañjali*

dwijaṙṣi huripĕn ṅhulun titisanâmrĕta waluyakĕnêŋ kadewatan,
Ĕmās maṇik anekawastu kĕta ṅ enaka panĕbusa ni ṅhulun hurip,
ṅhulun pwa kasihan muwaḥ syapa pametana pirak i rikaŋ tapowana,
mataŋnya k anaṅis panĕmbaha ri jöŋta panĕbusa ri jīwa ni ṅhulun*

tuhanku ƀagawānku hāḥ sipi lalista wulatana manĕḥta kāsy-asiḥ,
harĕp muliha tan wĕnaŋ mulih aṅantya ri kita kita melik i ṅhulun,
Unĕŋ niṅ abapebu tiṅhalana denta mapa karika hetu niŋ hĕnĕŋ,
kĕdö harĕp anona māti kĕna śāpa karika kita tan wruh iŋ wĕlas*

Ahā mpu wihikan ṅhulun ri wuyuṅanta kalalarana śudđa niŋ tapa,
kṣamākĕna manĕḥta tan tugĕtananta sakasalah i śīla ni ṅhulun,
prasidđa kita paṇḍitânumata riŋ wiguṇa wipaŧa tan wruh iŋ krama,
si sĕmbah ika jampya niŋ kadi kita n lumĕkasa wuyuṅ iŋ kadi ṅhulun*

kucup niṅ asanâluru ndan amalaṙ karirisana ri taṅgal iŋ kapat,
gaḍuŋ lumay aṅolakĕn tawaṅ aluŋluṅan amalar anĕmwa rambatan,
hĕlaŋ midĕr anambayaŋ saha taṅis kapanasan amalaṙ drĕs iŋ jawuḥ,
ṅhulun pwa kalaran mataŋnya k amalaṙ turunana wara de dwijeśwara*

Ahā pahalawö ta koṅ awakana ŋ kapalaṅ alaṅ i demu n apsarī,
kadaŋ kadaṅa de bapebu pĕkulĕmwa paḍa kari sirêŋ kadewatan,
pĕjaḥ ṅaran iki syapêka ta taṅis taṅisana mulatâsihêri ko,
wĕlasku ri hayunya sis mapa tikī hamĕṅana niki yan pĕjaḥ mĕne*

ƀaṭāra suranāŧa tiṅhalana de nrĕpati kasih arĕp patik haji,
huwus kalĕmahan śināpa kapana n maluya muwah i pāda saŋ praƀu,
hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥ surāđipati tan wuruṅa pĕjaha riŋ pamañcanan,
riṅ āśrama wĕkas ni jīwita patik haji wiꝑala pakon surāđipa*

praƀu praƀu rĕṅön taṅis ni hariṇī kapĕgan aputĕk aṅhiḍĕp lara,
pĕjaḥ pinatiwaṙ kinonakĕn i tan kawĕnaṅ ika gawe dinohakĕn,
Ikaŋ gati śināpa sis ya katahā ya katĕmu tuluṅĕn patik haji,
pati pwa balik iŋ hurip lara lalis pwa balika ni wĕlas surāđipa*

wijil sahana saŋ hyaṅ iŋ kusuma wāhu sumalaga nihan lawad ṅhulun,
hurip gĕlisa ni ṅhulun ya palakunta ri yatiwara haywa tâsuwe,
kunaŋ yan agĕgĕḥ dwijaṙṣi palalun sawuyuṅ ira sadenya saṅkulĕn,
tuhun kita lumĕṇḍwa lĕṇḍwa ri śawaṅku gĕsĕṅĕn i pañaṇḍi niŋ wuṅū*

manis ni mata ni ṅhulun labuhĕn iŋ jalađi luh irikaŋ tasik mađu,
raras ni waja ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ śrigaḍiṅ i pucak iŋ gunuŋ gula,
lĕmĕs ni lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun lĕpasĕn iŋ gaḍuṅ aṅĕlih aṅolakĕn tawaŋ,
laris ni wĕtis i ṅhulun kĕkĕsananta kĕmitana ni dèwa niŋ puḍak*

kĕlab ni tapih i ṅhulun suji ya teki pupulakĕn i posik iŋ sĕkaṙ,
pataṅkis i giriṅsiṅ i ṅhulun aṅantya ri lĕṅĕṅ i kiriñciṅ iŋ bañu,
pĕnĕd ni laku ni ṅhulun tan asarag waluyakĕna ri lampah iŋ liman,
pĕpö ni panaṅisku tan kahuniṅā ḍawuhakĕna ri śabda niŋ cucuṙ*

Ameta maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kita pamorana ni kusut i roma ni ṅhulun,
ri mimba ni taman ta paṅlĕpasananta ri rĕṅu ni halisku yan tikĕl,
gĕmuḥ ni susu ni ṅhulun wahu mijil tuhañaṅakĕna riŋ pucaŋ gaḍiŋ,
wĕnĕs ni muꝁa ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ wulan inĕmukan iŋ lamad lamad*

pamādapa ni mađya ni ṅhulun aros kirimakĕn iṅ aśokapādapa,
Ĕbun hana ri tuŋtuṅ iŋ trĕṇalatāṅkura patuwawanê luh i ṅhulun,
lawan pañurigênunus ni paṅawakku rakĕtakĕna denta riŋ tulis,
luṅid ni kuku ni ṅhulun turuṅ aṅanya ri jaja jajar iŋ sĕkaṙ taji*

nahan śruti ni de nikânaṅis atuŋtuṅ ucapan amĕlas mĕlas harĕp,
samasta para dèwa sūkṣma humĕnĕŋ tinaṅisan ika tan hanâṅlawad,
Arĕs hawa hawākĕnâwĕdi kumöl wruh i gĕgĕh i wuyuŋ dwijeśwara,
paḍâṅrĕs anaṅis naṅis taṅis ikā piniturun ika muṅgu riŋ waneḥ*

taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ kusuma sūkṣma tinaṅisakĕn iŋ mađubrata,
taṅis niṅ amarāśrayêŋ wulan awā tinaṅisakĕn i śabda niŋ cucuṙ,
taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ jalada cātaka manaṅisakĕn hanêŋ tawaŋ,
taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ masa kapat tinaṅisakĕn i gĕntĕr iŋ patĕṙ*

muwaḥ dyah anu mojar asrĕt ucapanya tuna tuna sinambaṅan taṅis,
mpu ḍaŋ hyaṅ apa tāh inanti ni manĕḥta paṅuṣađa ri duḥka ni ṅhulun,
yatan hana hineṙ manĕḥ dwijawarâsiha humuripana ṅhuwus pĕjaḥ,
kṣamākĕna magöŋ ṅhulun mpu warahĕn duga duga mara tan harĕp harĕp*

nahan rasa ni de nikânaṅis aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ kadewatan,
Uđāni ƀagawān paṅawruhana de nira mulat amanis wawaŋ lipuṙ,
Apuy siniram iŋ jawuḥ paḍa ni suṅsut ira tan agĕgĕḥ wawaŋ paḍĕm,
sĕrĕḥ waṅi lawan duh iŋ wwah aramĕs ri waja paḍa ni de nirâṅucap*

paran karika tan sihaṅkwa ri kitânaku kita karikâpan uttama,
manuṣya tuwi sāwakanya yan atön mara mara hiniḍĕp kadaŋ kadaŋ,
kunaŋ saṅ agawe laranta paramāṙŧa nira sira ƀaṭāra śaṅkara,
lukat ni kapalaŋ nikaŋ sukrĕta māṙgga ni kapalaṅ i denta dewatī*

priyanta riṅ anādijanma dadi mānuṣa lituhayu sūṙyyawaṅśaja,
narendra raǥu rakwa mānak aniru prakaśita suƀagêŋ purāntara,
Apañjy-aja đanuṙdđarânwam isi niŋ raǥunagara turuŋ smarātura,
tuhun kita dine ƀaṭāra yugalanya muwah akurĕnâsihê kita*

kunaŋ pwa siha ni ṅhulun ri kita tan kalawasana dadinta mānuṣa,
Aṅālihana kapraƀun kita lawan saṅ aja suꝁa sarājya tuṅgalĕn,
tuhun pamĕkasanta wīja sawijîrika kita maluyêŋ kadewatan,
sĕkaṙ sumanasântakanta ya tikâmĕgatakĕna ri śāpa ni ṅhulun*

huwus pwa kita mantuk iŋ surapadânaku katĕka tĕkêŋ wwaluŋ tahun,
samaṅkana narendra saŋ kawĕkas iŋ nagara muliha riŋ kadewatan,
Apaṅgiha muwaḥ lawan kita tumĕmwakĕna ꝑala nikaŋ kadigjayan,
mataŋnya pahayun manaḥta suꝁamāṙgga matĕmahana rājaputrikā*

nahan rasa ni de nirâmĕgati śāpa nira tĕhĕr ajaṙ satorasiḥ,
ri mūla ni dadinya len tĕmahananya tinalatah irâgalaṙ taṅan,
kunaŋ pwa wĕkasan hiḍĕpnya ri kaśāpa nika kadi wineh anugraha,
Unĕŋnya matĕmaḥ luh adrĕs i kapö lara turida nikâtĕmaḥ taṅis*

hāḥ saŋ mukṣa ri luḥku tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjah iŋ pasaṅgaman,
maṅke pwâmbĕka niŋ prahāsana bisâṅhari harih iṅ arĕs pinaṅkwakĕn,
ṅūni n hyaŋ kita riŋ surālaya manĕḥta milu matĕmahan warāpsarī,
maṅke pwâṅdadi rājaputra kita heṙ ṅhulun atĕmaha rājaputrikā*

hāḥ swāmiṅku dudut ṅhulun ri juraṅ iŋ lĕpihan alal aṅölakĕn laṅö,

suŋsuŋ riŋ maṅunĕŋ galuḥ lulut unĕṅku ri kita kaka tan wĕnaŋ kinas,
riŋ paṇḍan haḍaṅĕn ṅhulun lumaku śoka laku laku ṭikâhawan puḍak*

de niŋ gyānya tumĕmwa janma saṅ aniṅgalakĕn iriya riŋ kadewatan,
Amwit matya manĕmbah iŋ dwijawarânĕhĕr aṅusapi luḥnya riŋ sabuk*

huwus praṇata ƀakti tan paśaraṇāśraya mati lumah iŋ pamañcanan,
humuŋ taṅis i sundarī nikaṅ alas hinariwuwu ni śabda niŋ gaguŋ,
rĕrĕb kusumasāri tan papĕgatan kĕtug i tĕḍun iṅ eṙttalîŋ juraŋ,
luṅ iŋ gaḍuṅ aṅindracāpa humaḍaŋ hawana nika madadya mānuṣa*

hyaṅ agni hana riŋ śarīra mijil aṅgĕsĕṅi śawa nikâgilaŋ gilaŋ,
kasidđyan ira saŋ dwijaṙṣi gumawe dilah ika karaṇanya n ujwala,
bukuṙ pamiḍaran ndatan milu gĕsĕŋ kadi jalada rinĕṅgan iŋ kilat,
samantaji paḍĕm tuhun hana kukusnya kari sakukus iŋ damaṙ pĕjaḥ*

hayunya milu ƀasmiƀūta tĕka riŋ gĕluṅ ahawuk amiṇḍa riŋ kukus,
lumöŋ wa nikaṅ asŧi mātra kadi śeṣa ni luru ni matanya yan wulat,
baṅun tura turaḥ nikaŋ sipat ikaŋ latu latu tumibā paḍâhirĕŋ,
hilaŋ sinirir iŋ samīraṇa hawunya tumuluy anarīra riŋ hrĕbuk*

saŋ hyaŋ niŋ suraloka tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjah iŋ pamañcanan,
sūkṣmâṅjanma marêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī sira ta pinakasāri niŋ sarāt,
putrī śrī kraŧakeśikeśwara nĕhĕṙ hayu nira kadi ṅūni n apsarī,
ꝁyāti śrîndumatī panaṅgah i sira n pamuꝁa kadi śaśaṅka pūṙṇnama*

lwīr iŋ swapna wijil nirâdƀuta karĕṅwan i wali nira riŋ kadewatan,
rĕmrĕm taŋ daśadeśa de ni sahab iŋ jaladakusuma muṅgu riŋ tawaŋ,
lĕŋlĕŋ de ni gĕrĕḥnya ṣaṭpada maliwran apupul irikaŋ limut hrĕbuk,
sumyuk taŋ mađupuṣpawaṙṣa maduluṙ jaya jaya ri jayā nrĕpātmajā*

ṅūni n tuṅgal anak nareśwara lawö manah ira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā,
ndātan pembuh ikaŋ suꝁê sira baṅun bañu humidĕṅ aṅanti riŋ ranu,
maṅke n pembuh anak nirâhayu sinamƀawa maṅadĕha lakṣmi niŋ purī,
Embuḥ göŋ kadi sāgara rwab amĕpĕk suꝁa nira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā*

rakryan saŋ pinakeña rakwa kulawaṅśa wĕka wĕka kadaŋ kadaŋ haji,
Aśrī waṙṇna nirâraras kadi saroja kinĕlabakĕn iŋ ṙyyak iŋ bañu,
de niŋ mĕñcuh aṅambĕk ambĕki saƀāwa nira tĕka hirĕŋ kineriṅan,
suswan bāhwan agasyak aṅhalĕpakĕn wruh iṅ aṅinakanê tuhan tuhan*

lāwan towi nirâhalĕp marĕka hadyana kunaṅ asawaŋ priyambada,
ndan paṙṇnaḥ kaka de nirêña nira karwa sira paḍa suśīla wīṙyyawan,
kāliḥ kālih irâṅharis haris anuswani rahina wĕṅî suputrikā,
saṅkêŋ swaṙgga hulun tuhâṅgĕh ira ṅūni ri hana nira riŋ kadewatan*

wwaŋ ri jro juru niŋ mĕṅĕs pinarĕk iŋ wagĕd amirit i hatwik iŋ manis,
sakwan selwan atūt manaḥnya kalawan kabayan iṅ arĕjêŋ kaguṇḍikan,
tuṅgal riŋ katĕkāsihan lawan ikaŋ pinuji pinakagusti riŋ raras,
rūm rakryan nrĕpaputrikā mawa hayunya tuhu ratu ni raśmi niŋ prajā*

strī māwak caturaṅga saƀya tan aŧāni panagara tĕkâhawan raŧa,
prāyâpāmbĕkan aśwasañcari lakunya wagĕd aniru lampah iŋ liman,
nistanya n wiparīta rūpa nika tan kasah i pada narendraputrikā,
himpĕṙ peka minantryakĕn huwus aƀūṣaṇa hinalĕpakĕn yayâhala*

rakryan rājasutânwam eṅgal atuhâṅiṅĕt iṅĕtakĕn aṅdĕlö tawaŋ,
Aṅliŋliŋ kinahaṙṣan iŋ kaka kakâmwaṅi sira rinĕbut pinaṅkwakĕn,
kahyun hyun kumurĕb kurĕb kumĕdal asriṅ aniru niru putra niŋ pĕñu,
wahw-âhuntw-aputiḥ katon sĕḍĕṅ irâsĕmu guyu baṅun aṅhĕmū mĕnuṙ*

solaḥ ƀāwa nirâmaṅun sih aṅĕwaḥ bapa bapa juga de nirâṅucap,
yan paṅjaṅkah aṅaṅguh aṅguhi gumoḥ lumaris asĕmu lĕmbu kanyakā,
mogâhyaŋ sira yan maluṅguh ararĕm tumiru tiru paluṅguh iŋ gaṇa,
yan sore mulat iŋ wulan wruh awawā wulan anuduhi wimba niŋ wulan*

Endaḥ budđi nikaŋ waneḥ mamitaṅis mitaṅis i sira haṙṣa riŋ taṅis,
Eṅgal mary-anaṅis pinakpak amanis wulat ira sinawe pinaṅkwakĕn,
len tekaŋ harĕp iŋ halâhala halan mamalaku hala hāsyakāraṇa,
maṅkin tībra raras narendratanayâhayu ri huwus ira n paweh ala*

Anwam tapwan apâsarik hayu nirân inaṅĕtan apupuk ri wunbunan,
tan paṅde hala tambĕh iŋ hayu bajaŋ bajaṅ ira mata niŋ lawak bulu,
pantĕs yan pagĕlaŋ lawe wĕnaṅ i kāla nira kapĕjahan rare bajaŋ,
tambā niŋ sĕgu tuŋtuṅ iŋ sĕrĕh aṅimbuhi manis ira yan hanê rahi*

ndi nyū danta paḍā mĕne n lĕwiha yan marĕk i sira sĕḍĕŋ pinaṅkwakĕn,
lāwan ketaka dūra n aṅhiriba nista nika n inuparĕṅgan iŋ ṭikā,
sakweḥ niŋ kusumâwĕnĕs pinakataṇḍiṅ ira wawaṅ alum sakêŋ taṅan,
maṅgĕḥ de niṅ anuswanî sira dudū lawan anak anakan sinuswakĕn*

Eṅgal wruḥ tinitaḥ bisâtaratayan wĕgig aṅadĕg adĕg wawaŋ tibā,
guywan wruḥ makukuk bayan tinañakĕn kahanan ira bisâtukup mata,
sorêsuk malĕbū lĕbū cala kinon ahuwusana ya saṅkan iŋ taṅis,
haṙṣânon gigirĕn sirâṅgyat anĕpak bisu bisu nĕhĕr aṅgigiṙ gigiṙ*

dudw-aṅkĕn wĕṅi de nira n wruh aṅucap mari bisu bisu saṅsayâbĕnĕṙ,
sāmpun rakwa sirâpupak pinakapūṙwwaka nira n aṅajî munīśwara,
prajña wruḥ ri kalīṅa niŋ pada kadi wruh alawas anulus wicakṣaṇa,
Eṅgal paŧya ri kaprayogan i rusit niṅ aji kadi tĕmaḥ saraswatī*

Umwat śīǥra tuwuḥ nirâhayu sawaŋ salaga niṅ asanâṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
tapwan wruḥ riṅ iraŋ dahat kalukaran tapih awuda wudâgĕlaŋ gĕlaŋ,
tan pendaḥ lĕṅĕṅ iŋ wuluḥ gaḍiṅ i kāla ni pamilĕt i luṅgah iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mambĕt mađya nirâwĕlū buṅah i waṙṇna nika kadi giliŋ giliŋ kuñit*

niṙwā tan pagūṇa ŋ pūpuṙ pinakāpahyas ira tĕwas aweḥ kram Iŋ muꝁa,
dūrâṅhaywana tan padon sipat irâṅlĕtuhi ri hĕniṅ iŋ matâbiru,
lāwan taŋ paṅĕluk lĕṅĕn wiꝑala yeka karaṇa ni halis nira n tikĕl,
wyaṙŧâŋ tūlahanânukĕṙ nukĕri tan wuruṅ amaṅunakĕn srĕt iŋ susu*

sumraŋ sraŋ mata wahw-atön ri lĕṅĕṅ iŋ gĕrĕh aṅirim irim lawan riris,
Aṅlūd ry-ambĕk ira n rimaŋ taṅis ikaŋ ƀramara kalilipĕn saḍĕk hrĕbuk,
yan sore ri huwus nirâhawu hawu wruh amawa kalaṅön irêŋ nataṙ,
Aṅhĕmban karas esi ƀāṣa pinakānak anakan ira tan sah iŋ tanaḥ*

piṇḍa dwādaśawaṙṣa kāla ni wijil nira rumara rara n hanê dalĕm,
yan paṅhyas hyasi moǥa tan kawanĕhan tiniru tiru sade nirâṅhyasi,
sotan ta ṅhyaṅ iṅ indraloka kapana n tan apĕnĕda tĕmaḥnya mānuṣa,
lakṣmī niŋ nagarâhulap mulat i rūpa nira n ahayu katwaṅ iŋ tulis*

miṅkil tapwan agöŋ payođara nirâṅlĕwihi buṅah i tuŋtuṅ iŋ gaḍiŋ,
hyaŋ hiŋ tāman aṅiṇḍarat sĕmu ni rūpa nira n ahayu muṅgu riŋ taman,
tistis lālana tan hanâṅiriṅakĕn laku nira kadi tan tuhan tuhan,
molaḥ sumpiṅ irâsanâlum awĕnĕs baṅun awĕdi ri luñcip iŋ mata*

paṅrāt niŋ kalaṅön tinurwakĕn irêŋ watu karaṅ aṅilo wway iŋ ranu,
tan śoƀā humiriŋ lumaḥ makakaraŋ hulu lĕṅĕn ira mūṙcꞓitâṅligā,
paṇḍan raṅkaṅ aṅöbi tan panisi mātra ri sira n apulaŋ lawan hrĕbuk,
Amrĕm karwa karas lĕṅĕŋ kadi ṭikā piniturun inamĕṙ sakêŋ puḍak*

maṅkin maṙmma narendra māsih anĕkāni samaṅinakanê manaḥ nira,
budđi śrī parameśwarī suꝁa makānak i sira samanaḥ nirênariḥ,
maṅke n tan hana wahw-atakwan ahiḍĕp nrĕpati tĕka sirâṅhĕmū guyu,
maṅgĕḥ budđi nirâjajaṙ lawan anak nira baṅun aṅabehi jīwita*

saŋ ƀojânak irâtuhâpagĕh ikaŋ guṇa ri sira paṅawruh iŋ ratu,
sākṣāt prāṇawa Īśwara nrĕpati kāsih ira sira suśīla nītimān,
Aṅhiŋ rakwa pakö nareśwara ri ƀūmi nira sira sadā janapriya,
maṅgĕḥ rowaṅ irâṅadĕg ri hiḍĕp iŋ mulat i suꝁa nira n paḍâpagĕḥ*

ndan griŋ saŋ praƀu saṅsayâbwat atĕlĕb maṅinak inaki tan tulus waras,
tĕṅrān iŋ hurip iŋ śarīra paḍa rūkṣa mawarah i tĕkā nikaŋ pati,
yekā hetu nirâṅutus marĕka riŋ dwijawara rĕṣi śꜽwa sogata,
mwaŋ mantrī winĕkas wĕkas nira n anak nira sumiliha ratwa haywa len*

sakweḥ saŋ winĕkas wĕkas paḍa tĕñuḥ twas ira kahĕnĕṅan mulat juga,
de niŋ duḥka tumon i kāsy-asih i saŋ kawĕkas ira dumeḥ sirâsiha,
mojaṙ mātra pĕgat pĕgat wĕkasan amrih asayut amĕlas mĕlas harĕp,
luḥ lāwan sĕkĕl iŋ taṅis dulur i de nira sumahur i śabda saŋ praƀu*

he nāŧaṅku huwus kapaṅku wacana nrĕpati rasa nirâwĕkas wĕkas,
An saŋ ƀoja gumantya ratwakĕna yadyapi pĕjaha mĕne nareśwara,
ndan lwiṙ wyaṙŧa ḍawuḥ ni śabda naranāŧa ri sama marĕk aṅlawad lawad,
Āpan ṅhiŋ sira keṅĕ keṅĕt alawas kumalilirana kapraƀun haji*

śaktin de naranāŧa haywa lĕsu saŋ praƀu tahapana wedya kinkinĕn,
śrī dewîndumatī katoliha katon uwuh uwuha nira n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja sirânwam aṙdđa kapalaŋ wĕkasakĕna narendra riŋ prajā,
ndān amriḥ mriha saŋ praƀu syapa parāśrayana sama marĕk mĕne n kari*

nāhan liŋ sama maṅlawad lawad i saŋ praƀu lara nira membuh aṅlare,
wahw-âṅlumpuhi saṅsayâmaṅĕti roga nira wawaṅ alum sirâwĕnĕs,
tan polaḥ sira tan kĕḍap ṅuni ṅuni n paṅucapa sira kewalâturū,
ṅhiŋ maṅguḥ kalawan miṅĕl sahur ira n tinaña tañan i de nirâlara*

satya śrī parameśwarī tan awĕdîŋ pati tumuta ri līna saŋ praƀu,
ndan dewîndumatī tinolih ira kāsy-asiha nira mĕne n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja paḍânwam anwam anaṅis paḍa wihikan i tībra saŋ praƀu,
kāliḥ kālih irâpupul tinaṅisan pinĕkul ira nĕhĕṙ sinuṅkĕman*

Ꜽ ƀojaṅku wĕkaṅku haywa tan asiḥ kita bapa riy arinta kāsihan,
putrīṅkw-indumatīṅku ƀaktya ri kakanta kita sarika samƀawâsiha,
Anwam kāri tuhanku deṅku kawĕkas riṅ iña lawan uwâmalaṙ tuha,
himpĕṙ hantiga niŋ manuk taḍahasiḥ sy-anaku tinuwawākĕn iŋ waneḥ*

wuṅsw-amwīta bibinta matya tumutê kapati saṅ ahulun ṅhulun tuhan,
lwâmbĕk māsku saṅ aprihêŋ ƀuwana sĕmbahĕn iṅ amawa rāt kitânaku,
Ꜽ putrîndumatīṅku māsku t ahurup tapih alah ibu kenku kenakĕn,
soŋsoṅaṅkwa tapiḥta karwana lawan haji lĕpasa mamukṣa mukṣana*

sĕmbaḥ ni ṅhulun alpađaṙmma ri padadwaya paramawiśeṣapaṇḍita,
pun dewîndumatī kayatnakĕna de wiwuđapati bapebwa māsiha,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja muwaḥ wuruk wurukĕn iŋ nagara palar aniṙwwa saŋ praƀu,
waṙṣājñāna parâđipaṇḍita dumadyakĕna kawijayanya riŋ prajā*

nāhan liŋ parameśwarī tucapa saŋ praƀu kasih arĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,
saŋ hyaŋ jīwa hanê gulū nira lawan kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira saṅsayâsamun,
sāmpun kāku pasāra sāra ni waraḥ yatiwara rinĕgĕp nareśwara,
tan simpaŋ kadi de nirâṅayatakĕn panah aṅĕnani de nirâṅhiḍĕp*

trĕṣṇābanđana riŋ śarīra pinĕgat nira manah ira kewalâhĕniŋ,
sadyotkranti linakṣyakĕn pataṅananya tumutupana simpaṅ iŋ hĕnū,
lāwan mantra nikā ndatan dwa sira saŋ praƀu wiƀu riṅ awak wawaŋ mĕsat,
kewalyâśraya sūkṣma māri kahiḍĕp mamarĕṅi śiwamāṙgga dug mĕṅā*

sāmpun māti nareśwarâtri sakaḍatwan anaṅisi pĕjaḥ nirâlara,
śrī dewîndumatī muwaḥ tinaṅisan kapati lumay awak nirâwĕnĕs,
mādan śrī parameśwarī marĕk anĕmbah i śawa haji satya sādara,
mājaṙ yan sira milwa matya pawaraḥ nira karaṇa ni luḥ niṅ aṅrĕṅö*

he nāŧaṅku nihan ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti tumuta saparanta tan saha,
yadyastun kita dewatâŧawa manuṣya huluna pakĕnaṅkwa de haji,
putrī putra rarā sĕḍĕŋ mĕrĕ mĕrĕḥ kaŧamapi tan ikā katoliha,
patrĕmta praƀu yeki haṇḍĕmana ni ṅhulun amah aku suŋsuṅ iŋ hĕnū*

nā liŋ śrī parameśwarī nĕhĕr apatrĕm amĕkasi hurip sirâsĕgu,
himpĕṙ waṙṣa tibā nikaŋ luh i widaṙbƀanagara humilī mawaḥ wahan,
sambat sambat ikaŋ sarājya gumĕrĕḥ kadi kĕtĕr i gĕrĕḥ niṅ ampuhan,
tawwan riŋ kusumâṅjrah iŋ masa kapat paḍa ni taṅis ikā n rinĕṅwakĕn*

prāpta ŋ truḥ kadi sĕmbu sĕmbur i jajâṅawara ri gĕmuh iŋ payođara,
waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ kuwuŋ kuwuṅ apiṇḍa pupuk i rahi keṅgutan halis,
polaḥ niŋ kilat iŋ tawaŋ kadi kĕḍap niṅ asamaya kapaṅgihêŋ taman,
his hīs niŋ bañu muṅgu riŋ tarĕtĕpan kadi luh iṅ anaṅis pinaṅkwakĕn*

muṅgw-iŋ maṇḍyusa kāli kālih ira moǥa kadi kinasut iŋ pasaṅgaman,
keṅĕṙ mātra gulū narendramahiṣī kadi cala cala tan panūt kinol,
piṅgiṙ niŋ kanin iŋ jajâsĕmu miraḥ kadi karagĕt i tuŋtuṅ iŋ kuku,
rāhĕn siñjaṅ ira n lume miṅay awaṙṇna wahu kawawa de nareśwara*

śrī dewîndumatī lĕwĕs lara nira n panaṅis asidĕhâṅure gĕluŋ,
mambĕt mađya nirâṅgaluṅgaṅ araras tĕṅah ira sumawe ri saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tan kewran lukar iŋ tapiḥ wijil i luḥ nira tan inusapan hanê muꝁa,
sambat sambat irâṅrĕmĕk hati rasanya karaṇa ni taṅis niṅ aṅrĕṅö*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

Ahā bibi haji ndi siḥta winaliṅku ta kita tulusâsihê ṅhulun,
muwaḥ bapa haji ndi siḥta palakunkwa tulusa ni wĕlasta ri ṅhulun,
Ujaṙtta kita ṅūni kāsihana niŋ jagat anaku sadā pakāśrayan,
jagat karika māsihêry-aku kita pwa paḍa tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn*

praƀuṅku kita kālih ĕndi parananta pawuṅu sakarĕŋ waraḥ ṅhulun,
yan iŋ śiwapadâŧawêŋ haripadâŧawa lĕpasa kunaŋ sakêrikā,
ṅhulun tumuturâpa don iṅ ahurip wiꝑala yan apasaḥ lawan kita,
patiṅku hawanaṅkwa muṅsir i padanta bapa tañakĕnêŋ kadewatan*

pulaḥta humĕnĕŋ diṅaryan asagaṙ ndi kari culu culuḥta ri ṅhulun,
nihan ṅhulun anakta paṅkwakĕn aḍâtiśaya bapa kita n huwus pĕjaḥ,
prayojana ni deṅkw-asambat akusā baribinana kita n paḍâturū,
palaṙ palar awuṅwa de ni panaṅisku nĕhĕr ajara māsku cĕp tuhan*

nihan tĕtĕlakĕn hatiṅku bibi muṅgah akĕsĕl ahĕnĕk tĕkê jaja,
muwaḥ prih i mataṅku tīsana rahup rahupana bibi bawwa bawwana,
pilī piliṅan i ṅhulun dumadak aṅhĕlu pupukana tulya tulyana,
guluṅku kadi meḥ kahötana rasanya n anaṅis i patinta sĕmburĕn*

ri kāla ni huripta ṅūni bibi sāhasa kita sahasâṅabĕt ṅhulun,
hasiḥ bapa hajî ṅhulun tĕka sirânuluṅ aṅusapi luḥ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mataŋ ya bibi maḥ palu ṅhulun alaḥ pawuṅu sakaharĕp ṅhulun habĕt,
ndya sī yan anuluŋ muwaḥ bapa hajî ṅhulun atĕhĕr ataṅguhê kita*

syapêka śaraṇāśrayaṅkwa ri pĕjaḥta bapa haji nihan dudut ṅhulun,
Apan kaka turuŋ wĕnaŋ śaraṇa ni ṅhulun apituwin anwam iŋ wayaḥ,
kadaŋ kadaṅ adoḥ sirâsih alĕbâmihutaṅanana sī kadi ṅhulun,
mataŋ yan anakanta riŋ suruwayan ṅhulun alah alapĕn maran pĕjaḥ*

Aḍā hyaṅ aparan ta koŋ wiđi ṅaranmu tan awĕlas adĕṅky-anon suꝁa,
bapaṅku sira māti demu mapa doṣa nira huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
lawan bibi tumūt prasidđa tika ko muwah amĕjahi tan pakāraṇa,
mataŋ ya wĕtu ko rwa sānak aku patyani saha bala demu hĕntyakĕn*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nāhan sambat irânaṅis kaḍĕḍĕtan lara hati nira tan wĕnaŋ kinöl,
simsim wāhu hilaŋ maṇiknya kalĕbū paḍa paḍa nira niṣpraƀâkucĕm,
dady-âteja katonan iŋ rahina tan parawi wĕṅi tiniṅgal iŋ wulan,
saṅkê rūpa nirâsawaŋ karĕbahan gunuṅ alara ri līna saŋ praƀu*

paṅde niŋ wiđi tan wĕnaŋ winađa tiṅhalana kasih arĕp suputrikā,
kāry-anwam ri pĕjaḥ nareśwara samaṇḍyusa sira kalawan nareśwarī,
de niŋ duḥka kĕdö sirâmalaku milwa maṅatigana maṇḍyusê dalĕm,
patrĕm wahw-inunus nirênayatakĕn ri jaja kaka kakâkrak aṅrĕbut*

maṅkin ǥūṙṇnita śabda niŋ wwaṅ anaṅis wĕdi kaluputanêŋ nrĕpātmajā,
Āpan budđi nirâṅhuwus huwus apakṣa pĕjaha tumutê nareśwara,
göŋ trĕṣṇâsih arāma rena kapĕgan kapati pati sirâlarânaṅis,
drāk sidđânĕmu duḥka niŋ dadi manuṣya paṅawaśa ni śāpa saŋ rĕṣi*

saŋ ƀoja prihati n tumon kasih arĕp ny-awak ira kari de nareśwara,
kady-agriŋ sira de ni duḥka nira tan sah anaṅis i dagan narāđipa,
Āśāƀūta marambĕhan wĕtu ni luḥ nira mulat i narendrakanyakā,
maṙmmâmaṅku pĕgat pĕgat sapitutuṙ nira tuna tuna de nikaŋ taṅis*

rakryan haywa wiraṅrwaṅ induṅ ĕnĕbĕn ta pamanas i laranta tīsakĕn,
riŋ swaṙggasŧa narendra sāmpun atuhâpituwi huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
pakṣa kṣatriya rāka rakryan apagĕḥ wĕnaṅa śaraṇa rakryan iŋ hayu,
ṅhiŋ yan māti kakanta mamrih iṅ ayun kita pĕjaha tumūta ri ṅhulun*

haywâśâlara duḥka yan bapa haji mwaṅ ibu haji pĕjaḥ sirâduluṙ,
yāwat janma ṅaranya tan hana tuwuḥ watu kaluputa saṅka riŋ pati,
tan pendaḥ kadi cakra niŋ raŧa tĕka ŋ dadi niyata midĕṙ puriḥ nika,
saṅkêŋ mrĕtyu tĕka ṅhurip kunĕṅ ikaŋ pati niyata mijil sakêŋ hurip*

māyākāra hanêŋ crĕmin paḍa nikaŋ dadi sahana hananya tan sŧiti,
himpĕṙ pādapa tan wuruŋ manirarâmĕkasi tuha tuwuḥnya tan lanā,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ hurip iŋ manuṣya juti tattwa nika tan alawas wawaŋ hilaŋ,
kintw-îkaŋ pati jāti tattwa nika tan kṣaṇika pinakađaṙmma niŋ dadi*

Eman ṅwaŋ lumĕkas mamet pati sakêŋ lumĕkasa ri kapetan iŋ hurip,
pöŋpöṅĕn ta huripta yogya dadahanta makahuluna de munīśwara,
Āpan yan wruh i ƀeda saŋ rwa kalawan wruha ri pasamudāya niŋ tiga,
Icꞓā nora kasaṅśayêŋ hala lawan hayu niyata luput sakêrika*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 20

kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hayu nikaŋ hayu yan gawayĕn,
ri wruh i saŋ rwa ƀineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn,
kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hala nikaŋ hala yan gawayĕn,
ri wruh i saŋ rwa ƀineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn*

siṅgih ujaṙtta ri saŋ krĕtasamaya wiśeṣa paṅawruh ira,
kweḥ nira riŋ nagarêṅ acala paḍa tikā pinakoṅgwan ira,
ndin rakĕta ŋ suꝁaduḥka ri sira satatâbrata tan palabuḥ,
lokaparāśraya kāraṇa nira magawe hayu tan wipaŧa*

saŋ wruh i saŋ wĕkas iŋ samaya winuni de paramādiguru,
kewala śudđa manaḥ nira linĕtu lĕtuḥ kapanâlĕtuha,
wāhyaśarīra pinucꞓa nira ri tĕka niŋ pati tan ginĕgö,
jñāna wiśeṣa śarīra nira taya śarīra nirêŋ wĕkasan*

wwaŋ magawe hayu yan wruh i sira saṅ amukti gawenya hayu,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hayu hayu ni gawe nika tan wiꝑala,
wwaŋ magawe hala yan wruh i sira saṅ amukti gawenya hala,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hala hala ni gawe nika tan wiꝑala*

wwaŋ magawe hayu tan wruh i sira saṅ amukti gawenya hayu,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhayu hayu ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ,
wwaŋ magawe hala tan wruh i sira saṅ amukti gawenya hala,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhala hala ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ*

saŋ wiku gūḋa nihan wulatana mamaṅan tĕḍa riŋ pahĕhan,
tan tĕḍa tan śuci ta pwa sahana hana niŋ pinaṅan liṅ ira,
hetu nirâmbĕk alokika winulatan ajrĕm apiṇḍa kasop,
śudđa nikaŋ pratipatti makalarapan uttama niŋ samaya*

māsku mataŋnyan ikaŋ hayu gawayakĕnanta sĕḍĕŋ mahurip,
paṇḍita towi yayā sira maṅulahakĕn brata tan kaluṣa,
budđy-ahĕniŋ brata yoga tapa taki takinta maran kawaśa,
gĕgwana rakryan anĕmwakĕna wara waraḥ paramādiguru*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

Anĕmu nĕmu kĕtêkā saŋ sāmpun krĕtasamaya,
wihikan i rasa saŋ hyaŋ tattwajñāna kalĕpasĕn,
tan ulih ulih iṅ aṅdoḥ saṅkêŋ pāda muniwara,
Ulih iṅ asaṅu tasyan ƀaktîŋ paṇḍita matuha*

Aṅinak inaka taŋ wwaŋ yāwat jñāna pinakadon,
syapa ta sira mamaṅgiḥ tattwajñāna dudu gawe,
hana satata masewā tan byaktanya pinihanan,
sukrĕta juga maṅinte lāwan duṣkrĕta maṅiriŋ*

hana sira guruputrânak niŋ paṇḍita nagara,
sahana nira ta rakwâdrĕwya ŋ jñāna pakagurun,
taha tan ika panidđan wet niŋ paṇḍita matuha,
Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ tattwêṅ uṅgwana rahayu*

Anak iṅ apirak akweḥ ṅūnî nwamnya paḍa suꝁa,
sahana nika ta rakwânirw-akweh apirak ika,
taha tan ika panidđan wet niŋ śreṣṫa panariman,
Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ śrī tan siŋ kahanan ira*

kita yayi sĕḍĕṅ anwam priḥ saŋ hyaŋ rasa kawikun,
pira karika musuḥ niŋ wikw-aṅhiŋ nĕm ikaṅ akas,
Alahakĕn i dalĕm twas pet siŋ soṅgwan ika raraḥ,
Alaha pĕjaha rakryan yêki swaṙgga ṅaran ika*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

nā de nirâwara waraḥ ri narendraputrī,
tapwan tĕtĕs tinuna sanđi nikaŋ prayoga,
Anwam suśīla guṇamanta krĕtopadeśa,
saṅkê paṅajyan ira kawruh irâđiguhya*

śrī putrikā kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕŋ tumuṅkul,
sāmpun ƀinasmi śawa saŋ praƀu de munīndra,
muṅgw-î taman sira cinaṇḍi lawan sudewī,
sampūṙṇna bapra nira ratna mahāpraƀāwa*

saŋ ƀoja sāmpun aṅadĕg ri widaṙbƀarājya,
swasŧā saƀūmi nira ƀakty-anukūla sāđu,
mawwat paḍâmarahakĕn ri suꝁanya rakwa,
Anwam muwaḥ nrĕpati liŋnya muwaḥ manĕmbaḥ*

sāmpun sirâyugala ratna wiśeṣaputrī,
rājāṅkurâwilĕt ikaŋ pakurĕn sawanđu,
soluṙ lulut sahati lĕŋlĕŋ aluŋluṅan kuŋ,
saśrī sakĕmbaṅ alaṅö sakurā sawīja*

kaywan ragas paḍa nikaŋ nagarî widaṙbƀa,
riŋ wrĕdđarūpa haji dewata lahru sākṣāt,
maṅke n prasidđa kadi kaywan aron akĕmbaŋ,
śrī ƀoja maṅdani sirânwam apiṇḍa rĕŋrĕŋ*

wet niŋ krĕtā ri paṅadĕg haji nora duṣṭa,
rāmya ṅhĕnū tĕgal ayun tĕka riŋ wanādri,
wāni ŋ wwaṅ aṅhaliwatîriya tuṅga tuṅgal,
Aṅhiŋ gaḍuŋ luṅ ika maṅhabĕt asriṅ oliḥ*

mantrī nirâtuha tuha dwija śꜽwa bodđa,
kāsiḥ kapaṙccaya narendra wĕnaŋ marê jro,
prajñêṅgitajña ginulaŋ halu riŋ wiweka,
sojaṙ niṅ āgama tinūt nira tan wimāṙgga*

söḥ śāla đaṙmma kuṭi kīṙtti narendra riŋ rāt,
wwaŋ śreṣṫi đaṙmma ginawe nira sāri sāri,
wwaŋ duṣṭa moǥa kapitūt milu đaṙmmabudđi,
solaḥ swaƀāwa haji tan dadi tan tinūtnya*

śrī ƀoja sāmpun apagĕḥ siniwîŋ kaḍatwan,
Okĕṙ tumiṅhal i saṅ indumatī hanê jro,
Āpan samāsa niṅ akaṙmma wayaḥ nirâgöŋ,
Aṅhiŋ swayĕmbarakĕnêṅĕt iṅĕt narendra*

nā de nirâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt kalawan sudewī,
sāmpun wināhyakĕn irê kulawanđu ri jro,
riŋ saṙwwasidđi tuwin amrĕtayoga tĕmbe,
höman hajînarahakĕn para taṇḍa mantrī*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

Eñjiŋ śrîndumatī kinon marĕka kāliḥ saŋ sunandâṅiriŋ,
lāgy-âmūṙṇnama mopawāsa ya ta maṅde suṅkawā niŋ hati,
tistis meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu lumampaḥ tan kwa de niŋ harip,
mukṣa lwīr amarāśrayê muꝁa nira śrī niŋ wulan tan lumöŋ*

sāmpun prāpta sirê dalĕm praṇata maṙmmâtwaŋ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu,
lāwan śrī parameśwarī sira sinambaḥ māsih aṅliŋ rĕsĕp,
Om rakryan pada nīlakaṇṫa kinaƀaktyantâstu dīṙgǥāyuṣa,
swasŧā tuṅgalĕn iŋ manuṅgali jagat māskw-îbu nā liŋ nira*

mojaṙ saŋ praƀu māsku tan tugĕta niŋ twastân inundaŋ mami,
rākanta prihati n harĕp mamituhê māsku ndan ewĕḥ juga,
saŋ ratw-âsiha len sasamƀawa muwaḥ yekī pinet ni ṅhulun,
kady-amrat mrati mās juga ṅwaṅ amagantākĕn puriḥ niŋ dadi*

yāwat đaṙmma ṅaranya riŋ dadi manuṣyâwās hiwĕḥ yan pinet,
lwiṙ sūkṣmā maganal ƀaṭāra gumawe tiṅkaḥnya yan maṅkana,
yadyastun jalu jalw-ameta sawawanyêŋ janma haywâsali,
byaktêwĕḥ niki kimpunaḥ kita yan iŋ strī strī n mameta priya*

saŋkṣepanya kita swayĕmbarakĕnaṅkwânugrahaṅkwê kita,
sakweḥ saŋ ratu hundaṅĕn pilihanantâsiŋ sayogyê hati,
yadyan hyaŋ palakunta māsku yugalantâmriḥ mrihaṅkwâṅhyaṅa,
Aṅhiŋ yan hyaṅ anaṅga kahyuna hade tan pāwak ewĕḥ pinet*

nâjñā saŋ praƀu yogya paṅkwakĕna de saŋ mās maṇik niŋ purī,
Āpan māsa nira n prapañca saputĕn riŋ rāga de hyaŋ smara,
tan wruḥ riŋ sahurâwiraŋ mata sira n paṅyogyanê saŋ praƀu,
tan maṅguḥ sira tan miṅĕl kadi liṅiṙ mās aṙcca paṅhyaŋ hyaṅan*

tan saṅkêṅ awalepa kāraṇa nira n lwiṙ tuhwa monabrata,
kepwan budđi nirâtĕgĕg maṅucap agyā gyān harĕp mantuka,
wahw-âdandan anĕmbahê nrĕpati mojaṙ saŋ sunandâṅjawil,
Om yan Om huwusĕn huwus liṅa ni māskw-âlaḥ tuhan mājara*

tan kewö pitutuṙnya de nrĕpasutā mantuk sirêŋ pamrĕman,
strī strī mājar ajaṙ gumanti humatuṙ prāptêñjiṅ akweḥ marĕk,
moliḥ tīṙŧa binuṅbuṅan winalun iŋ handoŋ sakêŋ paṙwwata,
maṅde śudđa ri budđi saŋ praƀu suꝁā sāmpun sirâcāmana*

<puṣpacāpa> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓ = 20

prāsāda sꝑaṭikâlaṅö ri tĕṅah iŋ nūsâraras pañcuranya,
strī stry-âmaṅku puḍak winimba makaranya lwiṙ lĕṅĕŋ de ni kuŋnya,
kady-ahyun n-amahaywa luṅsur i tapiḥnya n maṅligā yan hana wwaŋ,
lāgy-ânaṅga suśūnya saṅka ri pacuṙ niŋ wwꜽ ya tâṅde ṅĕliḥnya*

ri prāsāda hanâṙcca ratna ri dalĕm ndān aṙdđanārīśwarâhyaŋ,
wimba śrī naranāŧa dewata lawan dewī nirârok śarīra,
ṅkā saŋ ƀoja maṅaṙccana pratidinâṅaƀyāsa ri swasŧa niŋ rāt,
kady-âmakpak aṅastwakĕn ri jayaśatrwa śrī narendra n pamūjā*

saŋ ƀoja wruh i tattwa niŋ japasamāđi n đāraṇa đyānapūṙwwa,
mwaŋ tiṅkaḥ niṅ adehaśudđi pinakānuṣṫāna yan recakādi,
sāmpun kālap ulaḥ dwijeśwara mamūjā paŧya riŋ brahmamantra,
saŋ hyaŋ kūṭarahasyamantra jinapākĕn de nirâtūt gaṇitri*

tatkāla nrĕpati n paṅuccaraṇakĕn mantra stutî saŋ hyaṅ aṙcca,
tan polaḥ wiṣayâṅhiḍĕp ri sira saṅyogānta riŋ yogya yogan,
maṅgā tan lĕpara ŋ japastawa sĕḍĕŋ niŋ jñāna n enak tĕtĕpnya,
simpaŋ niŋ hati yeki kāraṇa nirânaṅhāra saŋ hyaŋ śiwātma*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

ri huwus ira mamūjā līlā śudđa manah ira,
Aṅusapi muꝁa saśrī de niŋ candana karakĕt,
mijil aṅinaṅ aṅicꞓā riŋ wwꜽ niŋ ranu maṅilo,
nĕhĕr anisigi dantê tuŋtuŋ niŋ gagaṅ inapi*

tucapa ta para mantrī śꜽwa brāhmaṇa sugata,
parĕṅ apupul asewa ṅkānê jro paḍa humatuṙ,
nrĕpati sira maluṅguḥ riŋ siṅhāsana kanaka,
Aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i sidđā niŋ kāṙyya n gawayakĕna*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

ndin kāṙyyêwĕha riŋ wicakṣaṇa sujanma lituhayu kawi priyambada,
ƀaktîŋ hyaŋ praƀu śakti đꜽṙyya saha wānđawa saha bala kośawāhana,
yadyan sāgara tambakĕn satakĕnâŧawa wukir alihĕn ratākĕna,
byaktâwās kawaśanya de nira saṅ uttamapuruṣa wiśeṣa riŋ jagat*

śrī ƀoja pwa sira n prasidđa guṇamanta saꝑala sira ƀūmipālaka,
prajñā śāstrawit iṅgita wruh iṅ apālapan aṅinaki budđi niŋ marĕk,
Akweḥ drĕwya nirâprameya kadi sāgara papupulan iŋ wway iŋ nadī,
wany-ânindita riŋ parākrama yan iŋ naya kadi ƀagawān wrĕhaspati*

maṅke pwa n hana rājakāṙyya gawayĕn kakaratala tĕkap nareśwara,
śrī dewîndumatī swayĕmbarakĕnâmiliha ratu sasamƀawê sira,
sāmpun saŋ praƀu motusan maminaṅê para ratu samayogya hundaṅĕn,
lāwan saŋ haja milwa winwitakĕn iŋ nrĕpati raǥu katon tĕkā nira*

sāmpun höman irêrikā ta para taṇḍa sama sama samâṅharĕp gawe,
sorêsuk gumĕrĕḥ makakrĕtug abaṇḍuṅ asahuran aganti loṙ kidul,
len taŋ wwaŋ maṅusuŋ lakaṙ lakar ikā winaca wuhaya de nikaŋ mulat,
Akweḥ wwaŋ ka gĕrāh arĕp mulata wāhu mĕtu sinurakan muliḥ pacĕḥ*

Abwat hajyan ikaŋ humuŋ saha garantuṅ atabĕ tabĕhan paḍâsĕluṙ,
Agyā lagy-aṅuhuḥ sirê harĕp alaḥ laku laku liṅ ikaŋ hanê wuri,
tuṅgul paṅharĕp osik akrĕp asinaŋ kumuliliṅ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
lwiṙ guntuṙ kamarĕkrĕkĕn kayu pĕtuŋ priṅ asalĕsĕk agĕṇṭah iŋ lĕbuḥ*

Ewĕṙ nora lĕgâṅ apaṇḍay anulis para lukis asipĕt mwaṅ aṅjahit,
sakweḥ niŋ ginĕlaṙ wruhâṅanam anam wruh i suruhan ikā siliḥ tuluŋ,
solaḥ niŋ tama tan hanâtaña ṅaranya huwus adu kabeḥ dinadyakĕn,
paprāsan winaṅun paḍâcarita paṙwwa piniturun atuṅgalan kaŧā*

<widyutkara> 
– – – |⏑⏑– |⏑– ⏑|⏑⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏓ = 25

Embuḥ ƀūṣaṇa niŋ tĕkĕn wuwuṅ apūṙwwa karacanan ikā tĕkêŋ pamanisan,
lāwan tiṅkah ikaŋ paṅastryanan apaṙppat ahalĕp akilā paḍâhayu hayu,
de niŋ mās pinakopacāra sinisik pĕñu pinakawuwuŋnya kumram asinaŋ,
lwiṙ digdāha riṅ astapaṙwwata sĕnö nika murub apadĕlwan iŋ kṣititala*

Aśrī rāmya ni de nirâmahayu rājya kaliliran apūṙwwa kādƀuta dahat,
miṅgaṙ bapra nikê dalĕm watu hitĕm kuṭa nikaṅ i yawā lumaṅkuṅ ahirĕŋ,
kulwan wetan agopurâtiśaya loṙ kidul agupura piṇḍa maṙppat aruhuṙ,
krĕṣṇākāra paḍâṅlunaŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukus i sĕḍĕṅ iŋ darâwrĕg aputiḥ*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

luṅhā ŋ wrĕtta ri kāṙyya saŋ praƀu paḍâdƀuta sahana nikaŋ wwaṅ aṅrĕṅö,
wwaŋ wwaŋ pora ḍusun ḍusun paḍa harĕp wihikana mulatêŋ swayambara,
tan samwas raray aṅhwan iŋ tĕgal atakwan i tĕka ni gawe nareśwara,
salwiṙ niŋ baṇijêŋ pĕkĕn taliṅa lintah anaḍah ucapan gawe nika*

sāmpun prāpta samotusan humatur iŋ nrĕpati sĕḍĕṅ irân hanêŋ saƀā,
Enak budđi narendra de ni panuwal para ratu rasa tan wuruŋ tĕkā,
lumrā ŋ wrĕtta tĕkê dalĕm ri ḍatĕṅâṙyya raǥusuta marêŋ swayambara,
twas niŋ strī sakaḍatwan aṅdadak aluŋ turida paḍa rumūpakê sira*

strī strī haṙṣa pinöm pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara ri pamihaŋnya riŋ yayaḥ,
tan haṙṣêŋ kawi rakwa rena nika monaguṇa pisaniṅūn tumiṅhala,
ndan rakwêki hinuṙnya matya saka riŋ tuluyakĕna susatya riŋ priya,
liŋnya n kewala tan hinanti ni papaṅgiha nika pĕjahêŋ panambaṅan*

tapwan māri taṅis taṅisnya n inalap hinaturakĕn i jöŋ suputrikā,
wrā niŋ roma maṅekadeśa ri piliŋ piliṅan ika baṅun pamer i luḥ,
Enak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥnya mamalaṙ malar i pada narendraputrikā,
Āpan swāmi nikā karĕṅwan i parĕknya ri saṅ aja tĕwĕk nikâpasaḥ*

Antuk saŋ priya maṅdawākĕn inalĕm para kawi sumĕnāha riŋ kajaŋ,
yeki n rakwa kinonya kady-aṅucapâmah aku tuhan alap waca ṅhulun,
moǥa nyan ya kinonakĕn wacan ikā ri pamaca nika maṅdadak lumuḥ,
swāminyâdadi pustakânuturakĕn hiḍĕp ika pinapagnya riŋ taṅis*

ṅūnî kāla nika n turuŋ marĕk i jöŋ nira ṅaran ika ken mađūdakā,
saŋ mambaŋ mađusūdana priya nikā kawi taruṇa marĕk ri jöŋ haji,
wiđy-âmiđyani kāraṇanya wirahênalapan alara luḥnya tan pĕgat,
ndaḥ rakryan jayawaspa teki wĕkasan ṅaran ika satĕwĕk nikā marĕk*

<Aƀikrĕti> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 25

para praƀu kaḍaṅhanan turida rāga nira sinaput iŋ smarâmulaṅuni,
huwus katĕka kuŋ nirâhawan ujaṙ tuhun amĕlas arĕp riniptakĕn ira,
lawan punagi kesy-anambaha ri jöŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā hana hyuna nira,
Akiṅkiṅ aṅalap kasoṙ paḍa tan apraƀu sahana nirârĕbut kahulunan*

wawaŋ nrĕpatiputrikā rinĕbut iŋ hiḍĕp inaṅĕn aṅĕn raras raras ira,
hanan kahiḍĕp iŋ mađubrata rĕṅiḥ rĕṅiha nira n arĕs kapaṅkwa harasĕn,
lĕyĕp hayu nira n linaṅwakĕn amūṙtti kakawin inapus wineh amanisa,
hanê hati kinubđa kady-apĕga kāraṇa nira mijil iŋ puḍak dadi ṭikā*

Adandan asĕnāha sañjata para praƀu ḍatĕṅa marê widaṙbƀanagara,
lanâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ri pahyasan irâṅinakana ri manaḥ narendratanayā,
hanâṅdadak anat śarīra manahap nahap aharĕp alantasa n winulatan,
paḍâṅalap alap sipat jĕnu mĕnuŋ hawu karaṇa suputrikā n aharĕpa*

muwaḥ saṅ aja sāmpun aṙppat akire lumarisa makamaṅgala dwijawara,
sahasraśatakoṭi wīra winiđi nrĕpati tumuta śakti sāmpun ayaśa,
pĕnuḥ sahana niŋ lĕbuḥ tĕkap i sañjata nika kumaluŋ pinañjĕr aṅadĕg,
Ikaŋ nagara denya kady-akalaṅan wihaga saṅ aja moliha praƀusutā*

mijil sira śinaṅꝁapāṇyan i karaŋ ni patiga niṅ aśoka wahw-asalaga,
Ikaŋ ƀramara haṙṣa riŋ kusuma muṅgw-i taṅan ira marâṅisĕp tan awĕliŋ,
laki stry-aliwĕran hañaṙ hañar apaṅgih adulur akaraŋ karaŋ sĕkar arūm,
katampwan i kucuṙ nikaŋ wway atawiŋ tawiṅ i lawĕ lawö nikaŋ sarasija*

I sāmpun i kaśaṅꝁapāṇyan ira mañjiṅ i dalĕm aduluṙ lawan dwijawara,
Anambah aṅusap ri jöŋ nrĕpati mamwit i ḍatĕṅa nirêŋ widaṙbƀanagara,
sinuṅsuṅ iṅ ujaṙ prahāsana nĕhĕṙ jumaya jaya jayā nirê paran ira,
Ahum hanaku saŋ pakolihĕn i tiṅhal iṅ ahayu dumĕlwa jalwa rasika*

kunaŋ pawĕkasaṅkwa haywa ta bapaṅku tan apĕnĕd iṅ ambĕk iŋ para paran,
rare mara kita ndatan raraya de niṅ amawa manah atwaṅêŋ wwaṅ atuha,
Inuttama đanuṙdđarânaku taŧāpi tan ika paṅayāya riŋ kadi kita,
Ikaŋ guṇa ya tan paraṅkĕpana maryada rahayu lawö hananya kapalaŋ*

Ikaŋ sakahawan ri ƀūmi ni bapaṅku pahayu kita rakṣakâṅanumata,
sapawwat ika hantusākĕna sasamƀawa haturakĕnanya māsku tariman,
Ujaṙku pitūhuntā haywa kitā sahasa maṅalapā wastū mūlya tinĕṅĕt,
prasidđa kadaṅ iŋ jagat kita dumadyakĕna suꝁa nikā mataŋnya pahayu*

pamitran alawas rĕsĕp karaṇa niŋ wĕnaṅ aṅalapa wastu tan pamalaku,
yan iŋ wiṣayarāmajātaka puriḥnya karaṇa niṅ anĕmwa mās pirak ika,
karāsikaguṇan ya kāraṇa niṅ oliha raras i manaḥ niṅ adyah araras,
kaśaktin aƀimāna kāraṇa niṅ aṅrarah aṅalapa rājya niŋ ripukula*

sirat sirat i de narendra raǥu mojar amanis amađaṙmmakĕn ri saṅ aja,
minuṣṭi pinakādidewa hiniḍĕp rasa nika kinayogyakĕn pinituhu,
putus niṅ ađamā tan ahyuna rumĕṅwakĕna ri pitutuṙ nirâhayu dahat,
ya kāraṇa narendraputra makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ narapati*

ri sāmpun ira mamwit iŋ nrĕpati saṙwwi laku nira marê narendramahiṣī,
hanâṅhaḍaṅ aweḥ sĕrĕḥ saha taṅis wagĕd ahayu hinĕmban iŋ kaka kaka,
kataṅgamaṅ aweḥ sĕpaḥ nrĕpatiputra nĕhĕr amuhun amrih aṅhari hari,
tapiḥ saṅ araras pininta nira mūlya basahan ira raṇḍi paṅhurup ira*

byatīta ri huwus nirâṅucap ucap tĕka sira ri taman narendramahiṣī,
lĕṅĕŋ kadi kadewatan halĕp ikâpan ajuraṅ awukiṙ mapājar ajaran,
maEṙttali pinañcuran jinalatuṇḍa tinalaga ri soṙnya kādƀuta dahat,
Ikaŋ kaka kakânwam adyus anĕṅaḥ lawan anak anakanya ketaka miṅiŋ*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

kalpadruma taruwara pārijāta winaṅun bwat asana sakapat,
Aƀrâsinaṅ asĕmu sakêŋ kadewatan ululnya kanaka pinahat,
jinriṅjriṅ iṅ anak anakan maṇik cinaturaṅga lumarap amiraḥ,
mās jaṅga katirah awilĕt pralĕmba nika riŋ tarĕtĕpan alaṅö*

ṅkānā nrĕpatisuta marĕk ri rena nira sādara satiru tirun,
Amwit lumarisa ḍatĕṅêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī bibi nira wihikan,
maṙmmâsih awĕlas asĕgĕḥ mamakpak amapag riṅ ucapan amanis,
niṙwiǥna kita bapa jāyêŋ swāyambara sādaṅalahakĕna ratu*

rakryān aṅinaṅa tanayaṅku māsku mapa hetu niṅ awak akuru,
Agriŋ karika kita lawan waneḥ brata kunaŋ karaṇa niṅ awĕnĕs,
haywânaku kaluṣa kitâhyun iŋ kajayaśatrwan anuta ri harĕp,
Akweḥ ꝑala nika kaki saṙwwawiǥna niyatanya hilaṅ alaradan*

ndan rakwa kadamĕlan ikaŋ swayambara kahop riṅ anakĕbi rara,
sakweḥ para ratu pininaŋ ya teka pilihĕn sakaharĕp alapĕn,
de ni ṅhulun ahiḍĕp i budđi saŋ rara kapan harĕpa riṅ atuha,
ṅhiŋ kahyuna nika ratu cakrawaṙttitanayâguṇa kawi taruṇa*

rakryan pwa saꝑala wĕka cakrawaṙtti tuwi śakti wihikan aṅaji,
siṅhākrĕti tuhu tuhu siṅhaputra wĕnaṅ uṅsirĕn iṅ aśaraṇa,
byaktânaku mamĕnaṅa riŋ swayambarasaƀâṅalahakĕna ratu,
tan sĕṅgahĕn aṅalĕm anak syapêka kadi māsku lituhayu wani*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

tatkālê paṅucap narendramahiṣī tucapa ta para ratnakanyakā,
Osik tan pakawanwan agyaṅ i ḍatĕŋ saṅ aja kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,
tan pātmā kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn kalukaran gĕluṅ asidĕha tan hanâṅucap,
kady-âhöm turidanya n osah akĕcap lwir anicipi manis nrĕpātmaja*

wwantĕn lwiṙ śaśiwimba wāhu mijil aṅḍaḍari hayu nikânwam iŋ wayaḥ,
Aṅgöŋ mabrata śuklapakṣa nika paṅlwaṅ i manah ika tan wĕnaŋ licin,
rāganya n dadakan tumaṅgal i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasuta kadi tambwaṅ iŋ wulan,
krĕṣṇākāra tĕṅaḥnya de ni tapak iŋ suh asĕmu sĕmu rāhw-añumbana*

len taŋ lwiṙ pranitâdagaŋ kira kiranya sumikĕpa wĕkas nrĕpātmaja,
kapraŋ rwêpu kataṇḍĕgan turida tan patahĕnan aṅagĕm pralāpita,
toḥ toḥ nyân iṅ agĕgwan ambĕk apagĕḥ mapa tiki n alah aṅgĕgö smara,
Aṅlampwâṅusirê padadwaya nirân panikĕlakĕna tuṙ humaṇḍĕma*

strī saṅsāra sarāga mohita sawaŋ wana gahana kalahrwan iŋ kapat,
trāsa twasnya kakiṅkiṅan ginĕsĕṅan pinarawaśa tinunwan iŋ smara,
norânīsi manaḥnya kewala panasbaran alisuh aṅölakĕn lara,
maṅke pwa n karĕṅö gĕrĕḥ saṅ aja mañjiṅ aluṅ asĕmi kuŋ nikâsĕwö*

Endaḥ budđi nikaŋ waneḥ tĕkap ikâmawa turida luput linakṣaṇan,
muṅkuṙ tan huniṅê ḍatĕŋ saṅ aja mañjiṅ asila ri harĕp nareśwarī,
ndan denyâhyas apahyasan dudu dudū hiniraṅakĕn ikê nrĕpātmaja,
sūkṣmākāra ni raśmi raśmi ni wulatnya n araras apadĕlwan iŋ crĕmin*

kanyā rwaŋ siki rāmya kālih aṅisapwakĕn anak anakanya ketaka,
tuṅgal mājar i putra putran ika māsku saṅ aja sira rakwa maṅkata,

maṙmmanyâpasah ambĕk eṅgal apadudwan aṅuwahi pamitran aṅdadak*

strī strī sukṣĕka wahw-agātra turidanya mijil i wijil iŋ payođara,
tan saḥ riŋ salukat gawe nrĕpatiputra sinalukatakĕnya tan humuŋ,
ramyârūm karĕṅö manisnya sinameni pamawan ika riṅraṅ iŋ hati,
tan samwas ginarut garutnya hiniḍĕpnya saṅ aja sahasâṅisapwakĕn*

sakweḥ niŋ kumĕmit prapañca ni hatinya kumĕkĕsi taṅisnya riŋ karas,
Āpan budđi narendraputra kadi tan tulusa duga dugâṅhalimbaṅa,
ƀakty-ânĕmbah i jöŋ ni rena nira mĕṅgĕp amanis agawe wulat maliŋ,
luṅhā tan pracurânĕhĕṙ nĕhĕrakĕn manah iṅ ahayu kāri sukṣĕka*

<Aƀikrĕti> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 25

mijil saṅ aja kādƀutâƀinawa rūpa saṅ aṅiriṅ apan paḍâhyaṅ ahalĕp,
Ikaŋ gaja raŧâśwa sañjata saƀūṣaṇa nika dumilaḥ kasĕnwan aruṇa,

baṅun jalada tan pakāla gumĕrĕḥ ri taya niṅ aṅin aṅḍapuṙ saha kilat*

payuŋ payuṅan iŋ lĕbuḥ kadi sĕkaṙ sinawuṅ apan anekawaṙṇna sumĕkaṙ,
Ikaŋ paṅuṅaṅan huwus winalunan wĕḍihan inuparĕṅga riŋ tulis ĕmās,

hanêŋ gupura tan wawaŋ sira lumampah ataña ri gĕnĕp ni sañjata nira,

ri lampah ira ǥūṙṇnita ŋ paḍahi paṅharĕp ira kumisik maṅeṙttali tibā,
saru swara nikâbaruŋ binaruṅan tabĕ tabĕhan agĕnturan kadi gĕrĕḥ,

Arūm uni ni ǥaṇṭa niŋ liman aṅuṅkaṅ asahuran i paṅhrik iŋ kuda bisiṙ*

dwijāti rĕṣi śꜽwa bodđa śuci sojar ira maṅaƀiwāda muṅgu ri harĕp,
yaŧākrama paḍâdarâhalĕp agöṅ i wĕtĕṅ ira lawan huwan riṅ atuha,

humuŋ tĕkap ira n paṅuccaraṇa mantra kadi mađukarâṅisis humaliwat*

kĕliŋ wani wanîṅ usāna pamarakṣa nira mamawa ƀindiwāla palaga,

Agöŋ paḍa kaƀīma ƀīma kadi dānawa muꝁa muꝁa dꜽtya piṇḍa cawiri*

Ikaŋ marĕk i jöŋ narendratanayânwam aguṇa paḍa daṙśśanīya taruṇa,
titik nagara nora tan wruha n anak wĕsi haji tuwi mūlya kawwaṅan ika,
watĕk madana maṅdadi wwaṅ ujar iŋ mulat i lituhayunya n ahyaṅ araras,
kunaŋ saṅ aja kāmadewa sakalânurun ucapan ikaŋ kapūhan i sira*

samaṅkana nikaŋ wwaṅ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan haṅu haṅun arĕbut mulat ri saṅ aja,
hanan kadi harĕp siliḥ galaha riŋ susu manĕwĕka riŋ naꝁâkas aluṅid,
paḍâkira kirâkĕkĕs mata maliŋ maliṅ aṅiriṅi kāladeśa sumilib,
katon kadi siliḥ praṅêŋ halis arĕṅw-inayat ayatakĕnya maṅkin araras*

Ikāṅ amawa pawwahan lituhayu prakaśita kawi mambaṅ uttama rare,
hañaṙ tĕka sakêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī layat inalapan aṅhañaŋ hañaṅakĕn,

ya kāraṇa ni luḥnya mantĕn amalaṙ malar i saṅ aja molihê sira hĕlĕm*

manis ni kakawinya mūla ni papaṅgih ika lawan ikaŋ rinudđa winalat,
pinet pĕjahanâsĕnötan i kadaŋnya winuni karaṇanya yan lĕpas adoḥ,
paḍâpalarasan lawan jaruman amrih aṅalih ahawan wĕṅîṅ awa wulan,
tinūt i paṅaran ṅaranya kawidoṣa wĕkasan i ḍatĕŋnya riŋ nrĕpasuta*

ya tīka tan adoḥ ginĕgwan ira bāhu nika winisikan tinakwanan ira,
syapêka paḍa saŋ swayĕmbarakĕna prakaśita pinakādi niŋ wwaṅ ahayu,
Ikaŋ wwaṅ aṅuṅaŋ bwat indrawanitâhyas ika pahawasĕn ta ya n sama hirib,
kĕcapnya n aṅĕsaḥ miṅĕl ya pawaraḥnya ri saṅ aja wawaŋ rĕmĕk hati nira*

mahâṅjĕlagakĕn hayunya makapaṅhaḍa buṅah i muꝁanya tan patalutuḥ,
ri kāla saṅ ajâṅinaŋ winulatanya ri wulat ira löṙ matanya lumiriŋ,
baṅun hañar anūt harĕp sĕpah awĕdy-aṅucapa tumiliŋ miṅe kadi cala*

rarânwam akire wulat dudu dudū saṅ aṅĕsah i kisapwan iŋ kaka kaka,
tupis tupis i de nirâṅĕnahakĕn manah ira tumibê narendratanaya,
wagĕd wagĕd aniṙwwa niṙwakĕn ī de nira gamĕl ināmĕṙ nīrê taṅan ira,
tĕkāsih atabĕḥ sĕrĕḥ saha pucaŋ nika dalihan irâṅawe ri saṅ aja*

I soṙ niṅ asanâsĕkaṙ hana sirâṅuṅaṅ araras aliṇḍuṅan kaka kaka,
ṅĕliḥ ṅĕlih iṅ ekacitta ri narendrasuta ṅĕlih irâhuyaŋ pinĕpĕtan,

mulat pwa saṅ ajâṅdadak sira miṅe sĕmu niṅ awarahê katĕmwana nira*

muwaḥ wwaya sirâhalĕp rara sujanma pinawulaṅakĕn hanêŋ paṅuṅaṅan,
gaḍiŋ pinakaputra putran ira tan sah inarĕk arĕkan sakê nrĕpasuta,
ya teka tumurun hinĕmban iṅ iñâmawa sĕrĕh arĕnaḥ marĕk ri saṅ aja,
bapâṅinaṅa rakwa liŋ ra bibi liŋ nikaṅ aṅujarakĕn waśâsĕmu guyu*

pratāpa naranāŧaputra kumutug pracalita kadi paṙwwatâgni dumilaḥ,
Ikaŋ wwaṅ aṅuṅaŋ baṅun kusuma sālas anĕḍĕṅ ika kāri tan papĕgatan,
manaḥnya ginĕsĕŋ tĕkêŋ turida rāga nika paḍa hilaŋ syuh aṅdadi hawu,
ya teka hinañutnya riŋ nrĕpatiputra sakala sira pöḥ niṅ aṙṇnawa mađu*

manis niṅ ucapan kaka dyah ari liŋnya sinĕpuhan i raśmi niŋ wulat arūm,
ya teka kinabehan iŋ wwaṅ aṅuṅaŋ mrĕdu lalita rasanya rāgakaraṇa,
raras raras i denya miṅgĕk aṅĕnāni n aṅucap api tan wruhĕn hana mulat,
halisnya minahānya molah amaṅun gĕt unĕṅ arĕṅu maṅlare ri saṅ aja*

<Indrabajra> 
– – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

strī stry-âṅucap sojar ikā yinuktyan,
liŋnyê narendrātmaja mūḋabudđi,
Akweḥ sira ṅke nagarī ry-ayođyā,
sāmantaputrī paḍa yogya-yogyan*

yadyan tĕkā dlāha sirê widaṙbƀa,
tan suŋsuṅĕn riŋ kakawin wilāpa,
tan kewwa riŋ rāga tĕkap suputrī,
ƀagnapratijñā mulihêraṅ eraŋ*

nāhan wuwusnyê naranāŧaputra,
ndan rakwa paṙṇnaḥ jaruman gatinya,
wwantĕn suputrī paṅadunya yogya,
maṙmmanya duḥkê saṅ aja n tan ahyun*

paṙṇnaḥ kakanyâsrak atuṅga yôjaṙ,
Antĕn hade denta tĕkôjar apyak,
putrī paran tan harĕpê tuhanku,
hyaŋ niŋ purī towi yayā sirâhyun*

maṅko n marê śrī naranāŧa ƀoja,
Ambĕk nira śrîndumatī pakādin,
ǥārâpan atyanta wiśeṣaputrī,
sāmantaputrī sira tā maṅadyaḥ*

nāhan sahuṙnyê paṅucap ny-arinya,
ƀāwanya miṅgĕk tumikĕl halisnya,
koṅ aṅdĕlö solah ikā n asĕṅhit,
göŋ krođa sojaṙ nika kaṙṇnaśūla*

wwantĕn kili wrĕdđa sahuṙ nirâtwaŋ,
sajñêbu ni ṅwaŋ kṣama ta ṅhulun dyaḥ,
budđinta kewalya sumorakĕn saŋ,
sāmantaputrîndumatī wiśeṣa*

tan soṙ sirêŋ janma karājaputryan,
riŋ wīṙyya siṅgiḥ sira tan paḍâḍaḥ,
ndan yogya ǥārâpa hiwaŋ nirêbu,
mūlya n minūlyan krama niŋ dadi wwaŋ*

nāhan sahuṙ saŋ wiku wrĕdđarūpa,
mĕṅgĕp pratuhw-âsĕmu pakṣapāta,
milw-âhadenî sira yan lumampaḥ,
rowaŋ nirâgoṣṫi wulatnya hewa*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

tucapa ŋ wwaṅ i paṅguṅ ika kadi wayaŋ jinajaṙ kinudaŋ,
sakunaŋ kunaṅ iŋ taliṅa larap i hintĕn ika n kumĕñaṙ,
hana tâṅadĕg an hayu nika kahiḍĕp kadi modahita,
I kasiṅkab i kenya hana kadi gibaḥ winuluŋ sinurat*

paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ sahana niṅ aṅuṅaŋ mawagĕd wagĕdan,
Amanis manisan mata nĕhĕr araṅin raṅinan paṅawak,
Arupit rupitan susu nĕhĕr alĕmĕs lĕmĕsan luṅayan,
sira saŋ sinajinya saṅ aja juga nora muwaḥ kinire*

nrĕpaputra sĕḍĕŋ sapawulatan aweḥ lĕṅĕṅêṅ aṅuṅaŋ,
tadanantara meḥ lĕpasa laku nirā wĕkas iŋ nagara,
Amanis kadi tan pĕgata wulat irê salawaŋ salawaŋ,
Amalaṙ hana niŋ wwaṅ ahaliṅana kori mĕṅā sasisiḥ*

Araras rinasan patĕmu nira wulat rasa tan lĕpara,
kalawan saṅ akūṅ alawas i sira kady-awarĕg warĕgan,
Apatūtan unĕŋ kasih arĕp inatīta tiniṅgalakĕn,
I layat nira kāri saṅ ahayu wulatnya tinambaṅ ira*

nda Atīta sira n kajĕnĕkan akurĕn wulat esy-akadi,
Asalin wiṣaya n lĕpas i muꝁa nikaŋ lĕbuh iŋ nagara,
kuṭi śāla lumaṅkuṅ i tĕpi niṅ ayun tirisanya pĕnuḥ,
panĕḍĕŋ ni wuṅūnya mamituturi rāga nirêṅ aṅuṅaŋ*

kadi waḥ surasinđu bala saṅ aja kātatakut gumuruḥ,
raŧa rĕṅga padāti kadi parahu söh aduluṙ humilī,
gajah aṅgala ǥūṙṇnita piraṅ iwu kady-asibū gumuluŋ,
sagĕḍaŋ kahilī gaḍiṅ ika tulalenya lumintah awās*

paḍa ƀakti hĕnū nira sakalihatan paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ,
walahaṙnya lawan pahatan asaji mīna sayub cumaḍaŋ,
Amapag waṅi niŋ kusuma winawa niŋ pawana mrik arūm,
ƀramarâsĕmu maṅhaturakĕn i gawenya kiduŋ ri sira*

kadi maṇḍala rāmya ni papupul ikaŋ kayu kayw-asĕkaṙ,
waṅunanya wuṅū sĕḍĕṅ asinaṅ añaṇḍi minerw-aruhuṙ,
humilī wulakanya paḍa caluṅanêka katon humaḍaŋ,
hulu kĕmbaṅ ikaŋ gaḍuṅ anĕpĕrakĕn ri narendrasuta*

patapan kĕna rāga kayu manis ikā sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,
Amapag mata jāti ni mata ni wuluḥ nika tan wriṅ iraŋ,
Aḍahĕm haḍawanya rumara rara haṙṣaja denya mulat,
pajajaṙ ni pabañwan ika kapahiriŋ milu kady-aṅaraŋ*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

saṅ aja sira kaṅelan muṅgaḥ riŋ raŧa wĕkasan,
saṅ agajah aturaṅgânuṅgaŋ saƀya ciha ciha,
mwaṅ agiliṅan arampak wwaŋ sāmānya tan ahalĕp,
saṅ aḍarat alarêraŋ kagrĕk grĕk magarawalan*

nrĕpasuta lĕpas eṅgal prāptêŋ ŧāni kuluwutan,
satĕka tĕka ni lampaḥ niŋ wadwânamun aduluṙ,
I harĕp i wuri lumrânĕṅkw-âyun manasa nasaṙ,
hawan arupĕk inambaḥ membuḥ lwā kadi tinĕpa*

wukir ajajar ahaṇḍap haṇḍap śūnya maṅililan,
kadi kukusan amuñjuŋ puñcaknyâṙṇnĕb inululan,
hana talaga riṅ agra ndan wwꜽnyâhaṅĕt ahasin,
pinara paran iṅ adyus baṙyyan landĕp awukiran*

suku suku nika duṙggâtyantêwĕḥ nika pinaran,
pinĕga tinĕpa de niŋ molaḥ ṅūni riṅ alawas,
sahaja maliwat i jro ṅkân līlâmĕkasi parab,
dadali nika laki strī prāptânambĕr asahuran*

lura lurah aparĕk lwaḥ guŋguŋ wwꜽnya ḍinawuhan,
papupulan ikaṅ aṅhwan ramyâḍöm aṅariṅ ariŋ,
paḍa marĕk adum uṅgwan yan wwaŋ śreṣṫi humaliwat,
Asila sila ri piṅgiṙ niŋ māṙggâmalaku sĕrĕḥ*

Umah atiśaya denyâporaŋ mĕṅgĕp aṅililan,
wwaṅ ika paḍa humöt riŋ budđy-âlumbuṅ alit alit,
tĕka ri sapi nikâlit norâkral kral amĕḍusi,
talaga nika jugâlwâṅlaṅhuy laṅhuyakĕn agöŋ*

hana ta baṅun amet wwaŋ doṣa n krūra lĕkas ikā,
Amawa tali lawan kris pamraŋ mraŋnya habalaṅan,
sapi nika sinikĕpnyâṅrĕñcal maṅlawan agalak,
ri huwus ika katalyan keṇḍit dinwal iṅ aṅulaŋ*

nrĕpatisuta kaluṅhâdoḥ śīǥra n saha śakaṭa,
karaṇa nira n araryan mwaŋ sakweḥ ni bala nira,
Amarĕki pĕkĕn alwā ŧāny-âgöŋ pakulĕmana,
pira ta puluh i dūwanyâkweḥ söḥ paḍa winĕgil*

saṅ aja kadi hanê jro rājyâpan sira kinĕmit,
sahana hana nikaŋ saṙwwāstra lwiṙ pinakapagĕṙ,
raŧa turaga tiniṅkaḥ baprâṅrakṣa sana sini,
makagupura halĕp niŋ mātaṅgâruhur ajajaṙ*

tucapa para kadūwan tuṣṭa n paṅhinĕpan ira,
sahana hana ri deśanyâneka ŋ paḍa pamapag,
nrĕpasuta sira muṅguḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi loṙ,
sama humatur aṅantî soṙ niŋ wāṇḍira magĕlaṙ*

wiku haji jĕnĕk aṅher iŋ śūnyâlawas amarāt,
wruh aṅaji sira santoṣâṅdo dohi narapati,
nĕhĕr amarahi sāmpun wrĕdđâṅgöṅ ulah alaṅö,
Atuha tuha kadi brĕm santĕn kāku manis ira*

sira ta marĕk aluṅguḥ milw-iŋ dāyaka humatuṙ,
kinasĕgĕhan apan wruḥ ṅūnîŋ rājya sira kabeḥ,
Apituwi paḍa rowaŋ rowaŋ niŋ maṅikĕt ikĕt,
muꝁa niṅ aṅucap aśrī de niŋ mojar akakawin*

kṣamakĕna bapa pawwat niŋ grāmyâđama kaluṣa,
padapa hima lawan centĕn mepâlpa lihatana,
sama duwĕga ri rakryan yan twak haywa hali halin,
pinakabañu bañu ṅke ṅhiŋ yan len juga yan ikā*

wulatana kakudeśanyâŧānî gĕgĕr asĕpi,
ya tuna tuna sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ tĕkwan tan hana dinadak,
palapat alas agaryaŋ gaṙyyaŋ tan sawĕgilana,
linĕṅĕṅakĕn iṅ ambĕk maṙmmanya n rĕsĕp alaṅö*

Aluru wahu kalahrwan kaywanya n śrawaṇamasa,
Asĕpa humuraṅ awyaŋ rurwan ronya kapawanan,
Analukati tĕlā wwad niŋ saṙwwatrĕṇa riṅ ayun,
pĕjah amĕkasi kiṅkiŋ luŋ niŋ jaṅga kapanasan*

tĕwĕk i ragas i kaywanya n karwâraras alaṅö,
tĕṅah i tal ika mambĕt mambĕt kāṅinan aṅĕliḥ,
manis i lahaṅ ikâṅhiŋ panraŋ nraŋ wulat amanis,
tiniru tiru niṅ ahyas ronyâṙjjâpatah akiris*

sĕḍĕṅ iṅ asujimāsâtyantêŋ kaṣṭa gatarasa,
karikil ika kumĕṇḍĕŋ tūt māṙggâmacĕki suku,
saha panas i hĕnunyâdoḥ wwe nora pinalaku,
tuhun amuhara ramyā sakweḥ niŋ wwaṅ ika jĕnĕk*

jalada kadi pĕtĕŋ yan tĕmbe niŋ kapat alaṅö,
jawuh amĕkasakĕn rĕm riŋ kaywan hañar asĕmi,
wahu mari panaṅis niŋ kālaṅkyaŋ suꝁa sumayab,
Asiga kadi tinambaŋ wahw-înantukan agiraŋ*

trĕṇa taru paḍa mĕltik wījanya n masa kalima,
wawaṅ aluru kapiṅrĕs tūt māṙggâṅĕlih alume,
linaran i kĕñar iŋ wꜽ yan luṅhā ŋ rĕmĕṅ anisiḥ,
kadi pamanas i kuŋ niŋ kanyā dūra n atĕlĕba*

hañar abañu tĕgalnya n kānĕm tapwan acarĕcĕḥ,
kadi sinipatan apriḥ māṙgganyâracĕk abĕnĕṙ,
turah i wĕrĕh ikaŋ waṙṣâsat kāri kasarakat,
Asĕmu pupur areḥ tūt piṅgiṙ niŋ halis inamĕṙ*

brata nika ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ māǥâdyus rahina wĕṅi,
jawuh aṅapitu tan pāntyâdrĕs maṅkin akĕcĕhan,
Aṅura ṅuraṅi teja hyaŋ candrâṙkka kaginĕman,
suꝁa salabuh ikaŋ luṅlūṅan māri kapiṅĕliḥ*

lĕbug i palĕmahanyâjro riŋ ꝑālguna puraci,
patuna tunahan iŋ lĕmbw-âsaṅsiŋ tahi papuṅĕn,
dwijawara sira baṙyyan rĕŋrĕŋ moǥa humaliwat,
sumĕpĕr anasi pöhan maṙmmanya n śuci wĕkasan*

masa kasaṅa tĕka traŋ ndan mātrânĕlani jawuḥ,
ya karaṇa ni latĕknyâtiṅgaṙ wahw-asat anisiḥ,
sapapikatana göṅĕn tĕmbe niŋ manuk agalak,
tuhun asĕpi hĕnūnya lwīr agriŋ paḍa caciṅĕn*

kusuma sahana māywan yan wꜽśāꝁa paḍa wijaḥ,
sĕkar iṅ asana kantun kady-ahyun kalarakĕna,
paṅirim irim ikaŋ waṙṣâheṙ weh ayu ḍumawuḥ,
kadi jaruman aṅinte rāgânīs amawa taṅis*

muwah asĕkar alasnya jyeṣṫâmiṅrwani sahapit,
tuhun aṅuraṅi rurwan de niŋ waṙṣa wahu muliḥ,
tura turah i gĕrĕḥnyâgupyan meh amĕkasana,
tuna tuna kadi pamwit niŋ haṙṣâmĕkasi taṅis*

Analahasa laṅönyêṅ āṣāđâṅlarani kawi,
paḍa gumigil aṅinkin tiṅhalnyâniliṅi tawaŋ,
kamaḍiḍiṅĕn aṅepw-î roganyâṅgĕgĕs aṅĕsaḥ,
kadi kahapit aṅunṅun muṅgw-iŋ śūnya kakilatan*

nahan ucapan ira mpuṅkw-aṅde haṙṣa ri saṅ aja,
wĕṅi mara sakamantyan prāptâneka taḍah ira,
dwijawara sira māliḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi loṙ,
para wiku juga kāry-âgoṣṫi mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya*

paḍahi marĕk agupyan śabdanyâmanis inamĕṙ,
kadi paṅucap ucap niŋ muṅgw-i jro jinĕm akule,
Apituwi sinamenîŋ gīta śrī nrĕpatanaya,
rasa nika winiwekâneka ŋ pālapan amanis*

tucapa bala nirâkweḥ ƀāwanya n paṅinum inum,
Aṅigĕl aṅiduṅ asraŋ twaknyâkweḥ kadi humilī,
paḍahi nika gumĕntĕṙ sinraŋ niŋ tabĕ tabĕhan,
kadi baribina saŋ hyaŋ riŋ swaṙggâtukupa kapö*

<jagadđita>

luṅhā ŋ māsa piliḥ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi tiḍĕm sahana niṅ aṅinum paḍâturū,
tistis nora mumik tuhun saṅ aja tan mrĕm amaṅu maṅu tan kĕnêŋ turū,
Aṅhiŋ rāmya rinĕṅwakĕn panalimuṙ nalimur ira ri kiṅkiṅ iŋ hati,
gĕṇḍiŋ walyan arūm swaranya karĕṅö sawĕṅi kiniduṅan kiduŋ buwun*

loṙ wetan pamalantĕnan kaparĕk iŋ lwah adalĕm asamīpa paṅdyunan,
wwaŋnyâwuṅw-amasaŋ damaṙ wruh i masanya n amalu malu meḥ tibā ṅĕnĕm,
tan paśrī swara niŋ palu dyun asarag tĕwas amaribini ŋ wwaṅ aṅrĕṅö,
Endaḥ mwaŋ palu wastra rāmya kadi de niṅ amalu daluwaŋ rinĕṅwakĕn*

Aṅdyun karwa rabinya tan padiwasâwiḍiṅan awurahan siliḥ cacad,
nitya ŋ śabda paḍêṅgal asrak amalĕs hinalan ulih ikâgawe ǥaṭa,

kahyun hyun kadi śꜽwa sogata mapaṅǥaṭapaṭa juga hetu niŋ humuŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ baṇijêŋ tĕpas paḍa sumambutakĕn i sagawe nikâlawas,
norâpĕk paḍa loƀa lāƀa kaharĕpnya n akuṭa kaṭikan paḍâdamaṙ,
saṅkĕp dwalnya huwus ratĕŋ paḍa sumaṅgraha wijila niki n marêŋ pĕkĕn,
Asyaŋ syaŋ karĕṅö humuŋ saṅa saṅanya sĕmu niṅ aharĕp katumbasa*

Eñjiŋ wāhu huwus ḍawuḥ pitu muni ŋ paḍahi baṅun akon adandana,
sakweḥ niŋ prajurit paḍâmuṅu ri paṅhawin ika kamĕnanya maṅkata,
Aṙdđêñjiŋ pwa hiḍĕpnya tĕkwan apuyĕŋ ya ta karaṇa nikâturū muwaḥ,
ṅhiŋ maṅkat saṅ ajâkĕmul kĕmul alañciṅan aṅarahakĕn sakêŋ raŧa*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan wĕnaṅ adoḥ ri sira marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
prajñā tan kasilib ri tiṅkah iṅ asewaka maṅinakanêŋ tuhan tuhan,
wruḥ riŋ yogya kahĕnwa de nira tinūt sapawarah ika rāmya tūt gĕgĕṙ,
yekā rakwa hĕnūnya ṅūni n aṅaliḥ saha jaruman ikâmĕgat gunuŋ*

śūnyâporaṅ ikaŋ gĕgĕṙ hana guhā rĕbah adalĕm arĕs twas iŋ mulat,
tan pātmā ṅ aṅuṅaŋ hanan kadi hanâṅduhuṅakĕna tĕkā sakêŋ wuri,
tistis nora marâṅlĕṅĕŋ ri pataninya paḍa kadi sinaṅgan iŋ kawi,
ṅhiŋ raṅrö gumĕrĕḥ tinūb niṅ aṅin adrĕs aniru gĕrĕh iŋ labuḥ kapat*

ṅkānê lĕmbah ikâlaṅö pamaḍĕkan wwaṅ ika wija wijaḥ paḍâṅayaṙ,
lumrâkweh aputiḥ wuyaḥnya kasawuṙ sumarasah anamaṙ wway iŋ jawuḥ,
Awrā tampĕr ikâgĕlaṙ kasarakat sarakat asĕmu sāri niŋ puḍak,
haṙṣâmbĕk saṅ aja n tĕkâwuya wuyaḥ mata tuwin aharip kadînusap*

tambak tambak akaṇḍa loṙ kidul i pomahan ika kadi piṇḍa niŋ sawaḥ,
wwaŋnyârampak amet wĕlut kadi pucaŋ pucaṅan iṅ aṅurit katiṅhalan,
pakṣinyâgĕṅ agĕŋ humuŋ kadi kĕbo paṅulah awurahan siliḥ buru,
yan kawrĕg paḍa möṙ gumĕntĕr anamaṙ gĕrĕh iṅ adurugan paḍâwĕrö*

Aƀrā lwiṙ sĕkar iŋ laṅit braja katon pamĕwĕh i supit iŋ sahiŋ sahiŋ,
Aṅjraḥ tan kahanan lĕwas pasuṅ ikâsira sira kadi kĕmbaṅ iŋ karaŋ,
lwiṙ luŋ niŋ katiraḥ miraḥ ni suṅut iŋ huraṅ aṅariṅ ariŋ marêŋ lumut,
tūt māṙggâharĕmis pĕjaḥ kadi mĕnuṙ saka salawĕ lawö sumamburat*

sāmpun lĕpas raŧa narendrasutâpan adrĕs,
saŋ brāhmaṇê wuri lawan rĕṣi śꜽwa bodđa,
Agyā paḍânututi tan hana kāry-araryan,
muṅgw-iŋ gajâśwa raŧa masraṅ alumba lumba*

lwaḥ naṙmmadā katĕmu de naranāŧaputra,
saŋ brāhmaṇâsaƀa saƀā ri ya sāri sāri,
Atyanta niṙmmala paṅawruhanê śucinya,
maṙmmanya n uttama wijilnya sakêŋ śaśāṅka*

söḥ puṣpa laywan iṅ atīṙŧa hanê hĕnīnya,
kuntul paḍâṅadĕg adĕg ri pacaṙ pacaṙnya,
līlā ḍarā ri kalakānya wijaḥ paḍâdyus,
Akweḥ mayūra maṅigĕl ri pasiṙ pasiṙnya*

nyū danta medi ri manaḥ nira keṅin eṅin,

manda swaranya karĕṅö nira tan sꝑuṭârūm,

Abyūran iŋ lwah alĕtuḥ kakĕbuṙ bañunya,

mĕttâwĕrö nĕhĕr asumpiṅ aǥaṇṭa kambaŋ,
Aƀrā katiṅhalan ikā kadi nāgapuṣpa*

meww-îwu saṅꝁya ni gajaḥ naranāŧaputra,

kĕnoḥ patakwanta ri tiṅkah i ṅhulun,

ṅke naṙmmadā ṅhulun acaṅkrama sāri sāri,
kañcit kapaṅgih aṅadĕg ƀagawān pataṅga,
pakṣâdyusâpatĕlĕsan tumuluy marêŋ lwaḥ,

göŋ krođa wākcala sira n panibāni śāpa,

ṅke tôṅgwanamwa tan adoḥ ya sakêrikiŋ lwaḥ,

saṅkêṅ amaṅgih i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,
tapwan śināpa tumuluy matĕmaḥ gajendra*

An maṅkana bwat i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,
kāruṇya budđi nira riŋ wĕkasan sirâsiḥ,
Āpan ṅhulun marĕk anĕmbah apinta kāsiḥ,
maṅhyaŋ ry-anugraha nirê rikaṅ antaśāpa*

mojaṙ sirâsĕmu manis tĕkap iŋ tumiṅhal,
Om haywa saṅśaya ri sidđa niṅ antaśāpa,
tan lupta yan tĕka hĕlĕm saṅ ajâhawan ṅke,
tuŋtuŋ ni sañjata nikā hawananta mantuk*

sāmpun sirâmĕkasakĕn wacanântaśāpa,
luṅhā sira ṅhulun aṅanti humeṙ tĕkanta,
sowenta tan tĕka ya kāraṇa niŋ ƀramanta,
mĕttâwĕrö pira piraŋ tahunĕn byamoha*

maṅke n ḍatĕŋ kita sahâśwa sahasra saṅꝁya,
ṅke naṙmmadâwija wijaḥ sawatĕk watĕkta,
mātĕṅga papraṅ aṅiriŋ paḍa sāra śūra,
mawrĕg rĕbaḥ binuru ni ṅhulun iŋ paḍöman*

Aṅhiŋ kitâmanah anuṅsuṅ iṅ astra tīkṣṇa,
syuḥ kumƀa ni ṅhulun ikā tinut iŋ paratra,
ndātan paniṣꝑala wawaŋ maluyâdadi hyaŋ,
sākṣāt kitâmrĕta wijil nikaṅ antaśāpa*

Atyanta göŋ ni hutaṅ i ṅhulun apramāṇa,
saṅmohana ŋ pamalĕsê kita diwyaśāstra,
ganđaṙwwaśāstra pinajöŋ hyaṅ asañjatêka,
jñānanta maṅlĕpasakĕn saha mantra sidđi*

Atyanta yogya yan ajinta ya kawruhanta,
kārāđananya saha mantra sahêndikanya,
pöŋpöŋ ṅhulun wruh i wĕkas ni rusit rusitnya,
śaktinya kawruhan anambĕhanê guṇanta*

ndātan pamatyani guṇanya yadin guṇanta,
śatrw-âđamâpituwi tan mati denya mūṙcꞓa,
moǥâturū sahana niŋ ripu tan wri rātnya,
nistanya maṅkana yayā kita yan jayêŋ praŋ*

he saŋ priyambada kita n paṅutus paṅajya,
moǥâwiraŋ hulun apan gumawe laranta,
ṅūnî sĕḍĕŋta matĕmaḥ gajamattarūpa,
tan len ṅhulun kaṅaranan karaṇanta māti*

hā hāḥ hade saṅ aja denta manaṅgah eraŋ,
An sāhasâmĕjahi ri ṅhulunĕn gajendra,
Āpan prasidđa kita maṅhwatakĕn kajanman,
Atyanta göṅ i hutaṅ i ṅhulunĕn maluy hyaŋ*

yadyan saƀūṙ ƀuwah ikaŋ guṇa kawruhanta,
tātan sadoṣa yan atambĕha wīṙyya saswaḥ,
ndā maṅkanā kita n aṅajya wimohanāstra,
taṅgap nihan hila hila ŋ tumulak paweweḥ*

An saŋ priyambada kĕdö maṅutus maṅajya,
mary-âwiraŋ saṅ aja sāmpun atiṅkah uṅgwan,
loṙ saŋ priyambada kidul saṅ ajâtalaṅkup,
saṅmohanênaji nirêṅgal apan widagđa*

sanđinya kāku saha śakti ni dewatanya,
saṅyoga niŋ śarawara mwaṅ ikā tujunya,
sāmpun tama stuti nikā saha kūṭamantra,
saṅhāramantra paḍa kawruh ira praƀeda*

wruḥ saŋ priyambada ri haṙṣa narendraputra,
An pembuh astra śara sūkṣma mahāpraƀāwa,
tiṅkaḥ niṅ apraṅ inucap nira moǥa jambat,
Amwit sirâsĕmu manis baśa de niṅ ojaṙ*

he mitra mantuka kakanta lumarya maṅke,
sidđā ŋ prayojana kita n ḍatĕṅêŋ widaṙbƀa,
nāhan wuwus nira nĕhĕṙ maṅagĕm sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,
luṅhâhawan gagana mĕltuk apan sira hyaŋ*

sāmpun prāpta sirêŋ surālaya wicitraraŧa paḍa suꝁa n tumon sira,
