ṙyyak niŋ tīṙŧa sinrĕṣṭi wastra tinulis pinakatiba tibān linaṅwakĕn,
tustus niŋ maṇi sūṙyyakānta dumilaḥ rahina wĕṅi dinadyakĕn damaṙ,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ cirapattra kalpatarupuṣpa sadĕdĕg aṅadĕg tigaŋ siki,
māyā niŋ wulan iŋ samudra mađu śudđa saꝑala ginawe laṅit laṅit*

byaktâbyakta nikaŋ tulis wuwuh i kādƀuta nika tulis iŋ huwus tama,
yan kĕmbaŋ kadi mambwa rūmnya kadi molaha winilĕt i luṅgah iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mwaŋ yan wwaŋ wwaṅan aṙjja kady-aṅucapâsĕmu sĕmu guyu de nikā mulat,
wimba hyaŋ smara śudđi de niṅ anulis lwir amanaha manaḥ nrĕpātmajā*

ṅkā tôṅgwan nṛpatiputrikā piniḍuḍuk tuhu tuhu sira janma dewatī,
tan sāmānya mahāpraƀāwa tĕka riŋ kaka kaka kadi dewakanyakā,
Aśrī pahyas ira bwat indrawanitâmuwuhi halĕp ira n hanêŋ saƀā,
ḍaŋ saṅǥâguñĕpan ƀaṭāra karikâṅrakĕt ujar ira yan tumon sira*

sakweḥ kweḥ nira saŋ kadaŋ haji huwus kili marĕk atatā paḍâtuha,
mambö paṙwwata pājaran halĕp i de nira humalĕpakĕn suputrikā,
Endaḥ mwaŋ sira saŋ rare hañar ataṅkil ahayu hayu wahw-ameꝁala,
mambö maṇḍala riŋ saƀā paṅuparĕṅga ni halĕp ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā*

strī strī wāhu cumampakâsĕmu hijo pamulu nika pinantĕs iŋ saƀā,
sampiṙnyêŋ jaja tan paniṣꝑala hananya muwuhi halĕp iŋ wulaŋ tatuṙ,
tuṅgal denya mawâmbĕk abwat atuhan ri parĕk ika ri jöŋ nrĕpātmajā,
lwiṙ dewī humatuṙ sakêŋ surapadânrahakĕna halĕp iŋ surālaya*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

praḥ praḥ nrĕpawaraduhitā ri guṇḍik ira len i kaka kaka nira,
yan wruḥ wruh agamĕl aṅiduŋ lawan wruh aṅawat ya linĕṅĕnan ira,
Embuḥ pwa guṇa nika siniṅhĕlan kinaluṅan ya kinalĕwihakĕn,
sāmpun pwa ya kawi paḍa kāku siŋ guṇa samaṅkana ya kinarahan*

sakweḥnya paḍa marĕk anaṇḍaṅ anwam araras rara rahayu wagĕd,
saƀyâmanis aṅucap ikāṅ asiṅhĕl akaluŋ wahu kawi kakawin,
ndan rwaŋ puluh ikaṅ akaraḥ jitākṣara wicakṣaṇa naṭakagiṇa,
ṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayaluh ikaṅ inuttamâsisik ĕmās maṇi nĕhĕr amawa*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

prāpta ŋ rātri yayan katon hayu ni waṙṇna nira ri wijil iŋ niśākara,
hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ mađumāsa rūpa nira yan kasaṅa kasapuluḥ tiniṅhalan,
maṅke n māsa kapat hyaṅ iŋ masa kapat kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ mulat,
cañco strī liṅa niŋ tumon sira mĕne n huwus atĕmu lawan nrĕpātmaja*

lumrâmintaṅ ahöm ri bāhu lumarap jĕnu nira kanakâṅhulap hulap,
Embuḥ söŋ ni tutup gĕluŋ nira murub maṇik ika kadi motar otaran,
de niŋ kostuƀa nīla kādƀuta sĕkaṙ taji nira sumĕnö kapañjutan,
Ūṙṇnā śudđa huwus hanêŋ rahi nirâsĕmu paṅawaka tĕṅran iŋ hurip*

ndin ṅgānya ŋ wwaṅ anĕmwa rūpa kadi rūpa nira n ahayu rājaputrikā,
wwaŋ riŋ rājya yayan kapūhan aṅalĕm ri sira kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,
Aśrī waṙṇna nira n tuhan saꝑala yogya n adĕgakĕna ratwa niŋ tulis,
tan samwas lawaṅ iŋ kaḍatwan inucap milu milu kawĕṅān tiniṅhalan*

paṅkun mesya ṭikā kayogyan i wĕtis nira damarana teja niŋ wulan,
pantĕs yan makasumpiṅĕn kikirĕn iŋ kuku kuku nira kosapêŋ laṭi,
reꝁan riŋ kakawin wilāpa kahalĕp ni susu nira parantya niŋ parab,
tan sāhêŋ ratu śakti kenaka ni soca nira yan ikĕtĕn sĕkaṙ taji*

Ekĕl roma nirâraras kadi katona rumaraba sakêŋ gĕluŋ lukaṙ,
Akweḥ mahyun aṅuḍwa de nira yan ahyas anisigi wajâṅhĕmū guyu,
yogyâsaṅkan aṅin dumadyakĕna polah i tikĕl i halis nira n cala,
byaktâgatgat ataṅhya taṅhya manah iŋ mulat i muꝁa nira n pasaŋ damaṙ*

ndin putry-âhayu hayw-amaṅpaṅa hayunya ri hayu nira n ahyas aṅḍiri,
sakweḥ niŋ wwaṅ ahadyan akryan asawaŋ hinayu marĕk i jöŋ nirâlawas,
pahyas niŋ para pora maṅhiribi pahyas ira hinayu cihna niŋ manūt,
Ekacꞓattra raras raras nira paṅöban iṅ ahayu sujanmakanyakā*

sakweḥ saŋ ratu tan wĕnaŋ sahasa kewala humĕnĕṅ aṅantyakĕn pariḥ,
Aṅlampū sumĕsĕl śarīra nira tan wĕnaṅ anĕkani senakê hati,
mogânaṅgĕl arĕs rumĕṅwakĕn i kādƀuta ni hayu narendraputrikā,
mawwat rāga wilāpa cihna niṅ akūṅ alah alĕh akirim kirim ṭikā*

Akweḥ pahyas irârĕbut kahulunan kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ marĕk,
rorw-aŋ campaka rāmya māyun ayunan ri jaja nira n amaṅya maṅyani,
lāwan pādapa tan wĕnaŋ sah i sirâmĕpĕti gaway ika n sĕh iŋ gĕluŋ,
tañjuŋ muṅgw-i kapö nira n mrik inaṅit marĕk araras anulya nulyani*

prāptôliḥ kalaṅön ikāṅ asana rāmya pinakakalasā nirâturū,
mwaŋ roṇḍonya tinap rinūpaka tilam sinalinan i sĕḍĕŋ nikâluñut,
maṅgā sĕmpalĕn aṅkĕn eñjiṅ alapĕn humatura śayanā nira n rimaŋ,
swaṙgga n māti kakiṅkiṅan huwus akīṙtty-amihutaṅi laṅö ri jöŋ nira*

moliḥ waṙṣa sipat nirârahat i solah ika tĕka hirĕŋ hanê mata,
kālanya n kahĕmū sĕpaḥ nira baṅun pinakaliḍah ira n hanê tutuk,
kāsiḥ kāsih irâlawas karika puṇḍutan ira kasĕlap hanê hati,
ṅhiŋ kĕṇḍit nira mās tumūt i parahasyan ira wahu marĕk sinanmata*

tambe rakwa sira n swayambarakĕnâmiliha sakaharĕp nira praƀu,
ndān ambĕk nira kewalâwiraṅ i līṅa niṅ umulat anĕṅgahâhaṅan,
Āpan tan hana ṅūni kewala sirâmuṅari pinakakabwatan hañaṙ,
yekā hetu nirâwiweka kalawan kaka kaka wihikan riṅ iṅgita*

ndātan kaṙkkaśa de nirâṅucap ucap ri pasĕlur iṅ ujaṙ sirâṅucap,
ndi ŋ paṙwwa ndi kitâṅrĕṅö n hana kadi ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā,
yadyastun hana maṅkanā niyata ta pwa wiraṅ ika kadîraṅ i ṅhulun,
saŋkṣepanya huwus katon wiđi nareśwara dinulur i tan sih iŋ wiđi*

Āpan kenaka niŋ kadi ṅhulun aṅanti ri kaka haji yan sirâsiha,
heṙ herĕn palarĕn hanâsiha ƀaṭāra tumĕkakĕna đaṙmma ni ṅhulun,
prāptânomaha yogya liŋ nrĕpati samƀawa kaharĕpa ni ṅhulun muwaḥ,
yadyastun layata ṅhulun pi tawanĕn ry-uƀaya haji paran kasaṅśaya*

lāwan yan hana ratw-anomaha marā ta sira humaturê nareśwara,
ndātan kahyuna ni ṅhulun sira tuhun kaka haji sira kewalâharĕp,
haywâmiđyani ta pwa siḥ siha nirâmawarĕṅĕha ri budđya ni ṅhulun,
ndak ton duḥka nikaŋ kinĕdwakĕn apaṅgiha wiꝑala yan tan paḍâharĕp*

yan kāṅĕn suꝁa niŋ licin dumadak ahyun adaluwaṅa haṙṣa riŋ jamaŋ,
denya n kilya rarā makāśraya nareśwara kumĕmita kāla niŋ rare,
yan wrĕdđâjara đaṙmma riŋ giriwanâmagĕhakĕna ri đaṙmma saŋ wiku,
rāmya ŋ waŋ guru loka saṙwwa tĕka yan lumaku laku rinampak iŋ kili*

maṅke pwa n ḍumawuḥ wiđi nrĕpati tan pamawarĕṅĕh i budđi ni ṅhulun,
ṅwaŋ dūra n wĕnaṅâjñalaṅǥana tuhun rasa pĕjaha tibêŋ paluṅguhan,
Ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp kalīṅa ni manaḥ nira yan aharĕp iŋ swayambara,
maṅgâṅdadya limut ṅhulun ri wiraṅ i ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

tuhan i ṅhulun akṣamakĕna paṅucap ni manĕḥta rĕṅön,
wiđi saŋ praƀu samƀawa kĕkĕsakĕnê hati yogya dahat,
dumadak pwa hade n katĕkana rinasan ri manaḥta tuhan,
pira haywa nikâṅucapa n ahala yan hiniḍĕp mahala*

pituhun wiđi saŋ praƀu tuhan anipis kawiraŋta hade,
paḍa wāhu ḍatĕŋ sahana hana nikaŋ pariwāra marĕk,
Amahuṙ hurakĕn ri para ratu pinetnya sirêŋ wĕgilĕn,
sira saŋ kinabehan inalĕm ika rĕṅwakĕnanta tuhan*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saŋ nāŧêŋ magađa praƀāwa nira tan patĕpi kadi laṅit maṅambara,
lwiṙ widyāđara daṙśśanīya pakatonan i bala nira śūra dug siṅī,
Ahyaŋ solah irâmanis kawadi de nira lituhayu tan pasiŋsiṅan,
sākṣāt indra sakêŋ surālaya kaweni tumuta mijilêŋ swayambara*

krūrākāra saṅ aṅganāŧa sanirukti sira yan aruhuṙ sulakṣaṇa,
saƀyâmbĕk nira tan rinakwa sira yan praƀu lituhayu sādarâṅucap,
śakty-ânindya mahāpraƀāwa kumutug bala nira paḍa śūra suśrama,
tan pendaḥ kadi saŋ hyaṅ agni mijil amralayakĕna rumampaka ŋ jagat*

siṅhâmbĕk saṅ awantināŧa kadi saŋ yama guṇa nira lokapālaka,
norâđaṙmma ṅaranya rakwa yan i ƀūmi nira paḍa suꝁâgawe hayu,
söḥ wadwā nira piṇḍa kiṅkarabalâmawa curiga gadāyuđâpupul,
sākṣāt mrĕtyu curik nirâkas aluṅid baṅun aṅayam ayam parāṅmuꝁa*

tan pendaḥ baruṇânurun saṅ anupāđipati suyaśa ƀūmipālaka,
himpĕṙ sāgara kāṅinan bala nirâṅrwabi nagara hibĕk tĕkê dalĕm,
tĕkwan lwiṙ nira riŋ raṅin đwaja wĕlaŋ wĕlaṅ aputih arok lawan hirĕŋ,
rāhu mwaŋ śaśiwimba rūpa nika kāraṇa ni musuh irâtabĕḥ titiṙ*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

siŋ solaḥ saŋ susenā pracalita kadi saŋ bāyu riŋ budđi madrĕs,
wadwā wadwā riṅ ambĕk lituhayu katĕṅĕṙ yan prawīrâprih iŋ praŋ,
himpĕṙ seḍuŋ karĕsrĕs bala nira kumisik lwiṙ gĕlap holih asriŋ,
byakta syūha ŋ musuḥ de nira n asĕmu hudan sañjatâwoṙ halisyus*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgadâtyanta sugih ira hibĕk mās maṇik rājayogya,
līlâcum somya saŋ wꜽśrawana paḍa nira n ǥorarūpâdawâgöŋ,
norânaṇḍaŋ yatan mās bala nira satĕgal kāla niŋ hanyan aṅjraḥ,
sakweḥ niŋ śatru śīṙṇnâkuniṅa wulat ikā de nirâpan wah iŋ mās*

Aśrī saŋ pāṇḍya śudđākrĕti nira satirun paṇḍitânwam widagđa,
tan kāsy-asiḥ tuhun tan harĕp iṅ ulah agasyak yayan sopacāra,
saŋ hyāṅ īśāna sākṣāt paḍa nira n ahalĕp riŋ saƀā nora tan wruḥ,
Atyantêŋ yoga kawruḥ nira karaṇa nira n katwaṅ iŋ śatru śakti*

wwantĕn saṅkêry-ayođyā lituhayu dahatĕn rājaputrâdwitīya,
ndan rakwânak mahārāja raǥu saṅ aja saṅjñā nirêŋ rāt prakāśa,
saŋ saptāđikrĕtâtyanta halĕp ira kabeḥ soṙ kagöṅan pratāpa,
himpĕṙ candrâkucĕm tan wani mulat i narendrātmaja lwiṙ hyaṅ aṙkka*

saŋ hyaŋ brahmâgawe rūpa nira kadi paran riŋ raras māṙ manisnya,
yadyan ganđaṙwwa widyāđara niyata nikâsora riŋ rūpa kāliḥ,
Aṅhiŋ hyaŋ kāma saŋ samƀawa mapaga raras rūm nirêŋ maṙttyaloka,
sāmpun pwâṅāśrayê citta nira masuruhan rāga kuŋ don irâṅheṙ*

ndān ambĕk ni ṅhulun ṅhiŋ sira juga kadĕlö n kāptya rakryan suputrī,
Anwam pūṙṇnêŋ paṅawruḥ lituhayu taruṇâpālapan kṣatriyāṅśa,
jaṅgâṅuṅsiṙ kapat rāmya nira winulatan dlāha yadyan patĕmwa,
Āpan tuṅgal sirêŋ rūm kadi wulan aṅilo wimba niŋ candrakānta*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 20

nāhan ujaṙnya paḍâsĕlur awara waraḥ kinatuṅgalakĕn,
söṅ i manaḥnya katon sĕmu sĕmu niṅ akuŋ ri narendrasuta,
ṅhiŋ kakĕna prih ikā sira wiṣaya ni goṣṫi nika n paṅucap,
rūpa nira sŧiti ri twas ika sinamudāya lawan turida*

śrîndumatī suꝁa māṙ hati nira rumĕṅö ry-ucapanya rĕsĕp,
yan tan awĕdya sirêŋ wwaṅ atuha hana budđi nirâmĕpĕra,
rāga nirê saṅ ajâwĕtu taṅis inamĕṙ wĕdi kawruhana,
liŋ nira moǥa lumuḥ yan aharip araras parihāra nira*

mojar ikaŋ rinahasyan ira wacana liŋnya rĕṅön ta tuhan,
saŋ ratu tan hana tan lituhayu kadi dewata rakwa sira,
ndan paḍa soṙ sira de saṅ aja saꝑala putra narendra raǥu,
hīṅan ira n sira yogya kaharĕpana digjaya rūpa nira*

śrîndumatī kĕna rāga tuhun api hade kadi tan malara,
de nira mojar apet silib amarani lokika budđi nira,
haywa wawaŋ pinisiṅgih ujar ika tuhun hiḍĕpĕn sakarĕŋ,
Āpan ikaŋ dadi janma sakaharĕp ikā kaka moǥa dudū*

nista nikân apadudwan ibu kaharĕp iŋ dadi janma kabeḥ,
yan kinatuṅgalakĕn ndya tika hala nikā tuhanĕn pituhun,
māsku mataŋnya kakūṅana saṅ aja tuwin wwaṅ anakta sira,
haywa kĕdö liṅ ira ndan asĕmu sĕmu haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ gumuyu*

ndaḥ paḍa bindar ikaŋ marĕk i sira kapeṅin ajalwa muwaḥ,
moǥa girahyasĕn ambĕk ika katanĕhan turidâṅlarani,
Asyaṅ i rowaṅ ikâṅucap ucapa kinonya marĕk marĕka,
liŋnya nihan sanu saŋ ratu pili pilihan dumĕn i ṅwaṅ ari*

wwaŋ wwaṅ ahadwan agatgat anagu nagu mĕṅgĕp atĕṅw-ahĕniŋ,
ƀāwa nika n kĕna rāga hanan asidĕhâlupa tan paṅinaŋ,
wyaṙŧa sĕrĕḥnya hanê taṅan inagĕm agĕm tuhu tuhw-alaṅö,
ƀrānta rumūpaka saŋ suṅana sĕrĕh asūṅa sĕpaḥ ri waja*

len taṅ agoṣṫi ri gīta saṅ aja ginawenya hañaṙ katĕka,
dudw-aṅalĕm ri palambaṅ ira mamaranî manis iŋ paṅikĕt,
śrîndumatī kawĕlad hati nira rumĕṅö ri rasanya lĕṅĕŋ,
lwiṙ jaruman saṅ ajâmisiki hiḍĕp irâsriṅ akon mijila*

saŋ wwaṅ inuttama sāmpun adaluwaṅ adoḥ sira riŋ wiṣaya,
milw-atuhâmbĕk irârarĕm arĕja suśīla lanâsiḍakĕp,
tan rĕṅu tan lumiriŋ duga duga pakatonan i tiṅhal ira,
yan paṅucap sira tan paṅucap ucapa len saka riŋ kawikun*

strī sĕḍĕṅ iŋ wiṣayânwam ahaṅan apasabraṅan ambĕk ika,
mwaŋ sira saŋ wiku wrĕdđa marĕk aṅipi nāga milĕt ri sira,
yan wulat aṅdu matanya dinulur i halisnya tikĕl minahā,
maṙmma manisnya paḍâṅucapakĕn i kahaṙṣa nikā karĕṅö*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

wiku rājya kawi wruh aṅaji kaharĕpku siwiṅkwa sanu,
kakawinya palaṙ piguṇana ri parĕknya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,
Ulah iŋ paḍa kāsy-asih aṅapi laṅö hiḍĕpĕṅkwa suꝁa,
kĕmulaṅkwa jajanya taṅan ika saput saputaṅkwa susu*

Agaḍuḥ kawi kāpti mami sanu wĕnaŋ pasaƀā pawukiṙ,
wijil iŋ pihutaŋ pawadal inani rowaṅ ikânuꝁani,
kalawan kalaṅönya wĕnaṅ anigakĕn manah iŋ prihatin,
yadin aṅlĕṅĕṅâdulura maṅusirê trĕbis iŋ paraṅan*

Atitiḥ kaharĕp mami sanu wĕka niŋ pihutaŋ hutaṅan,
wruha têŋ kakawin kiduṅ ulah ulah iŋ wahu wāhu kawi,
saparanya pamaṅkwakĕna lĕpihan amrih ameta laṅö,
sumĕpĕṙ sĕpĕrêŋ papihutaṅan i saṇḍiṅ ikaŋ pasisi*

kaharĕpkw-alawas ṅhiṅ abasana wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅön,
niyatârarasĕn marĕk anigi nigî pamabaṙnya tapiḥ,
paṅapusnya hatiṅku laris i paṅawaknya katon adadaṙ,
prawalanya marêŋ papasaṅan ika ta n kaharĕpku sanu*

puhawaŋ wahu wahw-amrĕti mrĕti katönku siwiṅku sanu,
turidaṅku kaḍaṇḍa n alawas aharĕp wwatĕn iŋ banawa,
Aputĕk hati niŋ kasarapuṅ alaṅö mulat iŋ pasisi,
kaputĕṙ hati ni ṅhulun alal aharĕp tumutêṅ alayaṙ*

Anak iŋ prajurit mĕtu pajurit ikaŋ kaharĕpku sanu,
lĕwu rāmya niki n katĕkana lurugan ri huwuskw-atĕmu,
hawinĕṅkwa curiknya saha raṅin ikā payuṅaṅkwa tumūt,
tan arĕs yak umilwa sĕḍĕṅa nika keṇḍita riŋ palagan*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

ya ta tĕmahana tiṅluṙ denya n śꜽwa sira siwin,
Ikaṅ apalaran anwam wruḥ têŋ śāstra wiku haji,
lilu tumakula lampūn dan yan paṇḍita nagara,
Atuha tuha bagañjiŋ byaktâṅhöbi yan inusiṙ*

kunaṅ amuhara kiṅkiŋ yan bot swan sipi mararas,
wiku mirah aguṇâśrī maṅgĕḥ wikwa narapati,
sira ta siwin aharyan santoṣâmalara dĕmak,
palumutana yan anwam yan wrĕdđâpuput anadi*

taha sanu yan i rantĕntâṅhiŋ tyāga juga siwin,
sipi raras iṅ ataṇḍaŋ deśâdoḥ mahas alaṅö,
lĕwu suꝁa niṅ akarwan soŋsoŋ yan jamaṅ anipis,
pakararas ika paṅkun gantin mwaŋ palu daluwaŋ*

tuhu marika wuwusta ndan son moǥa salah ile,
tĕka turida kĕna priḥ de saŋ brāhmaṇa siniwi,
mulat iṅ awĕka mambaŋ prajñā prāya jitasaƀā,
ṅhiṅ amuhara wiraṅroŋ heman đūṙtta cala nika*

kunaṅ amuwuhi rāgī riŋ twas ni ṅhulun alawas,
wĕka wĕka capaṅ apriḥ riŋ praŋ wāni panagara,
Aṅawayuha saliŋ liŋnya n sāmpun ṅwaṅ apatutan,
Ikaṅ ujar ibu rakryan kady-asyaŋ maṅiṅin iṅin*

nahan ucapan ikaŋ strī tĕmbenyânĕmu turida,
tan awuni ri manaḥnya n ƀrāntâkuŋ managu nagu,
hana ta titir anambut wehan milw-aṅucap ucap,
mawara warah i rumrūm niŋ sāminya tan awiraŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rare mĕrĕ mĕrĕḥ pajātyan agĕlo winara warahan iŋ pasaṅgaman,
mapaŋ kumĕtĕr aṅgamĕl susu taṅanya saha kĕtĕ kĕtĕg sumamburat,
Uliḥ niṅ amuruk muruk tinaṅanan ri pataṅanan i sanđi niŋ prĕman,
huwus pwa ya tamâharĕp wayuha tan rĕṇa kadi manah iŋ tamêṅ aji*

dudū sanu lawan huwus pracacah asriṅ arabi siniwi priyambada,
huwus tama karāsikanya kadi waḥ mađu rasa nika riŋ giṇâmanis,
Amakpak aṅucap tuhan tinikĕlan halis i sĕḍĕṅ ikâṅgamĕl tapiḥ,
baṅun pĕjaha riŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan ṅwaṅ i paṅamĕr ikâṅalap hati*

Ikaŋ kawi ñamut laṅönya rinasan saha kakawin araśmi riŋ tilam,
Ikaŋ jariji moǥa kelu ginamĕlnya kinuku hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp tanaḥ,
lanânipati pet manis kawawa kelu kadi lĕkas ikânulis karas,
kiduŋnya panurū nurūnya sahajâṅgamĕli susu nĕhĕṙ kinaṅsyakĕn*

prawīra siniwi priyambada tuhun kawatĕk ulah ika n wanîŋ raṇa,
Añumbu kadi de nika n paṅalawaŋ raṅin i sĕḍĕṅ ika n paṅolakĕn,
Anaṅtaṅ amapag wulat nĕhĕr aminta linawanan anūt mamaṅkwakĕn,
marêŋ susu taṅanya moǥa hiniḍĕp nika ḍuka ḍuka niŋ curik siṅī*

lawan lawanan i ṅhulun wiku miraḥ lituhayu pinakesi niŋ kuṭi,
manisnya kadi poh apādapa tiki n mamaragi gula gaṇṭi dug siṅī,
liriŋnya pinarantyan i ṅhulun iṅ ambyan iṅ umah i sĕḍĕŋ nikânasi,
dudū swara nikê karinya karĕṅö panamaya nika yan parê ṅhulun*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nāhan de nika goṣṫi senak i manaḥnya panalimur ikâharip mata,
tan tuṅgal rumĕṅö ry-ujaṙnya hana hewa hana sĕmu pacĕḥ mĕṅĕn mĕṅĕn,
strī kryan kryan paḍa mūla mūla rabi niŋ kawi muwah aṅucap samaṅkana,
tan doṣâsiṅ ujaṙnya moǥa minanis manisan ika tinuṅtuṅan laṅö*

rakryan kenaka niŋ manuṣya sararā wĕrĕ wĕrĕha yayan papaṅgiha,
Ambĕk nāgarika wruhâṅikĕta ƀāṣa sakurasa sawīja riŋ laṅö,
yan pāywan kakawin maṅaṙwwana wilaḥ kakawin ika palambaṅ iŋ yaśa,
yekā kāma ratī ṅaranya n araras paḍa kawi sawawânak iŋ maṅö*

luṅhâṅdoha marêŋ pasiṙ kahalĕpanya n amarĕṅana māsa kāṙttika,
sakwan selwan ahimya himyana manumpaka ri walakaṅ iŋ karaŋ liman,
ramyâtuntunanêŋ hĕnī ri surud iŋ rwab i tĕpi tĕpi saṅsayâḍake,
līlâmeta huraŋ tanaḥ nĕhĕr asumpiṅ asaṅu saṅu saṅwa niŋ maṅö*

ndak ton haṙṣa nika n parambakana riŋ bañu tuna tuna mombak ombakan,
kāliḥ kālih ikâduluṙ paḍa girahyasĕn anĕmu laṅö lĕyĕp dahat,
strīnyâmiṅkasakĕn tapiḥ jĕnĕk amet uwur uwur agĕlaṙ marêŋ tĕpi,
byaktâlūma kaköma riŋ bañu hasin wĕtis ika panahā nikaŋ mulat*

rūpanya n mahasêŋ pasiṙ kadi katona mahasa ri samudra niŋ tulis,
Āpan de ni lĕyĕp lĕyĕp ni patĕmunya kadi tasik awoṙ lawan laṅit,
yadyastun yan aṅumbaṅêŋ jalađi kawruhan i pamilĕt iŋ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
sākṣāt dewata dewatī mahas ahas lĕṅĕṅ aṭika ṭikan sakêŋ tawaŋ*

budđinya n wahu wahw-acaṅkrama marêŋ pasisi wahu mahas lawan priya,
maṅgā n tan muliha n panon padulur iŋ layar asĕmu matuntunan taṅan,
soliḥnya n pakaraŋ karaŋ winawanan taṅan ulah ulah iŋ hañaṙ hañaṙ,
Apwī niŋ hiliran ya sāđana nikâkĕla kĕlana ri piṅgir iŋ tasik*

piṅgiṙ niŋ paraṅan gihā watu sumoŋ pinakapasaji riŋ marâṅlĕṅĕŋ,
priṅgârĕs tinataṙ hĕnū nika sumĕṅka tumurun atupis rĕṅat rĕṅat,
paṙṇnaḥ loṙ maṅuṅaŋ tasik muꝁa nikā dunuṅan i kĕñar iŋ niśākara,
ṅkāna n paṅhinĕpâmaḍaŋ wulana yadyan aharipa suꝁa n paḍâmrĕma*

tĕkwan pwêki n anak wĕsi nrĕpati kawwaṅan ika wĕka niŋ sinanmata,
yadyastun kilalan tĕkap saṅ ahulun pawĕkasakĕna riŋ marêŋ pasiṙ,
byakta n mantuka molih olih alaṅö haturakĕna ri jöŋ nareśwara,
cihnanya n kawi karwa kāsih ika wāhu wihikan asaƀā saƀâmasiṙ*

nāhan wastu ni denya mojar api doḥ ndan aƀimata nikê suputrikā,
śrī dewîndumatī huwus wruh iṅ apa n kasiliba riṅ ujaṙ samaṅkana,
kālap budđi nirêniriŋ winawa riŋ lĕṅĕṅ amasir ahimya himyana,
ndan mogâpi hade sahuṙ nira paṅawruhana panalimuṙ manaḥ rimaŋ*

siṅgiḥ ṅgānya wuwusta rāmya ṅ akurĕn sarara wĕrĕ wĕrĕḥ paḍâraras,
luṅhâsaṅwa karas tanaḥnya mahasêŋ pasir adulur ahimya himyana,
tan waŋ mātra kasiṅya mātra manah i ṅhulun irikaṅ ulaḥ samaṅkana,
ndak ton kewran ikaŋ giṇâniwi taṅeḥ mamaḍana raras iŋ wujaŋ wujaŋ*

tĕkwan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅhulun ataṇḍaṅa pasisi huwus tama ṅhulun,
pora wwaŋ nika tan wruh iŋ puruṣaƀeda hiliran amukĕt hanâmayaŋ,
moǥêraŋ ṅwaṅ isin maṅambila karaŋ karaṅan i pasurak niṅ ampuhan,
Aṅhiŋ ṙyyaknya maṅaṅkul aṅkul ajajaṙ baṅun asĕgĕh anĕmbah iŋ maṅö*

Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ wukiṙ tĕka rĕsĕp mwaṅ aṅalĕwihakĕn sakêŋ pasiṙ,
de niŋ kweḥ nira paṇḍitâtapa ri paṙśśwa nika kumuliliŋ tĕkê ruhuṙ,
yadyastun ṅwaṅ atiṅgalêŋ nagara wikwa rara maṅusirê munīśwara,
rāmya ŋ pakṣa wukiṙ yayan ku n aṅuṅaŋ ry-aƀimata saṅ apakṣa sāgara*

wöṅîŋ māsa kapat ṅhulun milu ri jöŋ nrĕpati mahas ahas mariŋ wukiṙ,
saŋ hyaŋ lek i surup hyaṅ aṙkka mijil aṅḍaḍari kadi maṅumbaṅ iŋ pasiṙ,
tūban mwaŋ gĕrĕh iŋ patĕṙ tan asarag đwani nika lalitânurū nurū,
Eñjiŋ meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu samaṅkana mawuṅu tinaṅhi niŋ cucuṙ*

Aƀrā kaywan ikaŋ wukiṙ wijah arūm kadi pinisalinan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,
len taŋ saṙwwalatâwilĕt samar arok baṅun ahurupa luṅgu luṅguhan,
sakweḥ niŋ kayu mās lawan kayu puriŋ paḍa paḍa masuṅut wĕlas harĕp,
ṅkānê piṅgir ikaŋ juraŋ pĕtuṅ ikā paḍa kadi pinituŋtuṅan limut*

sore ry-ampĕh ikaŋ jawuḥ kari gĕrĕḥnya muni pinakarāmya niŋ wukiṙ,
lāwan meǥa marantayan tura turaḥnya sinirir iṅ aṅin pĕgat pĕgat,
miṅsoṙ miṇḍuhur aṅlayaŋ kadi dinĕmwan añawĕli kukus carik carik,
himpĕṙ siñjaṅ iṅ apsarī kasarakat ri laris ika sakê pamañcanan*

saŋkṣepanya katon kasor i lĕṅĕṅ iŋ pasisi tĕkap i rāmya niŋ wukiṙ,
tĕkwan wiǥna niṅ aṅlĕṅĕŋ mahasa riŋ pasisi tarahan aṅhaḍaŋ haḍaŋ,
śudđa ŋ paṙwwata nityaśâsĕmu kadewatan i hana saṅ ugrapaṇḍita,
ndak gañjaṙ kita yan kitântuka tasik mamaḍana kapawitran iŋ wukiṙ*

<śiꝁariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ = 17

taham rakryan di ŋ paṙwwata lĕwiha saṅkêŋ jalaniđi,
Anūsâpaṇḍan raṅkaṅ apasir asaṅhub saha kilat,
muwaḥ tan pāntyāntyâmpuhan ika baṅun kāṙttika sadā,
manuknyâliwran yan wahu mari jawuḥ lwiṙ laru laru*

kumĕmbaŋ tuñjuŋ kāṅinan uwur uwuṙnyâṅjrah aputiḥ,
layaṙ niŋ baṇyāgânutakĕn aṅin aṅdoḥ kadi limut,
lĕṅĕŋ ṙyyaknya n sanđyâmirah asĕmu meǥânisik iwak,
laṅit suṅsaŋ lwiṙnya n maśaśađaramāyā makalaṅan*

ƀaṭārī śrī pöḥ niŋ jalađi pinutĕṙ lāwan amrĕta,
muwaḥ catrâśwâtyanta riṅ aṅuparĕṅgê halĕp ira,
tuwin hyaŋ wiṣṇu swāmi nira jĕnĕk i jro jalaniđi,
mataŋnyan mūlya ŋ sāgara karaṇa niŋ paṙwwata sinoṙ*

tuhan putrī tan kemĕṅan iṅ ucapan yogya sahura,
huwus wruḥ rakwê tiṅkah iṅ acala len kṣīrajalađi,
Apan yan mūḋā budđi nira pisaniṅw-ânĕmu sahuṙ,
kunaŋ pwâpan prajñā sira sumahur apyak saha guyu*

ndatan moli n hyaŋ śrī winijilakĕn iŋ kṣīrajalađi,
parĕŋ lāwan catrāśwa kapat ira tekîkaṅ amrĕta,
Apaṅgiḥ mwaŋ hyaŋ wiṣṇu hana riṅ anantāsana sadā,
ya hetunya n soṙ liŋta ṅ acala tĕkap niŋ jalaniđi*

kaka ndi n sora ŋ paṙwwata tĕkap i rūm niŋ jalaniđi,
Apan lwiṙ wruḥ riŋ swaṙgga ṅ aṅahasi puñcak niṅ acala,
paran saṅkan saŋ hyaŋ rawi gati niṅ astodayagiri,
Umādewī sākṣāt mara sira sinaṅguḥ girisutā*

sirâtekā duṙggā ṅaran ira kasaṅꝁyêŋ triƀuwana,
wĕkas niŋ strī sidđi syapa ta sira dewī kadi sira,
huwus limpad riŋ kāṣṭaguṇan atiduṙgga n tiru tirun,
kunaŋ tâpan riŋ bimba ya sira n awās kottaman ira*

ƀaṭāra hyaŋ rudra pwa siniwi nirâtūt silih asiḥ,
Apaṅgiḥ ṅkānêŋ meru sira paḍa sidđapraƀu wiƀu,
mataŋnyan nora hyaŋ kadi sira mahāsidđi dahatĕn,
Anādi n riŋ liṅgodƀawacarita pamyaktana kaka*

sirâtekā tūtĕnkwa lumĕwihakĕn riŋ mahiđara,
sakê sakweḥ niŋ sāgara mapa ta sī madwa karika,
sahuṙ haywâsowe kaka rasa rasâpan kita bisa,
tuhankw-ibw-amwītâlaha tuhu wuwustâhayu dahat*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nāhan de nira goṣṫi rāmya tadanantara rahina huwus ḍawuḥ pitu,
sakweḥ niŋ paricārikâṅiriṅa sāmpun anarima dadaṙ paḍâsalin,
lāwan saŋ wwaṅ inuttamâhayu sujanma paḍa sira marĕk sumaṅgraha,
śrī dewîndumatī sirâṅadĕg awaṙṇna ratu ni lĕṅĕṅ iŋ ṭikâṅaraŋ*

strī stry-ânekawiśeṣa pakṣa ḍatĕṅêŋ paṅuṅaṅan aduluṙ hanêŋ lĕbuḥ,
Ahyaŋ waṙṇna nika n hinĕmban araras pinayuṅan iniriŋ ƀinūṣaṇan,
sakweḥ niŋ kapapag lumiṅsir awĕdîŋ wwaṅ ahalĕp akĕmul ya riŋ wĕṅi,
pañ̈ñjut sañjata len garantuṅ i harĕp prakaṭa baṅun akon sumiṅgaha*

Eñjiŋ rāmya tiniṅhalan sahana niŋ paṅuṅaṅan atatâkatap katap,
de niŋ pañjut awaṙṇna wintaṅ anulaṙ wĕdi karahinanânusup nusup,
mrik ganđanya huwus kinasturi miṅiŋ rinacana tinulis linaṅwakĕn,
wwaŋnyâpiṇḍa surāpsarī saha wimāna wahu tĕka sakêŋ surālaya*

wastrâƀrā pinakapralamba hana riŋ walikuwaṅ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
kram niŋ cawli kukus baṅun truh anisiḥ pinakapaṅuparĕṅga niŋ hatĕp,
himpĕṙ nīrada citrameǥa nika riŋ haḍa pinakatawiŋ tawiŋ maraṙ,
luṅsiṙ baŋ pinakolur olur i pucak pucak ika kadi luṅgah iŋ kilat*

saśrī waṙṇna nikaŋ payuŋ payuṅan akrĕp asĕmu sĕmu paṅjrah iŋ jamuṙ,
Akweḥ waṙṇna nikā hanan dadu hanan prĕcik asira siran paḍâṅadĕg,
de niŋ kweḥ nira saŋ wĕnaŋ paḍa katon kawĕnaṅ ira mijil samaṅkana,
len taŋ biṙyyan amet sĕkaṙ niṅ asanâniru niru halĕp iŋ payuŋ kuniŋ*

saŋ hyaŋ sūṙyya mijil kamantyan abuṅaḥ pawulatan i saƀā nikaŋ kuwu,
wwaŋnya lwiṙ jaladâkĕmul kilat asoŋ hima sahana hananya riŋ lĕbuḥ,
de niŋ kweḥnya lawan praƀā ni sasinaṇḍaṅ ika lumarap aṅhulap hulap,
śaṅꝁa mwaŋ tarayan mrĕdaṅga kumisik mamaji taliṅa niŋ wwaṅ aṅrĕṅö*

wwaŋ wwaŋ ŧāni paḍâduluṙ wahu tĕkâṅibĕki nagara len hanêŋ hĕnū,
tĕkwan riŋ sakurĕn hanânak ika pat lima marĕk amilĕt milĕt laku,
strīnyâṅĕmban anuntun āmĕtĕṅ apan maṅĕlih ika manamby-anuswani,
Aprakprākan apan hilaŋ sasiki lūd kakutil awurahan siliḥ daliḥ*

len têkaŋ kaki kaky-amet putu nikā hilaṅ i sĕḍĕṅ ikā siliḥ sĕḍĕk,
liŋ niŋ strīnya mahâkas ī kita harĕp mulata kita nininya riŋ waneḥ,
Āpan de ni Uninta lāgi ta kitâmupuh i sĕḍĕṅ ikâṅucap kaki,
Iḥ dūrânaṅisâku yan kita midoṣana pĕjahana sĕṅgahĕn bahud*

strī strī wrĕdđa huwus tĕkêŋ kabuyutan milu milu mulat iŋ swayĕmbara,
Aṅhĕmban raray anwam akrak anaṅis winaliṅ ika putunya rakwa ya,
mojaṙ swāmi nikā nini syapiku hāpa ya kaki taha tan putunta ya,
hā hāḥ tiṅgalakĕn hade nini tĕwas kita kabrĕkĕkĕ duḥka kabwatan*

nāhan liŋ nika hāsyakāraṇa sapolah ika tucapa saŋ para praƀu,
ginyākĕn ḍatĕṅêrikaŋ pagĕlaran paḍa mijila kabeḥ sirêŋ lĕbuḥ,
wīṙyyā wīṙyyan amĕtwakĕn hati nirêrikaṅ aṅinakanê wwaṅ iŋ saƀā,
muntab lwiṙ ni halĕp nirâṅarab arab sama sama kadi bahni kāṅinan*

maṅkat śrī magađeśwarâtri gumuruḥ paḍahi nira karĕṅw-agĕnturan,
sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ kapūhan i halĕp nira paḍa mapipit pipit muꝁa,
kady-âṅaṙwwani sumpiṅ endah araras pinatihakĕn ika n paḍâṅuṅaŋ,
tuṅgal waṙṇna nikâbuṅaḥ kadi wulan sasiki pinarawĕñca niŋ smara*

Aśrī waṙṇna saṅ aṅganāŧa sawatĕk watĕk ira mapupul paḍâhalĕp,
himpĕṙ sāgara lakwa lakwan ira rāmya tan asĕpi kapiŋ rwa niŋ laku,
tĕkwan rūpa nirâsĕḍĕp tan ahañaŋ huwus amuyahi ri twas iŋ rimaŋ,
tan tuṅgal stry-aṅaraŋ tumon sira manaḥnya kalara lara karwaban laṅö*

lwiṙ guntuṙ saṅ awantināŧa tĕka gumrĕbĕg ahalĕp anuṅgaṅ iŋ raŧa,
himpĕṙ truḥ sumaput lĕbū nira mĕlĕk pĕtĕṅ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍa mrĕm apĕpĕt mĕpĕti muꝁa ri tuŋtuṅ iŋ sabuk,
Agraḥ rūpa nikaŋ kaḍatwan i kĕtug ni paḍahi nira mapratiđwani*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

liṇḍū lwiṙ saŋ hanūpāđipati manah ikaŋ strī mulat ƀrāntacitta,
miṅgut miṅgut halisnyârĕṅu rĕṅu kadi tan wwaŋnya kewalya mūṙcꞓā,

wānîŋ praŋ saŋ susenā laku nira lumurug kesyan ambĕk nirâkras,

<suwaṅśapattra> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏓ = 18

tucapa tikaŋ wwaṅ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan wagĕd aṅucap ucap,
liṅ ika suputrikā pinakaratna winuni ri dalĕm,
saṅ aja sujanma mās kinĕmit iŋ nagara wahu tĕka,
saꝑala sira n humambanakĕnê narapatiduhitā*

hulĕsana tan bawaŋ jasunanê sĕḍĕṅ ira kapati,
niyata sirâṅliliṙ saṅ aja saṇḍiṅakĕna ri jaja*

saṅ aja paṅisya mon sira wirāga sadaka pasaji,
Aŧawa yadin padadyana sipat narapatitanayā,
nrĕpasuta de nira n gagaṅa mon pusuh usapa mata*

sĕkara niṅ aṅhiḍĕp smara kunaŋ narapatitanaya,
saꝑala n apallawâmbĕt i tĕṅaḥ narapatiduhitā,

ndan atiśaya praƀāwa saṅ ajâdƀuta kagiri giri,
Asana lawan wuṅū paḍa nira ndya ta hurĕn i rika*

Osik budđi nikaŋ wwaṅ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,

Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ rarâhayu lawan lituhayu sawawân apaṅgiha,
ndan maṙmmanya n atĕmwa dūta lĕpihan pirĕsĕpakĕna riŋ pralāpita,
Āpan tan hana raśmi niŋ winaraṅ iŋ wwaṅ atuha tuna de nikâlaṅö,
ṅhiŋ ganđaṙwwawiwāha rāmya katigâmawa sĕrĕh amisāta riŋ pasiṙ*

luṅhâhĕmbana putra putran ika gantin arĕk arĕkanêŋ pararyanan,
liṅlīṅĕn kisapun kudaŋ kudaṅĕn iŋ kakawin ulih iṅ aṅdadak dadak,
yadyan māliha riŋ wukiṙ sipi laṅönya winulatan awikwa wikwana,
Aṅhiŋ gīta panĕmba nĕmbaha nika n huwus inuƀaya mantukêŋ bibi*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

nāhan liŋ nira n aṅlipuṙ lipurakĕn kiṅkiŋ nirê twas nira,
kāsiḥ kāsih irâṅlawan lawani goṣṫy âpan huwus wruḥ kawi,
wwaŋ śrĕṅgāra wicakṣaṇâṅrahati sojaṙnyân asiḥ saŋ praƀu,
pet pet haṙṣa sahuṙnya rāgakaraṇa wruḥ riŋ kasöṅan smara*

yan kanyā ri hiḍĕp patik haji hade kahyūnanâpan raray,
tonĕn de nrĕpati ndya taŋ mađukarā hānê kucup niŋ sĕkaṙ,
lāwan yan lĕwasa ŋ rarâpa pakĕnanyâpan lĕwas riŋ raras,
paṅliṅganya sĕkaṙ lĕwas pisaniṅū kumbaŋ marâṅambuṅa*

saŋkṣepanya sĕḍĕŋ rarā bwatana kiṅkiŋ hundaṅĕn riŋ ṭikā,
maṅgĕḥ de niṅ aṅolakĕn tĕṅah ikā sāmpun pinaṅkw-âṅliga,
kady-aṅgān i sĕkaṙ nikāṅ asana yan mĕmbaŋ katampwan riris,
ṅkāna ŋ ṣaṭpada miwya yan ƀramara saṅjñānya n jĕnĕk tan midĕṙ*

nāhan denya n apet sahuṙ mĕtu rarasnya n pāwak iŋ rāsika,
tambā niŋ rimaṅ aṅlawaŋ lawaṅi kuŋ pet rāga denyâṅucap,
lwiṙ truḥ niŋ mađumāsa kāraṇa ni kiṅkiŋ śrī narendrâsĕwö,
mambö ken lukar iŋ tilam sahur irâtuŋtuŋ rum iŋ saṅgama*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

kanyā liŋta hade kahaṙṣana paḍanya salaga kapana n kakūṅana,
kuŋ jaṅgâṅalayan taŧāpi kapana n pamilĕta raras iŋ rara n lĕwas,
drĕṣṭāntanya sĕkaṙ lĕwas riṅ apa rakwa wulatana mĕne n kasumpiṅa,
kiṅkiŋ tībra yan iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara rarasnya paḍa paḍa lawan jrah iŋ sĕkaṙ*

yêkā têka hade paṅawruhana campaka salaga nika n kinahyunan,
yadyan sumpiṅa niŋ maṅālihi hulĕs lĕwu raras ika yan pagantyana,
mambö rūmnya hanêŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan turah ika rumĕsĕp tĕkê hati,
haṙyyan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅwaṅ i sĕkaṙnya puru puru rĕmĕk katiṇḍihan*

yan laywan pakasumpiṅĕn hana rarasnya tuhun asĕpi solah iŋ lĕwas,
tĕkwan rakwa ꝑalanya moǥa pinalaywan asiṅ amupu luṅsuran sĕkaṙ,
denya n mantĕna rūmnya yan pakirim iŋ wwaṅ ahayu panuwal nikā ṭikā,
Ambönya n huwus aṅharas pipi ya târĕk arĕkana waṅinya kuṇḍaṅĕn*

mwaŋ yan strī hucapĕn rarasnya paḍa ta pwa kaharĕpana tan tayākĕna,
rūmrūm niŋ rara kanyakā kadi saroruha kumuḍu mijil sakêŋ bañu,
himpĕṙ paṅkaja karyakan wahu mĕkaṙ pamĕwĕh i raras iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara,
tan pendaḥ śatapattra wāhu lĕwas iŋ talaga hayu nikaŋ rara n lĕwas*

kanyā ta pwa wiśeṣa riŋ pawaraṅan raras ika marumaḥ lawan riris,
Antuk niŋ maṅalap kasoṙ karaṇa niŋ tinarima marĕkâṅaras pipi,
riŋ paṅkwan winaraḥ riṅ akṣara manaḥ wahu tama wahu wanwa koluyan,
Āṅ aḥ wus kaka liŋnya moǥa kawatĕk ri sĕḍĕṅ ika kinewalânukĕṙ*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ maṅaṙwwani hĕnū rumasa rasana rāmya niŋ kapat,
byaktâlona lakunya sotan ika tan tahu mahas ahas aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
tapwan wanwa dahat tuhun rĕṅu nikâmarahakĕn i harĕpnya hĕmbanĕn,
suṇḍaŋ suṇḍaṅĕn iŋ tĕgal payuṅanâsana hari harin iŋ pararyanan*

tan gyā gyākĕna de nikā lumaku mon karirisana ri mađya niŋ tĕgal,
yan paṅdöla paran kunaŋ wĕnaṅ akona pituhun ika yan lumampaha,
solaḥnyêriṅanâpa tan wuruṅa luḥnya patulaka nikā yadin kĕdön,
ṅhiŋ gānya nya lumampaha n hana gĕrĕḥ maṅarahakĕna kāla niŋ rĕmĕŋ*

ndan yan rāmya nikaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara kapiŋ rwa niṅ arabi rĕsĕp twas iŋ mulat,
kas kas pādapa kāṅinan kas i tĕṅaḥnya kinayuh aṅĕliḥ wawaŋ tumūt,
mwaŋ twasnyâṅasanâṅrĕṅö patĕr adan mĕkara hinudanan karāsikan,
kady-amrĕm kalawan puḍak ṅwaṅ aṅisapwakĕn arisi kanin ragĕt ragĕt*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ lumampah anukū sapara paran iṅ aṅraraḥ musuḥ,
śođâta pwa hayunya nora kakuraŋnya mata waja nikā paḍânulus,
mambö wīra raras rarasnya tĕkap iŋ hañaṅ aṅiriṅ akālihan tapiḥ,
pantĕs pantĕs anuṅgaṅêŋ śakaṭa pamrĕgakĕna kahalĕpnya riŋ hĕnu*

Aśrī raśmi nikaŋ rarā tuha kapiŋ tiga niṅ arabi mon kapiŋ pata,
prāyâsiḥ wilaja n kinolakĕn anaṅgap i waja nika yan wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
dūrâṅrĕṅwana yan kisapwakĕna riŋ śayana pisaniṅūn apaṅgila,
Eṅgal wanwa wisik pisan kadi sadoṣa ginupi tumuluy kataṅgama*

yogya n rowaṅa niŋ licin wanawasânusupa ri pasamūha niŋ sĕkaṙ,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa niŋ mahas mahas atīṙŧa riṅ acala mahārakā gaḍuŋ,
līlânaṇḍaṅa walkalâjar ajarânalawaha jawuh iŋ labuḥ kapat,
śrī rājādayitā pi yogya ta ṅaranya n adulur anusup lawan ratu*

nāhan de nira nāŧa mojar apadudwan ulah ulah ira n paḍâlulut,
budđi śrī naranāŧaputra milu rañca ri wulat ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,
mūṙcꞓâpan wahu wahw-anon rakĕt aṅiṇḍarat anĕmu ṭikā tĕkâlulut,
paŋ niŋ kūṅ asĕwö wilāpa kakawin tinama tama nirê dalĕm hati*

rakryan ṅke kahananku māsku mapa hetu niṅ asĕmu wiwal salaḥ wulat,
Ahyun suŋsuṅĕn i ṅhulun karika māsku karaṇa niṅ arĕṅwa pet ulaḥ,
Om om haywa miṅe nihan ṅhulun amaṅkwakĕna ri kita milw-aḍampana,
taṅgap māsku sĕpaḥku sāmpun amiraḥ rumĕsĕpakĕna rāga ni ṅhulun*

dyaḥ saŋ sāgara katruhan luh apasiṙ panĕpi saṅ ahĕnī hĕnī pupuṙ,
muṅgw-î jro hati kuŋta māsku kapana n rwaba sumapatanê kuṅ i ṅhulun,
Ambĕk ni ṅhulun amrih aṅlayari tan wĕdi kajahata kombakan halis,
swaṙggâku n karĕmêŋ tĕṅaḥta suꝁa kaprĕma kapaguta riŋ karaŋ susu*

rakryan saŋ mađu niŋ kaḍatwan ulih iŋ hyaṅ amituruni sāri niŋ sĕkaṙ,
lwiṙ tawwan pakatonan iŋ kaka kakâṅrubuṅ ahayu paḍâṅisis wĕtis,
de niŋ hyunku tumon manista n agĕlaŋ gupura maṇi duwĕg pakolihĕn,
ndak lampū pĕtĕṅ iŋ mulat sakahananta ri dalĕm ibu rohĕn i ṅhulun*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

ndaḥ nāhan liŋ narendrātmaja ri hati nirâpan sira ƀrāntacitta,
rakryan putrī marê śrī magađapati pĕnuḥ wwaŋ manonton marê jro,
Awrĕg de saŋ sunandā kadi lanaṅ aṅusī sāhasânĕmbuṅ iŋ hwī,
ramyâwelā katon riŋ wĕkasan aṅililan śrī suputrī tinonton*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

mojaṙ śrī magađāđipê nrĕpasutā nihan ibu marĕkâkisapwana,
socaṅkw-îbu lawan matanta sakadaŋ paḍa paḍa dadi niŋ gula drawa,
Atyantêbu hayunta tan patatalan tuhu tuhu n awatāra niŋ ratiḥ,
heman māsku yatan papaṅgiha lawan ṅhulun apan awatāra niŋ smara*

wruḥ ku n tan hana sanmatanta hana duṣṭa marĕki ri kitâmadohakĕn,
tonton denta matanta mĕṅgĕp amanis dumadak arĕṅu yan tumon ṅhulun,
paṅron wimba nikuŋ halista n abĕnĕṙ kuṭila milu ri tuŋtuṅ iŋ hiḍĕp,
tan saṅkêŋ hana doṣa kimburu manaḥta tĕka wiwal apeda ri ṅhulun*

rakryan janma ni janma ni ṅhulun adadyana ratu tumutêŋ swayambara,
ndan rakryan ta muwaḥ swayambarakĕnâmiliha ratu ri mađya niŋ saƀā,
denya n tan kinasanmatanta palalun sinalahasa ri tan sih iŋ wiđi,
rāmya ṅwaŋ pinagantakĕn tulusa tan tulusa tuwi yayâpuput raras*

nāhan de magađeśwarâṅucap arūm amalar i sahura nrĕpātmajā,
śrī dewîndumatī tan eṅĕh apa tan hana manah ira keṅĕrê sira,
maṙmma śrī naranāŧa mantĕn aṅucap tĕhĕr amaḍĕm ikaŋ smarê hati,
wruḥ ri wyaṙŧa ni kuŋ nirê nrĕpasutā n kadi wiꝑala niṅ ahyun iŋ tulis*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

ndaḥ mojaṙ saŋ sunandā ri narapatisutā liŋnya tiṅhal tuhanku,
nāhan ta śrī mahārāja magađapati saŋ yogya petĕn siwinta,
yadyastun sidđa rakryan sasisihana hulĕs dlāha lāwan narendra,
sakweḥ niŋ strī hanê jro nagara niyata tan sāha saṅkê padanta*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

sugyan tan wruha māsku yan śrī magađeśwara sira maṅaran parantapa,
sāmpun śīṙṇna musuḥ nirâwrĕg i kaḍatwan ika mati ri mađya niŋ raṇa,
Aṅhiŋ pat lima śeṣa niŋ karahatan paḍa kawĕkas anūt marê sira,
saŋkṣepanya yaŧāṙtta māsku sira yan prakaśita maṅaran parantapa*

yan riŋ wīṙyya lawan guṇa syapa sirâṅlĕwihana sira yan paḍa praƀu,
waḥ riŋ mās maṇik uttama ndya ṅ adagaŋ lumĕwihana sira n đaneśwara,
sāmpun pūṙṇna kadānaśūran ira kaprakaśita tĕka riŋ purāntara,
ṅhiŋ putrī kakuraŋ ni ǥāra nira hetu niṅ aṅadu ri māskw-aṅĕdwakĕn*

wwantĕn deśa lĕṅĕŋ ri puṣpapura ƀūmi nrĕpati pasamūhan iŋ kawi,
luḥ niŋ strī kĕna rāga rakwa talaganya pinarigi ri laywan iŋ gĕluŋ,
sambatnya n panaṅis ya tâṅdadi mađubrata hana dadi cātakêŋ tawaŋ,
mambö rūm ni muꝁanya sāmpun atĕmaḥ kumuda mĕkar i tambwaṅ iŋ wulan*

ṅkā tênduŋ parananta māmĕṅ amĕṅ an huwus atĕmu lawan nareśwara,
ƀuktin siḥ nira denta rāmya niṅ atuntunan adulur akālihan payuŋ,
yêkā wīṙyya ṅaranya riŋ kadi kitâhayu pinuji yan amrih iŋ priya,
ramyâṅaṙwwana ḍampa riŋ para paran sipi wanĕh iṅ akālihan tilam*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– |– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandâmanis araras arūm de nikâkon atĕmwa,
sāmpun kājaṙ pratāpa nrĕpati lawan ikaŋ wīṙyya sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ,
ndātan mlecꞓā suputrī n inucapan aṅucap len sakê saŋ narendra,
mogâsuṅsut mĕne n ahyuna kinĕdĕ kĕdö kewalâdoḥ riṅ ambĕk*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

śrī dewîndumatī katon sĕmu ni budđi nira n alalisê nareśwara,
Āpan tan hana raśmi raśmi ni wulat nira pinarĕkakĕn wawaŋ miṅe,
yêkā hetu nira n kinon aṅalihâmwita rumuhun anĕmbahê sira,
mambĕt mađya nirâṅgaluṅgaṅ i panĕmbah ira kadi panĕmbah iŋ tulis*

ry-aṅkat śrī nrĕpaputrikā śrī magađeśwara kawĕlas arĕp kamānuṣan,
mary-âteja sĕpaḥ nirâsĕpa sigit sigitan ira tibâkusêŋ lĕmaḥ,
tan śoƀâkilayū wulat nira sĕkaṙ nira maṅaway awe hanêŋ kapö,
trĕṣṇā kūṅ ira tan katolih inatīta nĕhĕr inilagan yayan tumūt*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

śrī dewîndumatī lumampah aṅĕliḥ prāptê saṅ aṅgāđipa,
ndātan wany-asaƀâhaliŋ haliṅan iŋ ceṭī paḍâkweḥ marĕk,
tan saḥ dyaḥ jayawaspa lot linihaṅan bāhunya karwâwiḍaŋ,
Āpan kāsih irâlawas tuwin arūm tan soṙ dahat riŋ hayu*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

Agyā ŋ budđi saṅ aṅganāŧa ri ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā marê sira,
mojaṙ tan panahânĕkākĕn i lulut lulut ira ri nareśwarātmajā,
ṅke rakryan mapa hetu niŋ kadi wiwal mulat ariris apakṣa maṅsula,
hāḥ wāliṅku tĕkâkisapwana kita n tĕka dumadak adoḥ tĕka ŋ tamuy*

Antĕnku n tuna kapwa siḥta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,
māskw-induŋ ndi wĕkas ni kuŋta palakuṅkwa hurupĕn i lara prih i ṅhulun,
rāganta mwaṅ unĕṅku denya n ahurup tali paṅuwata kiṅkiṅ i ṅhulun,
wet niŋ tan hana sanmatanta palarĕṅkwa karika karaṇanta tan sahuṙ*

dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa piniṇḍa ratnawanitâṅaraṅa karaṇa niŋ lanā lulut,
saŋ kiṅkiŋ ginawe rarâhayu sujanma karaṇa niṅ akuŋ tumon kita,
saŋ rāgānala maṅdadi wwaṅ amanas manasi hati kita n kinonĕṅan,
saŋ rĕs maṅdadi janma rājaduhitâmuhara wĕdi niṅ ahyunê kita*

nāhan de nira mojar aṅrĕṣi hatîniṅĕt iṅĕt apa tan kinahyunan,
heman wīṙyya nira mwaṅ uttama ni kapraƀun ira suyaśâdƀutêŋ jagat,
riŋ rūpâsĕmu rūpa niŋ smara sawaṙgga lawan asana riŋ labuḥ kapat,
tan kewö wiꝑalaprayāsa hana tan pinakadi kadi kambaṅ iŋ caru*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

mantĕn śrī naranāŧa mojar irikā ta dyaḥ sunandâṅucap,
liŋnya dyaḥku harĕp kita wruha ri pāwak niŋ gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat,
nāhan māsku saṅ aṅganāŧa pahawās gĕntĕṙ madadyan ratu,
yogyâtĕmwa lawan kitā kita tĕmaḥ niŋ cātakâmet jawuḥ*

ṅkānê rājya saṅ aṅganāŧa wĕkas iŋ ramyê huwus niŋ laga,
ry-antuk saŋ praƀu maṅlurug saha bala lwiṙ waḥ sakêŋ paṙwwata,
gĕntĕṙ niŋ grit ikaŋ raŧânĕmahakĕn kuŋ ni wwaṅ iŋ kāṙttika,
luḥ niŋ strī kahañaŋ ri līna ni ratunyâṅde paḍĕt niŋ lĕbū*

ndan heman tuna rājalakṣmi satĕwĕknya n rājya niṙdĕwatī,
hetu śrī naranāŧa tan sŧiti pijĕṙ luṅhā madewāśraya,
de niŋ hyūn ira n aṅhyaṅa ŋ nagara moǥa n kewĕhan tan hana,
ṅhiŋ rakryan pakarājalakṣmi nira maṙmmā de nirâṅundaṅa*

rakryan yan hana sanmatanta ri sirânambāna kiṅkiŋ nira,
ndak pinta nya sĕkaṙ tajinta pamahugya mwaŋ sĕrĕḥ riŋ kajaŋ,
taṅgap denta mĕne sĕpaḥ nira katon heman yatan suŋsuṅĕn,
nya ŋ siṅhāsana karwananta pakisapwan māskw-i paṅkwan haji*

nāhan denya n aṅĕdwakĕn nrĕpasutâhyun waspadê saŋ praƀu,
mogâcūm ararĕm wulat nira sinuṅsuŋ riŋ wulat löṙ miṅe,
ndan dūrâhyuna kewalâwĕdi kumöl ambĕk nirâṅdoh arĕs,
yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ mulat iṅ aṙccâṅher iṅ uṅgwan ƀaya*

māliḥ śrîndumatī riniṅriṅ inariḥ de saŋ sunandâmawa,
Āśāƀūta saṅ aṅganāŧa ri layad dewī nĕhĕṙ tan waluy,
de niŋ ƀrānta nirâṅikĕt rasa palambaŋ paṅlipuṙ luḥ pinöm,
ṅkānê watwan ikaŋ salö panulisan maṙmmā rasanyâmanis*

rakryan saŋ maliṅ iŋ matâmatik i rūpaṅkw-âṅĕḍap yan wulat,
kālap denta manaḥku mĕṅgĕp amanis rūpanta duṣṭêŋ hati,
mukṣa twaskw-i sĕḍĕŋta mūṙ syapa ta len saṅkê kitâṅambila,
Eman māsku tuhan tuhan maliṅ atimpuḥ duṙyyaśakṣatriya*

rakryan haywa kita pramāda ri surup niŋ lek mĕne riŋ wĕṅi,
prāptâmora kakanta haywa kita tan yatnā ry-awaktêŋ jinĕm,
sāk niŋ ken awanaṅkwa mañjiṅ i parāhasyanta riŋ pamrĕman,
maṅgā matya matâku pökana kukuṅku n paṅguhā riŋ pupū*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nahan rasa ni de nirâhyun amaliŋ maliṅana ri raras suputrikā,
Agöŋ suꝁa nira n tibā manah i saŋ katuduh arusita pwa riŋ manaḥ,
ri kāpusan ikaŋ smarâpunagi yan waluyana sira de nrĕpātmajā,
lumakwa mapasaŋ pasaŋ wuyaha yan mulih iriṅ iriṅĕn marê dalĕm*

Atīta sira saŋ narendra maṅaraŋ tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,
sinuṇḍaṅ inamĕṙ kininkin aṅĕliḥ rasa tumayuṅa kabwatan raras,
tuwin manah ira n prapañca kumĕtĕṙ hati nira mulat iŋ wwaṅ iŋ saƀā,
baṅun lumaku ri wwat ewĕh alĕyö maṅamĕr amĕr i de nira n laku*

sahaṙṣa saṅ awantināŧa ri ḍatĕŋ saṅ ahayu pinakahyaṅ iŋ saƀā,
hanan pasiḍakĕp hanan pasidĕhâṅurah arih ulah iŋ girahyasĕn,
wah iŋ kapitu tan pahī wĕtu ni rāga nira ri naranāŧaputrikā,
pĕnuḥ maṅarape tĕkêŋ kaka kakânwam atuha sinarambahan lulut*

I maṅkana ni de nira n karakĕtan turida sinaput iŋ manoƀawa,
tan enak aṅinaŋ tan enak aṅucap humĕnĕṅ apĕga ta n sayâwĕnĕs,
sawet i pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,
ya kāraṇa nirâṅucap tan awiraŋ sumĕgĕ sĕgĕh i saŋ nrĕpātmajā*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rakryan ƀāgya kita n ḍatĕŋ nihan aluṅguha yayi ri kisapwan i ṅhulun,
mās lāwan maṇik uttamâṙjja humaḍaŋ pakĕna nika panumbasê kita,
yadyan kapraƀun i ṅhulun suṅakĕnaṅkwa ri kita yayi yan kitâharĕp,
yan praŋ yan kakawin panĕkwa ni kakanta ri kita yayi yan n-apaṅgiha*

yan riŋ kāṙttikamāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕṅ amĕṅ iŋ pasiṙ wukiṙ,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅĕn i ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kakawinku riŋ yaśa,
yan māsâsujimāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕnĕm i rājya niŋ musuḥ,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa ni ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kawaninku riŋ raṇa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

nāhan de naranāŧa mojar araras mambö laṅö niŋ jinĕm,
siṅgiḥ yan pracacaḥ karas waśa ri tuŋtuŋ niŋ tanaḥ riŋ kapö,
siŋ soṅkab ni tutuk nirâwĕtu laṅö kāmīrasâpet manis,
pöḥ niŋ haṙṣa pinöm atūt guru laǥunyâṙjjâṅĕnoḥ lambaṅa*

saŋ katwaŋ niṅ awaṙṇna campaka tumiṅhal sakṣaṇê saŋ praƀu,
ceṣṭākāra nirênariḥ winulatan de saŋ sunandâtaña,
māskw-induŋ mapa budđi rakryan i narendra n swāmya rakryan sira,
yogyâpan kadi mūla tuṅgal apasaḥ maṅke n tĕmaḥ mānuṣa*

<Upendrabajra> 
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

yadin kitâtĕmwa lawan narendra,
ry-awantideśâtiśayêŋ suƀikṣa,
wwaṅ uttama wwaŋnya kawîṅgitajña,
pacaṅkramānanta pasiṙ wukiṙnya*

gunuŋ mahākāla ṅaranya rāmya,
kapunpunan de saṅ awantināŧa,
I pāṙśwā pāṙśwanyā patīṙŧa tīṙŧan,
pĕnuḥ dwijaṙṣy-âjar ajaṙ tan imbā*

saƀā ƀaṭārêśwara nityakāla,
śiwāmƀa sakweḥ ni bañunya śudđa,
kulĕm pwa saŋ hyaŋ tuwi krĕṣṇapakṣa,
yayâpaḍaŋ de nikaṅ aṙdđacandra*

paran tatan rāmya nikā parāna,
pamenanê kāla nikaŋ basanta,
Ikaŋ larâgöŋ mala niŋ śarīra,
Awās hilaŋ māry-aṅaweśa denya*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

tāman saŋ nāŧa tan popama halĕp ika sāmpun prakāśâdwitīya,
piṅgiṙ niŋ lwaḥ srĕp ātis ny-aṅin ika humaras ganđa niŋ paṅkaja mrik,
sākṣāt swaṙggātmakâpan sahana hana nikaŋ kĕmbaṅ aṅjraḥ paḍârūm,
heman yan lena saṅkê kita śaraṇa ni kādewatanya n pinūjā*

nāhan de saŋ sunandâmirĕsĕpakĕn i saŋ yogya kaṙmmā sudewī,
ndān ambĕk śrī suputrī miṅay atimĕs adoḥ tan hana ŋ rāga mātra,
sāmpun wruḥ saŋ sunandā karaṇa nika n akon muṅsirê saŋ pratīpa,
Asrĕt lampaḥ nirâlon laku laku jaladânūtakĕn mārutâlon*

ndan saŋ kāry-âṅaraŋ sis kawĕlas arĕp irâmeri luḥ tan tinoliḥ,
baṙyyan tiṅhal ri dewī sira rasa pĕjahâpan rĕmĕk twas nira syuḥ,
limbe limbe sudewī kadi maṅaway akon milwa ri śrī narendra,
wet niŋ ƀrāntâṅikĕt ƀāṣa ri saruṅan ikaŋ patrĕm aṅrĕs rasanya*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

ṅhulun yaśana rāga māsku pakađaṙmman ĕnahana raras niṅ aṅrĕṅiḥ,
hayunta makawāṇḍiranya ya paṅöbana para paranaṅkwa yan rimaŋ,
prasĕnta ri dalĕm jinĕm titisananta luh i lukar i kenta riŋ tilam,
susunta pakasāđananta kalawan pipi katiga tĕṅaḥ maran lĕpas*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

nāhan de śrī narendrânĕmahakĕn i lulut kuŋ nirâwak wilāpa,
yêkī tan saḥ ri paṅkwan winaca tiniliṅan koŋ rinĕṅwan winaswās,
Adrĕs luḥ śrī narendrâṅrasani rasa nikâpan katuhwan rasanya,
yogyâṅantyêŋ mahantĕn wacan iṅ alaradan kālapan ratnakanyā*

rakryan putrī huwus mālih asĕmu paṅaliḥ niŋ sĕkaṙ sālas aṅjraḥ,
kweḥ niŋ guṇḍik nira mwaŋ kaka kaka rumarâṅasturi mrik waṅinya,
lagy-âtaṅkis humuŋ hambuluṅan i tali kenyânamaṙ ṣaṭpada strī,
haṙṣâmbĕk saŋ pratīpâmapag iṅ ujar arūm tustus iŋ laṅwa laṅwan*

<krĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏓ = 20

Ibu t asy-asiḥ kita kadaŋ kadaṅa ri sĕḍĕṅ i ṅhulun rimaŋ,
kita yogya mitra kulabanđw-amarasana ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
pakawaṙgga ni ṅhulun i paṅkwan asisihana raśmi niŋ prĕman,
Arĕnaḥ manahkw-aṅaku sānak iri kita patĕmwan iŋ jaja*

pakĕnaṅkwa yan marĕk i māskw-amibikana laṭinta riŋ waja,
lumut iŋ payođara huwus kakiṅan usapanaṅkwa riŋ jaja,
Iruṅ i ṅhulun panutulaṅkwa luh i pipi ri pamrih iŋ sipat,
lukar iŋ tapiḥ salinanaṅkwa karatala mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

ndaḥ yêki n liŋ narendrârasa mijila sakêŋ ƀāṣa lāwan palambaŋ,
sotan ta ŋ sāri niŋ rāga piturun i laṅö niŋ kawi ƀrāntacitta,
tan paṅgintiṙ manis niŋ tĕbu sawukir apan tan patuŋtuŋ manisnya,
maṙmmânyuḥ prāṇa rūmnyâsĕmu paṅucapan iŋ wahw-amaṅkw-âṅdudut ken*

rakryan putrī mulat riŋ nrĕpati kadi wulat niŋ ṭikā riŋ wilāpa,
mojaṙ ta dyaḥ sunandā wwaya ta sira siwin śakty-asaṅjñā pratīpa,
sākṣāt swaṙggânurun rūpa ni nagara nira ry-ânupa ꝁyāti riŋ rāt,
kumbaŋ kĕmbaŋ papaṅgiḥta kadi patĕmu niŋ kāṙttika mwaŋ basanta*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saṅ aṙjjuna sahasrabāhu riṅ usāna sira siniwi śakti nītimān,
prakāśa sira saŋ daśānana musuḥ nira huwus ayaśâmatī musuḥ,
taŧāpi kaparājayêŋ raṇa huwus hinuripan alawas pinañjara,
hana pwa sira saŋ pratīpa sira rakwa wĕka nira suśīla digjaya*

paran pwa wĕkas uṅsirĕnta paḍa wastu kita wĕka niṅ uttamapraƀu,
para praƀu kapan paḍâsira lawan sira tĕwas amilĕt milĕt wulat,
Ameta kita len muwaḥ tĕwas aṅel midĕr ibu kapana n pamaṅgiha,
mataŋnya sira sĕṅgahĕnta kaka yogya sira manuwalêṅ ujaṙ yayi*

<śiꝁariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ = 17

yadin sidđā rakryan sasisihana rūm niŋ silih asiḥ,
Awās rakryan glānâhuyaṅ apupul i jro pakasutan,
hana lwaḥ ramyâlwā prakaśita si rewā ṅaran ika,
kitâdyūsa ṅkānêsuh isuhana lāwan saṅ ahulun*

raras niŋ karwa swāmi paran ika rakwâṅlĕwihana,
marā riŋ tāman tan hana marĕka līlā ṅwaṅ aṅĕnĕs,
yadin madyūsêŋ lwaḥ talaga wulakan śūnya kasĕnĕt,
wĕnaŋ sāmbĕk niŋ swāmi tariman apan tan hana mulat*

kalīṅanyâlaḥ māsku marĕka nihan dak parĕkakĕn,
paran maṙmmantâsuṅsut arĕṅu miṅe tan pamituhu,
paṅantî paṅkwan saŋ praƀu hila hila ŋ duḥka siwuhĕn,
Apan māskw-âpet pet hayu pahayu budđinta ri sira*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandâmirĕsĕpakĕn i tiṅkaḥ narāṙyya pratīpa,
paŧya wruḥ sopapattîṅgita nikaṅ ucap akrĕp kĕna priḥ narendra,
yâṅde tan saṅśayê twas nira ri ḍatĕṅa rakryan suputrî kisapwan,
kady-aṅhyaŋ motusan wallaƀa mamagĕhakĕn tan wuruŋ niŋ swakāṙyya*

rakryan putrī miṅe tan wawarĕṅĕh apa tan trĕpti rakwê narendra,
saŋ nāŧa wruḥ sira n tan kinaharĕpan ikaŋ budđi maṅkin prapañca,
Āśāƀūtânulis ketaka rasa kakawin pöḥ nikaŋ rāga tībra,
tambā niŋ keraṅan tan winadal i liḍah iŋ kāma nāhan rasanya*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

Ibu tan paꝑala pwa ṅ amalar i hayunta sĕḍĕŋta rare,
syapa māsku kadi ṅhulun aṅurati rāga lawan turida,
katunan lĕpihan kita kinirimakĕnku karaskw-i kita,
tĕka riŋ kararan pwa kita mapa tiki n sahajâpi lupa*

sĕḍĕṅ iŋ pabĕlaḥ turida kinĕkĕsanku kitêŋ lĕpihan,
makasāđana kuṅkw-aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i rūmta lanā n pinalaṙ,
Aṅadĕg pwa kitêŋ puḍak araras inastwakĕn iŋ ƀramara,
winaliṅku kitâŋ liṅa puji puji yan ratu niŋ kusuma*

saṅ apiṇḍa wukiṙ ṅhulun ajar ajarê kita muṅgwa sadā,
tarukāṅkw-i hayunta pamiṣayana rāga sĕḍĕṅkw-alulut,
licinêŋ śayanâkw-anusupa ri hulĕsta suganđa miṅiŋ,
sipi māsku suꝁaṅku katuruna ri sor i tĕṅaḥta rari*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

nāhan de śrī narendrâkakawina maṅani twas nirê jro drawâṅras,
ndātan tiṅhal muwaḥ riŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā kewalêraŋ tumuṅkul,
māry-âśāƀūta sāmpun pinĕgat ira lulut kuŋ nirê śrī suputrī,
hetunya n tan wijil luḥ nira pamaḍĕm irêŋ rāgabahnî dalĕm twas*

sāmpun māliḥ sudewī kasusu laku nirâṅĕñcuh ĕñcuḥ kaṅelan,
ndan tiṅhal saŋ susenâṅiriṅakĕn aṅamĕṙ tan wĕnaŋ sāh amaṇḍĕŋ,
kady-âdandan kisapwan yan alihan asilâhyūn amaṅkwê sudewī,
haṙṣâgyā gyān anuṅsuŋ riṅ ujar akakawin lwiṙ katonêŋ palambaŋ*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rakryan saŋ pinunagyakĕnku śaraṇāśraya tumuluṅa kiṅkiṅ i ṅhulun,
Aṅlū māsku kisapwan i ṅhulun aluṅguha kita yayi haywa saṅśaya,
t asy-âsiḥ kita māsihê kawi guṇaṅku palar amalĕsêŋ karāsikan,
lambā kapraƀun i ṅhulun kita rumaṅkĕpana saꝑala yogya tuṅgalĕn*

maṅke n prāpta ni māsku tambay iṅ anon wwaṅ ahayu kadi dewakanyakā,
yan riŋ śūnya katĕmwananta saha ƀūṣaṇa maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
byaktânĕṅgaha dewatī kalĕmahan ṅhulun iri kita dūra saṅśayā,
Āpan de ni hayunta yogya kita māsku panadinakĕna n pinaṅkwakĕn*

paṅkwankw-îbu paranti niŋ wwaṅ anukĕṙ nukĕr aṅĕsah ĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
śīṙṇna syuḥ lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun pinakarantunan i kuku niṅ epu tan panūt,
tan pamwas jaja ni ṅhulun wahu waras linawad i panĕpak niṅ aṅrĕṅiḥ,
lagy-emö pipi ni ṅhulun saƀa saƀā ni waja niṅ anulak wineḥ sĕpaḥ*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

sojaṙ saŋ nāŧa kady-âṅalapana kasusuk niŋ kĕnêŋ rāgapāśa,
kady-ânambāna kiṅkiŋ niṅ amalaku suwal kewĕhan kāladeśa,
sākṣāt sambat niṅ onĕŋ kinirimakĕn apet pet manis de ni kuŋnya,
mambö rūm niŋ katurwan winuṅu ni jarumanyânĕkākĕn wilāpa*

tatkāla śrī suputrī sapawulatan aṅantî harĕp saŋ susenā,
tan kantun saŋ sunandā marĕk ataña tĕhĕṙ sopacārâtalaṅkup,
rakryan sāmpun kita wruḥ ri narapati mapâmbĕkta māsku n patĕmwa,
Āpan saŋ nāŧa sākṣāt madana midĕr amet hyaŋ ratī riŋ kaḍatwan*

yadyastun māsku sidđâṅhaturakĕna hayuntêŋ kisapwan narendra,
ṅkānêŋ gĕṅgā kitâmena mahas ahasa riŋ nūsa śūnyê tĕṅaḥnya,
mwaŋ yan rakryan marêŋ wrĕndawana taman irânopamêŋ laṅwa laṅwan,
Akweḥ ƀuktinta ramyâmarĕkana yamunā lālanâkuwwa kuwwa*

rakryan putrī tan eṅĕḥ sira kinĕdĕ kĕdö yan paniwyê narendra,
siṅgiḥ rakwa n rarā suṇṭi masĕmu lĕṅa suṇṭy-âkalis de nirâmbĕk,
ndan budđi śrī susenā kadi pulut atĕguḥ tan lumeṙ de nirâhyun,
saŋkṣepanya ndi tan sidđa kapalikĕtana śrī suputrî narendra*

luṅhā lampaḥ sudewī narapati kawĕkas keraṅan tan tinoliḥ,
kady-agriŋ nora rakwâṅinaki laṅu laṅun yan mulat riŋ sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,
rakryan putrī jugânuṅgayap i hati nirâtyanta riŋ priṅga wiṣṭi,
maṅkin ƀrāntâṅikĕt ƀāṣa panalimur irê tībra niŋ rāga tikṣṇa*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

dyaḥ maḥ luṅsuran i ṅhulun pasuṅa ni ṅhulun iri kita māsku taṅgapĕn,
siñjaŋ siñjaṅa rakryan iŋ paṅaraṅan ri huwus iṅ anulis pralāpita,
göŋ ny-âsiḥku ri māsku yogya suwalĕn ṅhulun amalaku luṅsuran tapiḥ,
donyêbū pinakātmarakṣa n amĕrĕnkw-abasahana tĕhĕṙ pamera luḥ*

rakryan saŋ hinarĕp harĕpku śaraṇāśraya mulata ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
tan sênuṅsir adoḥ manaḥta salawasku tĕka ri kita moǥa tan liniŋ,
ṅhiŋ gānyā hana kāsihanta ḍatu ḍatwa kahulunana tan sahê kita,
yêkī pañjiṅanaṅkwa nitya saparan ṅhulun aṅucap ucap lawan kita*

nāhan ƀāṣa nira n tiniṅgalakĕn iŋ paṅaraṅan i layat suputrikā,
mantĕn duḥka nirâsamun turida rāga ni manah ira tan tinūtakĕn,
śrī hemāṅgada kabwatan kuṅ i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā marê sira,
wwāgan moǥa gumanty-amukti lara rāga niyata sira tan kinahyunan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

śrī dewîndumatī ḍatĕŋ sira ri saŋ sāmpun kaciry-an smara,
Ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp harĕp nira lawan tan hyūn irê saŋ praƀu,
ndān eman wĕkasan kataṙkkan i kalis ny-ambĕk nira n tan rimaŋ,
Aṅhiŋ piŋ rwa mulat kapiŋ rwa sahajâtuŋtuŋ tikĕl niŋ halis*

sāmpun waspada doh i rāga nira tan tuṅgal panononana,
suṅsut suṅsut ira n kinon marĕka len tiṅhal nirâṅrĕṅwani,
Ākārêṅgita niŋ manaḥ saha wijil niŋ śabda norâkadi,
Ahyun kawruhana n tan ahyun ika kaprajñān irâpet wiwal*

tan wruḥ śrī naranāŧa yan tan aharĕp rakryan suputrî sira,
Aṅgĕṅgöŋ kamadan trĕṇāṅkura hiḍĕp saŋ nāŧa riŋ wwaŋ kabeḥ,
hamham paṙccaya de ni rūpa nira tĕkwan śakti wānîŋ raṇa,
kĕdw-âkuŋ makasoŋ larônĕṅ ira yan pojaṙ waśâkon marā*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saŋ sākṣāt smarakanyakā saṅ anarīra ri hati saṅ amiṇḍa riŋ hiḍĕp,
budđiṅkw-âlal aṅantyakĕn siha ni māskw-ahuyaṅ ajaruman pralāpita,
maṅke pwā tĕka tan wawaŋ marĕk awaṙṇna kĕna guṇa miṅe kitâriris,
rakryan haywa kakanta māsku sinaranta kalalah ibu rāga ni ṅhulun*

saṇḍaŋ ƀakta samotusankw-apuyĕṅ an layat alisuh amet rarâhayu,
ndātan polih aṅel aṅulwan aṅawetan aṅidĕri kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ,
maṅke pwa n hana māskw-arūm pakawayaŋ wayaṅĕn amĕrĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,
tan pātmā rasa kaprĕman saśayanânĕkĕnakĕna śarīra ni ṅhulun*

nāhan de naranāŧa mojar awuyuŋ sira wĕkasan adoḥ suputrikā,
śrī putrī katibān ujaṙ haji tan eṅĕh apuji sira yan tuhan tuhan,
Ājñālaṅǥana yogya daṇḍan apa tan hana sahur ira pakṣa māliha,
simbantĕn haji molihâmiđi balik sira kawiđi dinaṇḍa niŋ smara*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

sakweḥ saŋ marĕk uttamottama wiwal munduṙ paḍâmid miṅe,
Aṅheman ri narendra yan sira tan antuk śrī suputrī mulat,
mwaŋ strī strī paricārikā paḍa humuŋ maṅyogyanî saŋ praƀu,
ḍyam têkî wĕkasan tuhun hana mulat yan saŋ sunandâṅucap*

rakryan tiṅhalanâtpada nrĕpati sākṣāt ṣaṭpadâmet sĕkaṙ,
maṅheṙ her i dalĕm taman makapaṅanty-antyan kucup niŋ mĕnuṙ,
maṅke n mūr aṅaliḥ cumuṇḍuk i widaṙbƀâpakṣa tan mantuka,
Āpan maṙmma nira n ḍatĕŋ kita karĕṅw-an paṅjrah iŋ campaka*

śrī hemāṅgada laṅwa laṅwan asana ndātan mĕkaṙ kābunan,
saṅsāra kṣaya saṅsayâluru lume de niŋ smarāꝁyâpanas,
heman māsku kucup ni budđi nira yan tan sanmatan kāsihan,
ṅhiŋ gānya n mĕkara n kitâṅlawada māskw-âpan gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat*

wwantĕn rājya nirê kaliṅga kita yogya hyaŋ hyaṅanyâhalĕp,
tĕkwan paṙśśwa nikaŋ mahendragiri hetunya n kadîndrālaya,
gĕntĕṙ ny-ampuhan iŋ mahodađi karĕṅw-âgĕnturan tan pĕgat,
Aṅhiŋ donya mamuṅwa saŋ praƀu lawan māsku n katurwān apöm*

rakryan tan kasasaṙ hayunta kawawê saŋ nāŧa hemāṅgada,
Āpan budđi nirâbĕnĕṙ tan arusit wruḥ ry-ambĕk iŋ dug rimaŋ,
hĕnwanta n marĕkê kisapwan ira kewalya ṅhulun tan saha,
yêkī don i manĕḥta mājara ri māṙgganta n suꝁâsaṅgama*

Aṅhiŋ yogya siwinta tan patatalan trus tuñjuṅ iŋ kapraƀun,
prajñā wany-anulus bisâṅaji đanurwedâđika wruḥ nira,
yan riŋ kīṙtty-aniwāṙyya śudđa hana soṙ niŋ candrawimbâkucĕm,
tustus niŋ ratu śakti digjaya sĕkaṙ tajy-aṅkuran kṣatriya*

nāhan de niṅ amet manis niṅ aṅucap mambö juruḥ kābunan,
Antuk niŋ maṅalap manis ni kakawin saŋ wrĕḍđa wrĕdđîŋ laṅö,
ndātan paṅgarit aṙdđa tan rĕsĕp i budđi śrī narendrātmajā,
luṅhā wruḥ tumuluy sira n kinĕḍapan de saŋ sunandâṅaliḥ*

śrī hemāṅgada kāri keraṅan akiṅkiŋ tan wĕnaŋ sāhasa,
maṅgâmora makilya kilyana tumūtê śrī narendrātmajā,
saŋ hyaŋ manmaŧa duṣṭa tan rwa tĕlu pat rowaŋ nirâśâlara,
yêkī hetu nirâṅikĕt rasa wilāpâṅras rasanyê hati*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

maṅko pwântĕnku dentâmbĕk atiśaya dahat kewalâṅgöŋ kaputryan,
budđintâpyak madêŋ haṙṣa tan akuṅ iṅ akuŋ saṅsayâpy-âwalepa,
dentâweḥ rāga tan popama kadi ginawe lĕŋlĕŋâku n tumiṅhal,
māyā muṅgw-iŋ crĕmin lwiṙtta riṅ apa wĕnaṅaṅkwâṅisapwê tuwuḥta*

saŋ lwīr aṙccâṅaraŋ byakta pan ulaha ni māskw-i ṅhulun yan pamaṅkwa,
saŋ lwiṙ dewî tulis tan wuruṅa kasarikâku n marê pamrĕmanta,
saŋ lwiṙ wwe niŋ samudrâṅaraṅakĕn i manaḥku n surud siḥta māsku,
saŋ tuŋtuŋ ni rwi niŋ ketaka kari kacarik twaskw-i luṅhānta maṅko*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

nāhan manis ni paṅikĕt nira rāgacihna,
śrĕṅgāra rāsika pinöm atĕmaḥ wilāpa,
muṅgw-î dalĕm hati ginūḋa raras rarasnya,
pinrāṙŧanākĕn ira mĕtwa mĕne n papaṅgiḥ*

saŋ lwiṙ hyaṅ iŋ jalada kāṅinan iŋ basanta,
ndātan panis nisi huyaŋ ni manaḥ niṅ onĕŋ,
luṅhā lawan riris i budđi nirê narendra,
saŋ nāŧa kāri tĕlĕs i drĕs i luḥ nirâṅdyus*

byātīta saŋ praƀu narendrasutā wiwakṣan,
dolāyamāna ri turuŋ ni manaḥ nirêsi,
luṅhâmiliḥ milih i jalwa nirê narendra,
himpĕṙ sĕkaṙ midĕr amet ƀramarê kuwuŋnya*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ sira ri sanmuꝁa saŋ narendra,
śrī pāṇḍya haṙṣa kadi tan rāt ira n tumiṅhal,
runtuḥ lĕbuṙ manah irâsĕmu rāgabahni,
lwiṙ mās hanêŋ muṣa wawaŋ drawa de niṅ apwī*

saŋ pāṇḍya siṅhapuruṣākrĕti rāgaśatru,
śrī putrikâciri wĕdi n para riŋ paḍöman,
söḥ budđi sattwa naranāŧa paḍâwrĕg awri,
keṇḍit manaḥ nira lawan kuṅ irê dalĕm twas*

sāmpun pĕtĕŋ twas ira söḥ turidâṅaweśa,
Aṅhiŋ hineṙ silih asiḥ naranāŧaputrī,
Āpan katon muꝁa nirâsĕmu śītaraśmi,
yêkī nimitta nira mojar amanwa manwa*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

ṅke siṅhāsana māskw-aluṅguha paran karaṇa niṅ aṅadĕg baṅun wiwal,
rākantâlawas aṅrĕṅö ri hayu rakryan ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun ḍatĕŋ,
tĕkwan śrī naranāŧa ƀoja maṅutus ḍatĕṅa ri sĕḍĕṅ iŋ swayambara,
nāhan taŋ karas esi ƀāṣa pahulaṅkwa ri kita yayi hantusākĕna*

wruḥ ku n tan paṅĕnoha kuṅku ri kitâpan ahayu sakadaŋ lawan ratiḥ,
tuṅgal rakwa rarasta riŋ muꝁa lawan rĕsĕp i raras i māsku riŋ pupū,
rāgaṅkw-îbu hanêŋ tĕṅaḥta kapipis lara turida kinölwa riŋ susu,
lampūn kaprĕma riŋ pasaṅgaman i paṅhapit i wĕtis i māsku ri ṅhulun*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

sojaṙ narāđipati tan palawan manisnya,
maṅgiṣṭa śiṣṭa mari śiṣṭa sinorakĕnya,
lwiṙ tan mađu ŋ mađu tinaṇḍiṅakĕn yayān soṙ,
lambā manis manis ikaŋ gula tan panaṅkĕp*

śrī putrikā sira mulat ri harĕp narendra,
ndātan kapūhan apa tan hana paṅgaritnya,
mogâkalis manah irâsĕmu tan panaṅgĕl,
kady-adwa tiṅhal ira kewala tan papiṅrwa*

do doh i budđi nira niścaya saŋ sunandā,
śrī pāṇḍya tiṅhal ira kady-aṅutus maṅĕdwa,
ndan saŋ kinon ira bisâṅupacāra śabda,
mojaṙ tuhun pali palin ya tĕkapnya mojaṙ*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nāhan śrī naranāŧa pāṇḍya sira yogya paṅayatan i māsku riŋ hayu,
heman rūmta yatan pagĕgwan i manis manis ira n aṅisapw-aṅolakĕn,
Aṅhiŋ samƀawa rakwaṅöbana huyaŋta saꝑala parĕkĕnta riŋ tilam,
siŋ sojaṙ haji yan rahasya rasan iŋ śayana kĕmitananta cupwana*

yadyastun kita māsku n âmĕṅ amĕṅêŋ tuha rawa kalawan nareśwara,
byaktânaṅśaya cakrawāka dadi mānuṣa maṭika ṭikan mariŋ ḍarat,
mwaŋ yan karwa narendra māsku mahasêŋ pasisi mĕgila riŋ wwaṅ iŋ pasiṙ,
byaktânĕṅgaha dèwa niŋ miŧuna rāśi mĕtu harĕp ahimya himyana*

Atyantêŋ kalaṅön lĕyĕp winulatan patĕmu ni lĕṅĕṅ iŋ pasiṙ wukiṙ,
ndan dūrâmaḍanê laṅö ni patĕmunta matĕmu kalawan nareśwara,
yadyāpin paḍa riŋ laṅö pisaniṅū kadi rarasa ni māskw-asaṅgama,
ṅhiŋ gānyâmaḍanê rarasta raras iŋ rati madana n akālihan hulĕs*

<mālinī> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 15

nahan ucapan ikâpet pet manis tan pamandi,
kadi rĕsĕpa rasanyê budđi rakryan suputrī,
kunaṅ apa tan ikâṅde haṙṣa riŋ haṙṣa niŋ len,
wiꝑala kadi manis niŋ twak yan iŋ madyasakta*

narapatitanayâṅliḥ tan sahuṙ lwiṙ tulis mās,
rĕṅu nira paṅadeśan yan tan aṅgâmituhwa,
kalalu laku nirâṅdoḥ mūṙ lawan saŋ sunandā,
nrĕpati kawĕkas ākuŋ śīǥra māwak wilāpa*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rakryan saŋ kĕna rāga tībra kaka rakryan aṅuwatana haywa saṅśaya,
hrū saŋ hyaŋ madanê hatinta dahutĕṅkwa bĕbĕdĕn i taṅanku hĕmbana,
ṅhiŋ jampyanta karāsikanku n amĕkul garĕgĕtĕn amijĕt mijĕt susu,
romantâjumĕn i ṅhulun sadakanaṅkwa n anĕsĕpi laṭinta riŋ tilam*

kocap māsku wicakṣaṇôṇḍahagi yogya panagara bisâmaṅun lulut,
ṅke ta dyaḥ mata ni ṅhulun sipatananta pĕnĕdĕn usapanta riŋ pusuḥ,
yan kālanta pinaṅkwakĕn wwaya jajaṅku rari siku sikunta yan cala,
kuŋta mwaŋ turidaṅku pādwakĕna māsku patitisana luḥ maran rapĕt*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nahan tĕmahan iŋ prapañca ni manaḥ nrĕpati wahu lipuṙ linaṅwakĕn,
hanâmbĕk ira mantukâmruda tuhun mawaraha rumuhun ri saŋ praƀu,
katon ujara niŋ mulat ri sira tan pamahayu kadi budđi niŋ rare,
ya hetu nira tan wawaŋ mulih aṅantyakĕn i huwusa niŋ swayambara*

byatīta ri sĕḍĕŋ nira n mari rimaŋ tucapa sahana niŋ wwaṅ iŋ saƀā,
manaḥnya paḍa pakṣapāta ri narendrasuta tan aharĕp ri saŋ praƀu,
paḍâsraṅ aṅucap ry-uliḥ nrĕpasutā wruh i harĕpa nirêri saŋ haja,
Alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liṅ ikanâṅgĕtĕm asahuran atry-aṅadwakĕn*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rāga śrī naranāŧaputra masĕwö kadi kayu ragas iŋ labuḥ kapat,
Osik budđi nirê ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasutā winaliṅ ira tĕkâkisapwana,
Agyâweha sĕpaḥ sakê waja siliḥ suwala guyu panaṙkka niŋ mulat,
bwat śrĕṅgāra dahat panāntwa nira maṙmma rasa nika rĕsĕp rinĕṅwakĕn*

ṅke rakryan pakisapwan onĕṅ alawas ṅhulun ibu saṅ apiṇḍa nīrada,
saŋ saṅhub ni lulutku saŋ patĕr i kuṅku kilat i pĕtĕṅ i twas i ṅhulun,
saŋ rĕm niŋ turidâṅalaḥ sih apuput huyaṅ amĕkasakĕn putĕk hati,
saŋ truḥ truḥ ni laṅöṅku mukṣa hiniḍĕp kinisapu sahajâtĕmaḥ riris*

donkw-aṅlitlita roma rakryan anapak napaka hayu ni māsku riŋ tilam,
Āpan tan hana len pramāṇa ri rarasta n aṅaraṅ aṅisapwakĕn puḍak,
māskw-induŋ huniṅan ṅhulun ri manis iŋ mata sarasija kābunan mađu,
suŋsuŋ rāga tĕṅaḥ puriḥta kalawan pipi taḍaha ni luḥta pintanĕn*

paṅkwankw-îbu wĕtĕḥ turuŋ pinakapaṅrĕṅihan iṅ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
tapwan kāni lĕṅĕnku de ni kuku niŋ hinari hari miṅe kinolakĕn,
mwaŋ tapwan katĕpak jajaṅku kalawan pipi tĕkap iṅ arĕs kinewala,
ṅhiŋ rakryan karaṇanya n emwa ragĕta mwaṅ anuluṅa manĕmbu nĕmbura*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 20

ṅke saṅ apiṇḍa nirātmaka tinĕmahakĕn maṇi rājasutā,
tan hana ṅūni dĕlāha kadi kita sujanma suśīla wagĕd,
saŋ dadi janma sakêŋ taya taya kadi rakryan arūm anulus,
māsku śaśāṅkawimāna karika kita maṅdadi maṙmma dahat*

Aṅgriṅi simbali rakryan amarasana moǥa tĕkâṅlarani,
dyaḥku nihan tuluṅĕn ṅhulun uwatana kāraṇa niŋ warasa,
griŋ kĕna rāga laraṅkw-aṅinak inaki mĕṅgĕp atīs apanas,
māsku mataŋ yan akaṙ pipi guliga tĕṅaḥ palakun ri kita*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nāhan de saṅ ajâṅucap mĕtu raras ni kataruṇan irâṅhiḍĕp smara,
mambö turwan i paṅkwan aṅharas i paṅlawad iṅ ahayu riŋ pasaṅgaman,
kady-aṅrĕṅwa rĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsah iŋ kinisapu rasa niŋ wwaṅ aṅrĕṅö,
śrī dewîndumatī pwa muṣṭi niṅ akuŋ kapana sira n aṅiṣṭya mintara*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

Ujaṙ saṅ aja waṙṇna waṙṣa tumibânĕkarakĕn asanâṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
Aśoka ḍinĕḍĕṙ sawaŋ nrĕpasutā wahu kasiram alūṅ apādapa,
wawaŋ sĕkar irânĕḍĕŋ ƀramara tan hana wani mara kewalâtilaṙ,
Apan saṅ aja rakwa tan wuruṅ aṅol aṅarĕkana mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*

narendratanayâwĕnĕs mulat i rūpa saṅ aja wawaṅ agriṅ aṅlayuŋ,
kasambĕt i manis manis ni luṅid iŋ mata sarasija keṅgutan halis,
huwus wruh i manis nira n kasarik iŋ lituhayu suƀagêŋ swayĕmbara,
ya kāraṇa nirâharĕp marĕka paṅkun uwat uwatanêŋ sĕpaḥ sarik*

sawet ni pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,
tinaṙkka nira rājaputra dadi niŋ smara saṅ aja marêŋ swayĕmbara,
muwaḥ saṅ aja saṅsayânaha nahā mulat i hayu narendraputrikā,
ratiḥ karika sinwayĕmbarakĕn iŋ madananagara liŋ nirê hati*

sipat nrĕpasutā lutuṙ kadi humer i paṅusapa nareśwarātmaja,
gĕluŋ nira baṅun harĕp suruyanê jariji nrĕpatiputra yan lukaṙ,
Aṅrĕs kadi harĕp kadĕmwanana de saṅ aja mata nirâṅdadak lumuḥ,
paniṅsĕt i tapiḥ nirâsĕmu harĕp lukarana ni taṅan nrĕpātmaja*

waja nrĕpatiputra kātara rarasnya tĕka ta mamusuḥ yan iŋ laṭi,
Alal kĕtĕ kĕtĕg nirêŋ jaja lumiṇḍihana jaja narendraputrikā,
Asaṅgraha naꝁâluṅid taṅan irâmirah aharĕp adun lawan susu,
tĕkêruṅ ira tan pakāla kumĕsut sĕmu sĕmu niṅ asĕṅhit iŋ pipi*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan sah i narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
lāwan dyaḥ jayawaspa kāsih ika tan sah i pada naranāŧaputrikā,
ndan rakwênalapan sĕḍĕŋnya n ahañaŋ tinut ika mapasaḥ madum tuhan,
tĕmbenya n sapatiṅhalan paḍa lumuḥ kawĕlas arĕp aluŋluṅan taṅis*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa mājar i narendratanaya nĕhĕr aṅhĕmū taṅis,
rakryan honya manĕḥta tiṅhalana pun marika makaṅaran mađūdakā,
pun muṅgw-î hiriṅan marĕk linihaṅan wagĕd araras amaṅku pawwahan,
Aṅhiŋ pun juga tan wĕnaŋ mulat awaṙṇna lara mata n aṅölakĕn taṅis*

yadyastun nrĕpaputrikā mara mĕne humaturakĕna rūm nirê kita,
rakryan tan wĕnaṅ edihê sira yadin sira tumĕṅĕta pun mađūdakā,
dūra n đāraka riŋ lara smara manĕḥta pinasahakĕn iŋ tuhan tuhan,
ṅhiŋ maty-âṅaraṅê daganta bapa tan panĕmu kahulunan sadā marĕk*

mwaŋ yan śrîndumatī tan aptya ri tuhanku muliha sira tan panoliha,
suṅsut śrī naranāŧa rakwa ri manĕḥta bapa maṅulanĕḥ turuŋ lipuṙ,
byaktâṅgĕgwana sĕmpalĕn manĕḥta bāpa kita tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn,
mātîŋ māti kināladeśa kadi kambaṅ iṅ asana sinĕmpal iŋ kapat*

nāhan liŋnya nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul anaṅis tucapa ta panaṅis mađūdakā,
hāḥ rakryan kadi riŋ paṅipyan ahurip takari manĕ manĕḥta tiṅhali,
nāhan pun mađusūdanâmwaṅi narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
kĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕṅ i luḥ nipun marahakĕn sih ipun arabi tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ*

maṅke ry-antuk ipun tumūt ri naranāŧatanaya baṅun aṅhuwus huwus,
tan lot ṅgānya pun aṅhiḍĕp turida rāga kadi wuruṅa matya monĕṅa,
yêkā hetu nipun tĕkâhañutan aṅlalu pĕjahana de nareśwara,
Aṅhiŋ luḥ ni manĕḥta kahyuna nipun rurubakĕna lawan ṅrĕs iŋ taṅis*

Ājñā śrī naranāŧa ṅūni ḍumawuḥ ri para panĕpi riŋ pasiṙ wukiṙ,
An pun patyana tūt tlasĕn haḍaṅĕn iŋ hawan i hawan ipun marêŋ musuḥ,
maṅke n tan hana patya patyana sadoṣa nipun i sĕḍĕṅ iŋ swayambara,
pun ṅgānyêka dumeḥ pun ahyuna mulat mulata juga sawet ny-unĕŋ nipun*

hāḥ rakryan siha rakryan iŋ manĕ manĕḥ ṅhulun ibu pituhun ṅhulun tuhan,
nāhan śrī naranāŧaputra pakisapwan ibu ri sira haywa tâwihaŋ,
Āpan yan tuna kūṅ i māsku ri sirâpa ta hamĕṅana ni ṅhulun mĕne,
tan wanđyā mati karwa pun mađu manĕḥta tuhan i huwus iŋ swayambara*

maṙmmā de jayawaspa mojar ataṅis tĕka hirĕṅ i narendrakanyakā,
pantĕs pantĕs apolahan marĕk atakwan i manah ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,
siŋ solaḥnya wagĕd hanan pamisusal misusal api calâṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,
kĕdw-âkon marĕkâkisapwana nĕhĕṙ mulat arĕṅu waśâṅdĕlö mata*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>

sāmpun dyaḥ jayawaspa mojar irikā ta dyaḥ sunandâṅucap,
rakryan tiṅhalananta māsku saṅ ajâtyantêŋ halĕp riŋ saƀā,

śudđakṣatriya sūṙyyawaṅśa taruṇâṅhiŋ śakti maṅke n raray*

waswāsĕnta halĕp nirâṅdaśaguṇê rūm niŋ tulis mās tatuṙ,

Aṅhiŋ ketaka lot pinaṅkwakĕn ira n lwiṙnya n wĕtistâlaris*

yogyâmaṅkwa ri māskw-apan paḍa lawan dewī ratiḥ riŋ hayu*

rakryan tan sasiwinta māsku sira de ni karakĕtan irâṅurĕn laṅö,

Aṅlampū saṅ ajânahĕn turida māry-amalar i harĕpā suputrikā,

paḍa mamaluyakĕn mās lāwan wastra pamisalin,
saha manis iṅ ujaṙ ndan liśya n pawwata pahula,
mulih i huwus irâmwit duḥkâsĕṅhit i saṅ aja*

muwah ucapakĕna śrī putrī mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya,
saṅ amaraṅ i sira strī strī wrĕdđā pitu ṅ abuyut,
tuwi kadaṅ ira tan len riŋ sajñâhayu manulus,
Atuha tuha tinuṅgal sakweḥ niŋ marĕk i sira*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

bwat kāmeśwara ratna nīla winaṅun grĕha linaraṅan iŋ huwus praƀu,
lwiṙ padmâsana siṅha rūpa ni sakanya kumĕñar abirū paḍâkiris,
kasraŋ de ni sĕnö nikaŋ kanaka paṅhatĕp apituwi söḥ mađubrata,
sākṣāt rātri winĕtwan iŋ wulan awā linĕṅĕṅakĕn i śabda niŋ cucuṙ*

ṅkā dewī winaraŋ lawan saṅ aja māṙ hati nira rumaras paḍâwĕnĕs,
ry-antuk saŋ mamaraŋ maraŋ ri sira kāri sira kadi mađubratâsana,
maṅke pwa n tumĕmu ŋ prayojana ni rāga nira malawas aṅhiḍĕp smara,
kady-âṅipy-aṅisapwakĕn wulan awâmbĕk ira n aṅisapu nrĕpātmajā*

śrī dewîndumatī miṅe tan anumoda ri palaku ṅ asiḥ nrĕpātmaja,
heman luḥ nira maṅlĕtuḥ lĕtuhi soca nira kadi saroja kābunan,
moǥanya pwa mayat mayat halis irârĕṅu rĕṅu kaharas wawaŋ tikĕl,
tan pātmā kinisapwakĕn twas ira tan pajajamuga rĕmĕk sakê taṅan*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ lod lĕyĕp niŋ wukir inayu papaṅgiḥ nirârok piniṇḍa,
kālaṅkyaŋ mwaŋ rĕrĕb waṙṇna nira kadi liraŋ kāmukan saṅhub awrā,

dewī dewâṙdđanārīśwara patĕmu nira lwiṙ ṭikâkarwa karwan*

saŋ kady-ânaṅga māry-âtanu mijil atĕmaḥ rājaputrâdwitīya,
maṙmmâpet siḥ tan imbâmĕkul aṅamĕr amĕṙ cumbu cumbw-âṅalap soṙ,
sotan ta ŋ wwaŋ riris kāṅinan apĕnĕd arūm paṅhilaŋ rāgabahni,
pömpöman rāsika lwiṙ nira paliḍah iṅ elik miṅe riŋ kisapwan*

mambö sub niŋ smarâṅde huyaṅ i hati nirâwaṙṣih apriḥ rasanya,
sumyuk taŋ rāgawaṙṣâṅapitu makĕcĕhan lagy-awantö raras twas,
Atruḥ truḥ haṙṣacittâmarupuhi turidâwaḥ wahan sanmatâgöŋ,
trĕṣṇâṅumbaŋ lawan siḥ manis iṅ ujar arūm saṅsayâdrĕs hilīnya*

<jagadđita>

saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ ni laṅöku māwak aśarīra mĕtu ri paṅaweśa niŋ smara,
lwiṙ dewī sakalânurun bĕsur i rāmya niṅ amĕṅ amĕṅ iŋ surālaya,
lakṣmī niŋ nagarī turuŋ matĕmahan karika kita wiśāta lālana,
saŋ sākṣāt pratimâṅaraŋ hulun anugrahana tariman aṅharas pipi*

ṅūnî kāla nikaŋ swayambara mijil kita kadi wijil iŋ niśākara,
sakweḥ saŋ pininaŋ praƀāwa nira söḥ murub aṅabar abaṙ tĕkêŋ laṅit,

pet pet rāga mamanwa manwa mamĕpĕṙ mĕpĕr ataña ri mūlya niŋ tapiḥ*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 20

śrîndumatī kakĕnan wiṣa niṅ ujar arūm sumusuk ri hati,
ndan kadi tan huniṅā pawulatan ira moǥa mahâpi hade,
rwā ŋ katahā n uduhĕn brituha wilaja hetu nirâpi tulak,

maṙmma nirâwri lanâkiput awĕdi kasiṅkaba siñjaṅ ira,
tan huniṅan tinañan lara ni wĕtu ni luḥ nira niṣkaraṇa,
nora waneḥ paran iŋ manah apĕga kumöl winisik wisikan,
ṅhiŋ panamantara ri sru saṅ aja winiweka nirê twas ira*

sāma paran wĕnaṅânulaka ri pamĕkulnya tan eraṅ amĕl,
dāna paran ta kunaŋ wĕnaṅ anuculanê paṅagĕmnya tapiḥ,
ƀeda paran wĕnaṅanya kumawaśakĕna bwat i rāga nira,

suṅsut irê nrĕpaputra hana kadi gula drawa de niṅ ĕbun*

<jagadđita>

Ꜽ koŋ ƀrānta kasop i luḥ niṅ aṅaraŋ kasarik i laṭi niŋ wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
lĕŋlĕŋ denta mulat piliḥ winawa niŋ turida sinaput iŋ hyaṅ iŋ ṭikā,
rūm niŋ śabda mameka sambĕt i gĕluŋ kari kita pati jumput jumputi,
dentâṅol midĕr iŋ tĕṅaḥ kapana yan warasa kadi panumpal iŋ smara*

siṅgiḥ ƀrānta kakanta māsku mapa don iṅ aṅasag inawenta lĕŋlĕŋa,
twaskw-apriḥ binĕbĕdta riŋ tali gĕluŋ cinucuk i luṅid iŋ matâluru,

Aṅhiŋ prāṙŧana moǥa sidđa katĕkāna silih usapa luḥ lawan kita*

Intaṙ haywa marĕk paran karika donta paran iku kināṙyya niŋ marĕk,
tan siḥ rāga nimitta niŋ taṅis adoḥ tiki kakĕnana kapriyambadan,
lāwan tan suꝁa hetu niŋ luh aṅasapta ri mata tuwi tan gawe gawe,
luḥ luḥ duḥka luh i ṅhulun taṅi taṅis prihati karaṇa niŋ lanânaṅis*

nāhan de nrĕpaputrikânulak i sāhasa saṅ aja saranta riŋ prĕman,
tan paṅde wĕdi riŋ kĕdö marĕk aṅol nĕhĕr aṅarĕki de nirâṅucap,
maṅkin haṙṣa rinĕṅwan aṅlalu kasuṅsutana saṅ aja saṅsayâwawuḥ,
śrī putrī sira kāpĕsan ri panulak nira jaja wĕkasan sirânaṅis*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

Adawa n panukĕṙ saṅ ahayu kadi tuhwa nĕhĕṙ miṅaya,
Anaṅis kadi tan patĕmahana lulut pwa ri suṅsut ira,
Aṅĕsaḥ kadi tan silih asiha mĕne ri huwus niṅ ulaḥ,
Anulak ri sĕpaḥ nrĕpasuta kadi tan pamalakwa hĕlĕm*

Atukup taliṅâwĕdi katĕkana rūm niṅ ujaṙ kinire,
susu tan winĕḍaṙ wĕḍar awĕdi kakukwa ragĕt ragĕta,
Akĕmul kĕmul epu ri pĕpĕsa ni mađya nira n pinĕkul,
Asaput muꝁa kady-awĕdi hilaṅa rūm nira kārĕkana*

mĕtu kady-asirat sirata maṇik ujaṙ nira maṙmma dahat*

<jagadđita>

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

nāhan wĕtu ni turida rāga rakryan aja māwak ucapan amanis,
An sāhasa sira kahanan wĕlas ri panaṅis nrĕpawaraduhitā,
Om yan humĕnĕṅa sakarĕŋ maṅantyakĕna rāga nira saṅ anukĕṙ,

Aṅlampw-anaṅis aṅĕsĕsan paṅewala narendrasuta tinarima*

<jagadđita>

Utpāta nrĕpaputra riŋ śayana moǥa tĕka ri papupul nirêŋ jinĕm,

Olaḥ lwiṙ bubula ŋ tilam pakĕdal iŋ wĕtis amijilakĕn larap larap,

<wīralalita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

śrîndumatī huwus kawawa māṙ gupe kawĕnĕsan,
mĕṅgah awuṅw-anoliha paran tikāṅ inusapan,

<Udgatawisama>

⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏓ = 13

dumunuŋ sirêña nira kālih uwa nira kapaṅgih iŋ nataṙ,
muṅgw-i patiga niṅ aśoka liman,
Akĕmit lawan kaka kakâmajaŋ wulan*

tumuluy kataṅgamaṅ anuṅsuṅ iña nira wawaŋ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mojar uwa nira marĕk manuluŋ,
Ibu kölakĕn ṅhiṅ ika de nikâṅlare*

wihikan ṅhulun ri lara niŋ gati kawawa tinambay iŋ priya,
sor ibu lara lara niŋ kawĕlad,
kasahasraƀāga lara niŋ matâpĕpĕḥ*

Anulis ṭikā dinudutan puḍak ibu lara niŋ minaṅkana,
lwiṙ hrĕbuk aṅalilipi ṅrĕs ikā,
Aṅinaŋ sĕrĕḥ lĕgĕ paḍanya riŋ pĕḍĕs*

I kapiŋ rwa niŋ gati wĕnaŋ rinĕṅihakĕn ikaŋ larâhaṅan,
yan huwus alawas apöm akule,
Alilaŋ laranya kadi mukṣa riŋ tapiḥ*

tuhan i ṅhulun muliha rakryan alah ibu waluy parêŋ jinĕm,
tolihĕn alal ira saŋ kawĕkas,
mulat iŋ lawaŋ mapaga rūmta riŋ guyu*

Araras wuwus ny-uwa nirâṅlipu lipur i manaḥ nrĕpātmajā,
moǥa winawa nira riŋ kalaṅön,
lara niŋ hañaṙ kawawa riŋ pasaṅgaman*

sira saŋ kinon maluya tan paṅucap arĕṅu hewa suṅkawa,
kāṅĕn aṅĕn ulah ulaḥ saṅ aja,
kamatolihĕn tuhun arĕs kapiṅrwana*

wĕkasan hinĕmbanakĕn iŋ kaka kaka mara riŋ pasaṅgaman,
gaṙjjita saṅ aja sawet niṅ alal,
mĕtu kapriyambadan i de nirâṅucap*

<jagadđita>

yak maty-âku dĕlönta māsku palalun makahawana hayunta gĕgwana,
Ūṙṇnā nūpura ƀūṣaṇanta katĕkāna tĕmahana ni janma ni ṅhulun,

Aṅgon denta ri kāla niŋ piniḍuḍuk mapa rasa rasa niŋ sinanmata*

tan heꝑepĕn aƀūṣaṇâpan anukĕṙ nukĕri laku pataṅkis iŋ kale,
prāyâṅrup tĕka kaṙṇnaśūla niyatâmuhara tuna ni de niṅ aṅrĕṅö,
kaṇṫâṅrĕs tĕkap iŋ kaluŋ kaluṅ ikaŋ payuṅ aṅadĕg adĕg hanêṅ adoḥ,

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

nahan ujar ira mambö rāgânūta ri saṅ aja,
lukar i tapih irâsowe keṅkab hinĕnĕṅakĕn,
wahu sumahur anū de maṅke yan tinaña tañan,
mari luh ira kumĕmbĕŋ wahw-âweḥ maṅarĕkana*

nrĕpatanaya kasĕṅkwan rāgâmaṙppĕki sumaput,
Amahawas isi niŋ ken sāmpun waspada kaharas,
Aṅamĕr amĕr amakpak wruḥ ry-ambĕk niṅ aṅĕsaha,
lwir anadaki kĕnêŋ hrū maṙmmâṅrehi tan asarag*

ri huwus ira kapiṅrwan saŋ śrī niŋ tulis aṅaraŋ,
lara nira mahĕli prīty-âluŋluŋ hyun aṅalaya,
manah ira wahu tūtūt kālap de nrĕpatanaya,
turida nira kahĕnti mwaŋ siḥ niŋ hati kapulut*

paṅusĕṅ ira ri lambe lambe tan tĕka ri hati,
panĕpak ira huwus mūṙ mukṣâṅdohi taṅan ira,
mari marĕṅu tumiṅhal tuŋtuŋ niŋ halis alaris,
manis i guyu nirâṅdyun wruḥ giṅgaŋ wahu kasiṅī*

saṅ ahayu sira molaḥ maṅlaḥ laḥ kumĕda kĕdal,
saṅ aja sira sumuṅkĕm tan paṅle kumuru kurub,
paḍa kumĕsĕk iṅ ambĕk tan kewrān awuda wudā*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

riŋ krāban kalasā mijil sira sumaṅgraha wali nira pūṙṇna tan kuraŋ,
sāmpun kewwan irânaḍaḥ sira pĕnuḥ sama marĕk i sira wwaṅ uttama,
ramyâtiṅkah atūt paluṅguh ira saŋ huwus agati wineh akarwana,
Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira muꝁya pinituhu paḍa wruh iŋ krama*

ṅkānê sor apupul paḍâruhur iṅ ambĕk aruhu ruhuran paḍâṅaliḥ,
Ewĕḥ tan kawĕnaŋ tiniṅkah aputĕk saṅ amahayu makon atiṅkaha,
de ni kweḥnya wiwal paḍâwyahata budđi nika puji puji n pakawwaṅan,
siŋ sor uṅgwan ikânĕsĕl ri saṅ aniṅkah inucap ika tan wruh iŋ krama*

<sragđara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ = 21

wet wet niŋ brāhmaṇâtyanta wĕkas iṅ aruhuṙ kadwijāṅśan ginöŋnya,
wet niŋ śꜽwaṙṣy-aluṅgw-î nĕhĕr apuji kaƀasmāṅkuran mūlya denya,
wet niŋ bodđâdwitīya n rumĕja rĕja kabudđāṅkuran kāraṇanya,
tan tuṅgal māṙgga niŋ kādyan asĕmu hawan iŋ muṅgah iŋ paṙwwatāgra*

wwaŋ wruḥ riŋ lokikācāra sĕḍĕṅ iṅ anaḍaḥ tan kawoṙ woṙ manaḥnya,
denyâbudđy-âmanis mĕṅgĕp upaśama tinon mewĕh olaḥ tiniṅkaḥ,
Aṅdoḥ tan saṅgrahêṅ uṅgwan aruhur alĕmĕḥ worĕn iŋ tan kaśudđi,
maṅgā muṅgwêṅ asoṙ ndan yan apupul atatā sabrayârok sahāṙyyan*

guṇḍik rwa-rwâpupul tan wĕnaṅ apasah adoḥ de ni göṅ iŋ pamitran,
kady-âkarwan swarūpanya paḍa paḍa siliḥ mūla tuṅgal pināliḥ,
solaḥ seṅĕṙnya mogâṅinaki ri panunasnyêŋ tuhan sāri sāri,
denyâniṅkaḥ ry-awaknyâṅruhuri rinuhuran rāmya sawyāpasawya*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

paḍânaḍah akālihan sama kinon marĕka suꝁa linawwa lawwakĕn,
sawaŋ hudan atöb tibêŋ bañu kĕcap niṅ apupul amaṅan rinĕṅwakĕn,
marĕk sahana niŋ magoṣṫi humĕnĕŋ rumasa rasani paŧya niŋ rasa,
tuhun kasĕrĕtĕn jugâṅucap aminta paluṅan atĕkĕm jajâsĕgu*

lariḥ lumari tan pararyan alaris ri katahapan ika n hanâtulak,
surâsira siran rasanya surasârĕbu rĕbu sumĕḍaḥ kinahyunan,
maṇik pinakajaṅga tan papĕgatan kucur ika kadi pañcuran juruḥ,
kilaŋ brĕm inalap ginanti kadi tīṙŧa mađu mamulakan sakêŋ gĕḍaḥ*

paḍâlap alapan tahap sama marĕk wija wijah awĕrö girahyasĕn,
Apintiga hanan papiṅpat aṅigĕl katĕkan urak aganti tan bĕsuṙ,
Ikaŋ wwaṅ atĕrĕḥ manaḥnya kĕna riŋ sayub ahaṅan agasyak iŋ saƀā,
putus mar atĕṅö para mpu bini moǥa salah ĕluk ulaḥ nirâḍake*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

strī niŋ śꜽwa tan eraṅ eraṅ aṅigĕl kaguyu guyu wĕrö wĕrö dawā,
tan haṙṣêŋ swara niŋ mrĕdaṅga salukat ṅuni ṅuni yan i gīta niŋ waneḥ,
hetunya n paṅiduŋ wijil niṅ ajiyaḥ sahuli hulih ikâṅrĕṅö rĕṅö,
sahtote praŧamā kiduŋnya n aṅawat midĕm aṅujiwat ambahan tayoḥ*

ḍaŋ hadyan tumurun gumanty-aṅigĕl oṅsil aṅawak akikat rumampayak,
ṅhiŋ kahyunya kiduŋ buwun ya kiniduŋnya n aṅalik alik endah iŋ saƀā,

giḥ giḥ puŋ ri kipaḥ ḍuraŋ diniwayūh amamati juga de nikâmbahan*

Endaḥ ƀāwa nikaŋ waneḥ saha kiduŋ midĕr aṅilagakĕn wwaṅ iŋ saƀā,
ndan strī niŋ widu rakwa moǥa kawatĕk sawaṅ acarita de nikâṅigĕl,

Ꜽg lĕs liŋnya nĕhĕṙ muliḥ matĕlasan maṅumik umik aṅañjalîŋ tawaŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

samantaji tibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu muliḥ nrĕpasuta kalawan suputrikā,
parĕŋ maṅadĕg iŋ nataṙ sira kabeḥ tumut aṅiriṅakĕn marê dalĕm,
paḍâmwit atatā wineḥ maṅinaṅârarĕm upaśama sādarâṅucap,
dwijāṅśa maduluṙ duluṙ maṅaƀiwāda para wiku marĕk maṅañjali*

gumanti para wālakâmuhun anĕmbah inuƀaya sināntwa riŋ guyu,
Ikaŋ baṇija lot amaṅkari panambah ika kawagĕdanya tan hilaŋ,
paḍâṅucap akon ahosana marêŋ jinĕm agawaya paṅhawin laras,
mulat saṅ aja ri priyā nira nĕhĕṙ gumuyu guyu midĕm suputrikā*

Aliṅgih atitiḥ pupū silih usap muꝁa sira ri huwus nirâdamu,
prahāsana narendraputra manĕcĕk nĕcĕki rahi ri kĕmbaṅ iŋ hawu,
baṅun harĕp aminta paṅkwakĕna söŋ ni paṅawaśa ni siḥ suputrikā,
paṅawruhana ken lukaṙ kadi mahâṅiṅin iṅin i manaḥ nrĕpātmaja*

<śiꝁariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ = 17

suꝁâsaṇḍiŋ saṇḍiŋ samaṅinakanêŋ citta ginawe,
sĕlaŋ mā Ꜽn pojaṙ saṅ aja mawaraḥ ry-antuka nira,
manaḥ dewī kagyat gyat asĕkĕl ikaŋ twas kapĕnĕtan,
kumĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕŋ luḥ nira mijil aṅeṙttambaṅ asayut*

sĕnĕŋ yan yogyê jöŋta wawarĕṅĕhĕn luḥku k anaṅis,
wiraṅrwaŋ de niŋ tan wĕnaṅ apasah i śrī narapati,
manĕḥ rakryan ndi n yogya kawĕkasa tan tūta ri kita,
mataŋnya n paṅheṙ ṅke kahuluna kĕnaṅkwê kita sadā*

yadin muṅgwêŋ siṅhāsana pakaratun yan kita harĕp,
katon tan trĕṣṇā śrī nrĕpati palakun kapraƀun ira*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 20

yogya wuwusta tuhun ṅhulun aharĕp aṅuṅsira wīṙyya guṇa,
ndātan adoha sakêṅ ibu parĕkĕn apan sira māsih anak,
göṅ i kaƀaktin iṅ apraƀu maṅipulu ri twas akon muliha,
ṅhiŋ kita māsku rumaṅkĕpana kahulunankw-i narāṙyya raǥu*

yan muliha prihawak ṅhulun ibu kita kāṙyya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,
tiṅhali kāsihan iŋ huwus akurĕn asiḥ mara tambaṅana,
yan waluyâku muwaḥ ri kita pira piraŋ tahunĕn ḍatĕṅa,
ṅhiŋ panaṅisku lawan kita linalu ri dūra nikaŋ palagan*

mwaŋ yan anuṅgaṅa riŋ raŧa lĕpasa madoha sakêŋ nagara,
brāhmaṇa sogata śꜽwa rĕṣi sira ta maṅgala niŋ lumaku,
söḥ bala śūra kuraŋ hawan aṅiriṅ arampak aṅambah alas,
śūnya hiḍĕpku yatan hana kita maṅisapwana minta sĕpaḥ*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

priya kahiḍĕp ujaṙttârūm kady-âmrĕta kasirat,
kunĕṅ amuhara kepwan ry-ambĕk ni ṅhulun alawas,
ya tan asiha kitânaṅsārâpujya tinutakĕn,
syapa ta taṅisanaṅkwa ṅhiŋ matyânaṅisi tawaŋ*

ya ta karaṇa niṅ aswī yan rakryan jĕnĕka siwin,
Iwĕh iṅ aniwi maṅheṙ siḥ niŋ hyaŋ ya ta tinahā,
Atilara kita luṅhâtiṅgal wanwa n alalisa,
ṅhiṅ anaṅisana ri śrī ƀoja mwaŋ nrĕpamahiṣī*

taham ibu taha rakryan maṙmmâsiḥ ṅhulun atuhan,
saꝑala pinakadewī tan wwaŋ len kadaṅ aparĕk,
sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ sakwan selwan adulura,
kita pinakahuripku n sekaprāṇa silih asiḥ*

manis i wacana rakryan sāmpun kagraha ri hati,
pinakapaṅanumānan ry-ambĕkta n tulus asiha,
sapara parana rakryan ƀaktyâkw-âṅiriṅi kita,
yadin anadina lampūn matyâśânuku riṅ awak*

ṅhulun ibu wihikan yan budđyantâwĕlas asiha,
Ika karaṇa niṅ aswī māsku n rowaṅa muliha,
nrĕpati raǥu katon gyā gyā ny-ambĕk nira mulata,
niyata papagĕn iŋ strī sāyođyā n kita ḍatĕṅa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

sāmpun māyu wuwus nrĕpātmaja lawan dewī nira n maṅkata,
ṅkānê wwit niṅ aśoka rambay anaḍaḥ prāpta ŋ madaṅgâṅhaḍĕp,
luṅhā ŋ kāla huwus hyaṅ aṙkka sumurup sanđyā masĕŋsĕŋ miraḥ,
mambö kasturi niŋ paturwan araras kady-âṅutus mañjiṅa*

Ambĕk niŋ paḍa haṙṣa sāmpun amatĕḥ riŋ rāga soluṙ lulut,
trĕṣṇêŋ saṅgama tan kawaṙṣihan apöm māywan raras riŋ prĕman,
yan līlā mijil iŋ nataṙ pinanasan de niŋ smarâṅras hati,
Oṅsil tuŋtuṅ ikaŋ halis jaruman aṅgyākĕn marā riŋ tilam*

sāmpun muṅgah aṅanti riŋ pasamayan saŋ hyaŋ hyaṅ iŋ pamrĕman,
maṙmmâsiḥ paḍa de nirâṅĕnahi rāga wruḥ ri tuṅgal nira,
A-rwa-rwan manaḍaḥ manis niṅ upadeśâtyanta riŋ rāsika,
nora ŋ saṅśaya riŋ rahasya winĕḍaṙ kāgĕm rasanyê hati*

saŋ raśmînayu niŋ smarâṅucap ucap riŋ pamrĕman tan bĕsuṙ,
sekaprāṇa sapakṣa tan wĕnaṅ adoḥ māsiḥ sađaṙmmâduluṙ,
