paṅliṅganya n anak sināđya nira masw-aswâmiƀāwêŋ tilam*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

I sāmpun iṅ ulaḥ kapintiga nikaŋ ǥaṭita kawalĕsan sirâturū,
Ikaŋ hulĕs adoḥ sakê sira lanā kawadal alulunan marêŋ dagan,
hanan pawuṅu sakṣaṇâlĕh akaraŋ hulu taṅan aharip suputrikā,
tapiḥ nira huwus lukaṙ kasarakat kahurup i basahan nrĕpātmaja*

huwus kalalu de nirâmrĕm asuwe paḍa tan umik aṅel asaṅgama,
Ikaŋ manuk anaṅhi riŋ ḍawuh ĕnĕm suꝁa muni maṅuyūyu riŋ taman,
cucuṙ taḍahasiḥ swaranya kawĕlas harĕp anaṅis i paṅlwaṅ iŋ wulan,
Ikaŋ mrak akakab munîŋ gupura lagy-amuṅu ri sira riŋ ḍawuḥ pitu*

paḍâsraṅ aṅajîŋ kulĕm sahana niŋ manuk anarawatâguṇêriya,
parañjaṅan aṅanti riŋ gagana paŧya tumiru tiru śabda niŋ pĕkiŋ,
I soṙnya hana caṅkiluŋ muni laki stry-asĕmu mamarahi ry-anak nikā,
syapêka ta kunaŋ paṅajyan ika maṅhuwusakĕn ika yan bisâṅaji*

Awuṅw-ajajar iŋ surambyan arahup nrĕpatanaya lawan suputrikā,
Anĕṅgah atis aṅharas harasakĕn susu saṅ ahayu maṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,
kataṅgamaṅ aṅolakĕn saṅ aja maṙmma maṅĕmuli nĕhĕṙ mamaṅkwakĕn,
pupū nira kasiṅgahan hulĕs i polah ira kasuluhan niśākara*

samaṅkana ni göṅ i rāga nira kālih aṅisapu lawan mamaṅkwakĕn,
taŧāpi sinamantaran manis i de nira ṅucap araras prahāsana,
saṅ adyah api hewa hewa tuhun ambĕk ira tumiliṅ iŋ karāsikan,
nrĕpātmaja mañumbu ñumbu mamibik tapih aharĕp i buṅkah iŋ tĕṅaḥ*

ri luṅsur i tapiḥ nirârukĕt ikaŋ luṅayan asĕmu luṅgah iŋ gaḍuŋ,
Ikaŋ gĕlaṅ ataṅkis iŋ wĕtis apiṇḍa mađukara marâhyun iŋ puḍak,
payođara lanâpipit kadi wĕdinya kaharasa ri tuŋtuṅ iŋ kuku,
Ikaŋ muꝁa sawaŋ wulan marĕk i wimba nira sĕḍĕṅ ira n sapamrĕman*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

maṅkin wrĕdđi wijil ni rāsika nira n pa-rwa-rwan iŋ pamrĕman,
nidrâcumbana ta pwa nitya ginawe maṅde suꝁê twas nira,

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

samantaji mijil hyaṅ aṙkka kadi raktakumuda sumĕkaṙ sakêŋ bañu,
wulan mari lumöŋ kagöṅan ahulap sumirĕp awĕdi tan wĕnaŋ mulat,
tĕkêŋ grahagaṇânusup nusup arĕs karahinana humöt paḍâkucĕm,
Ikaŋ wĕṅi huwus paḍĕm kadi hilaŋ pinĕjahan ira riŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu*

Ikaŋ ƀuwana kālapan wĕṅi baṅun jalađi karaṅ asat ḍasaṙ nika,

Urut saka satal kumĕṇḍĕṅ ajajaṙ paḍa paḍa kadi nāga maṅlayaŋ,

<puṣpacāpa> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓ = 20

ri wwit niŋ kayu pārijāta hana tīṙŧâlantaran wwad kucuṙnya,
tūsanyânalagâjajaṙ watu karaŋnyâgroŋ rinoŋ pañcuranya,
tampyak tampyakan iŋ wĕrĕḥ pamarigi lwiṙnya n patap de nikaŋ ṙyyak,
wwꜽnyâƀrā kadi saṙwwawaṙṇna ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ puṣpamāyā hanê jro*

ṅkā dewī marahup rahup sira yaŧālīlâṅuḍoḍâñawuk wwꜽ,
tan saḥ śrī naranāŧaputra maṅĕmit lwiṙ kumbaṅ aṅrakṣa kĕmbaŋ,
wruḥ riŋ cāmana pītrĕtaṙppaṇa satiṅkaḥ tiṅkah iŋ tīṙŧayātra,
mādĕg pūṙwwamuꝁâjajaṙ parĕṅ amūjâṅañjalî saŋ hyaṅ aṙkka*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

mantuk śīǥra marê dalĕm humatur i śrī ƀoja riŋ pamrĕman,
Akweḥ strī haji samƀramê tĕka nirâganty-âṅucap gaṙjjita,
maṙmma śrī parameśwarī mulat anuṅsuŋ cumbu cumbw-âṅucap,
Ī Ī śrī maṇik i ṅhulun sira ḍatĕŋ kāliḥ nihan liŋ nira*

śrī dewîndumatī parĕŋ sira manĕmbaḥ mwaŋ narāṙyyātmaja,
riŋ lampit hana siṅhacaṙmma humaḍaŋ kāna n pratiṣṫârarĕm,
saŋ nāŧa wruh i don ira n para wawaŋ śoka drawa twas nira,
Amwit sādara sopacāra saṅ ajânĕmbaḥ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

sĕmbaḥ niṅ aśaraṇa ri jöŋ narendra huniṅan parĕk i narapati,
Amwīta muliha satatâṅriwĕg riwĕgi tan bĕsur amaribini,
tan sĕṅgahĕn akalis i pāda saŋ praƀu pasaŋ kuhira pinahayu,
paṅgil wĕnaṅa dadaha riŋ raṇâṅharĕpa śatrukula yan iṅ ayun*

Om wruḥ ṅhulun ika mara hetu niŋ kahĕnĕṅan kapĕgan aṅucapa,
māsiḥ ṅhulun iri kita moǥa tan wĕnaṅ asiḥ karaṇa niṅ asĕkĕl,
maṅke n mulat iri kita tan palekan aṅĕḍap mulih analahasa,
wahw-âpupul alal alawas tĕka pwa kita sakṣaṇa wawaṅ apasaḥ*

pintaṅkw-i kita bapa sihanta tan kapalaṅâmipila riṅ agati,
saṅkan raray uwuh uwuh ūpamānĕn iṅ ulaḥ kasih arĕp alawas,
maṅke n marĕk iri kita sanmatan kawiguṇanya tan ucap ucapĕn,
Aṅhiŋ pakadaṅan i bapaṅku tolihĕn i māsku laki pakatalin*

nwam ny-ambĕk ika mĕṅĕ mĕṅö kalotakĕna denta kajugulan ikā,
tan wruḥnya riṅ aṅinakanê mulat pipili denta pituturi piṅit,
saŋkṣepa nika kita waśa pramāṇa guṇadoṣa nika wawarĕṅöḥ,
yadyastun iwĕṅ iwĕṅa riŋ hulun bapa manaḥnya palu palu waraḥ*

Atwaŋ saṅ aja sumahur apraṇamya rumuhun saha manis iṅ ujaṙ,
Ājñā nrĕpati rasa nirâwĕkas wĕkas akon silih asiha sadā,
sāmpun karĕgĕp i hati de patik haji minuṣṭi maṅinaki hati,
ṅhiŋ gānya n apasaha ri tan sih iŋ wiđi harĕp mulata riṅ alara*

Atyanta hĕla hĕla niṅ aṅrĕṅö wacana rakryan aṅinaki hati,
niṙwiǥna kita bapa tökêŋ sīnāđya wĕnaŋ Uṅsirĕn iṅ aśaraṇa,
śānti dwijawara ri bapaṅku kesyana tumirw-a narapati raǥu,
swasty-astu saha tanaya dāra māsku saṅ anĕmwa jayaꝑala sadā*

mwaŋ yan pawuwuha kita ǥāra pat lima sujanma wĕka wĕka ratu,

yogya n kalĕwihakĕna tan paḍan ꝑala nikâṅurati kahulunan*

saŋ lekan aṅucap apagĕḥ tuwin binisa kāraṇa niṅ amituhu*

nāhan paṅucap ucap ira lwir amrĕta hañaṙ mĕtu siniratakĕn,
maṅdadyakĕn i suꝁa narendraputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā,

ƀeda mwaṅ ujar amanis iŋ pralāpita namun rĕcĕpa rasa nikā*

kañcit paḍa tĕka maduluṙ sirêŋ pagaḍuhan marĕk i narapati,

wastrādi pinada pinadāti pādadara tan wuruṅ apan adadaṙ*

sāmpun sirâhyas asalin hima puṣpawaṙṣa,

ri sĕḍĕŋta siliḥ galah oliḥ,

śīǥrâdandan kinon de saṅ aja marĕka lumrā katon sañjatanya,
Āpan prāpta ŋ musuḥ sāhasa waragaṅ ikā krūra tan paṅgalaŋ twas,
sakweḥ niŋ śūra śūra ŋ watĕk aja kumutug söṅ ikaŋ krođabahni,

śrī magađāđipa sāhasa mijil aƀimāna nirêŋ palagan,
nāgamayāstra laras nira sĕḍĕṅ inayat ƀramita ŋ prĕŧiwī,
göŋ swara niŋ tali de ny-aṅin ika kumusuḥ mĕtu kātatakut,
hrū nika kādƀuta kātara gunuṅ ahĕlaṙ warakadga murub*

prajwalitāgni cucuknya kagiri giri đūma dilaḥnya murub,
sek gumuruḥ paṅawaknya kumisik amĕgat jaladêŋ gagana,
boṙ kumutug śara bajra saṅ aja kumĕtug lĕpas aṅdwiguṇa,
teg tumibā ŋ wihagācala mati pinanaḥ makĕbĕt kĕbĕtan*

muntab krođa saṅ aṅganāŧa kadi bahni maṅaraman i puñcak iŋ wukiṙ,
ṅkānê kūwara niŋ raŧâmahayu lañciṅan ira pinisit siniṅsĕtan,
hrū lāwan laras adwitīya sinamāđy-amijilakĕna saṙwwasañjata,
wuntw-îkaŋ gaganāntarāla tĕkap iŋ panah atip atĕtĕl turuŋ tibā*

dewanyâwurahan tĕkâṅamah amaḥ harĕp amususa riŋ nrĕpātmaja,
lwiṙ meǥodaya māǥamāsa sumaput pĕtĕṅ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
saŋ hyaŋ bāywanala pracaṇḍa pamanaḥ nrĕpatanaya dumeḥ kawaṅsula,
bĕk gĕk toṙ cĕrĕcĕb tibêŋ bala nareśwara makasulayaḥ kawaṅsulan*

śaktîŋ praŋ saṅ awantināŧa sira mrĕtyu sakala yan i mađya niŋ musuḥ,
maṅgĕḥ budđi nirâpuliḥ nĕhĕr aṅakw-amĕjahana nareśwarātmaja,
rāhasyântya nikaŋ kaśaktin inayat nira mĕtu ṅ ayuđâgnipaṙwwata,
boṙ muṅgw-iŋ gaganāntarāla paḍa yatna bala saṅ aja kebĕkan panas*

tan kewran saṅ ajâpan adƀuta kaśaktin ira tumiru śakti saŋ raǥu,
rĕp mārāđana pañcabāyu mĕtu kātaratara gumĕrĕḥ magĕnturan,

ƀuṙ tog söŋ prĕkĕtĕk nahan swara nikâmĕkasi hurip i mađya niŋ tasik*

maṅsö sāhasa tan surud saṅ anupāđipati manah ira n wanîŋ raṇa,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda len grit iŋ raŧa karĕṅw-asĕlur i hiriṅan hanê harĕp,
pakrak niŋ balasaṅǥa maṅgyat aṅasut ri bala saṅ aja wāni kāmbulan,
teg tok lwiṙ garuḍâḍahĕm kĕtug ikaŋ gubar asahuran apratiđwani*

sāmpunya n lumĕpas panaḥ saṅ anupāđipa kadi ruga ṅ aṇḍamaṇḍala,

byuṙ laṙ lĕs paḍa mukṣa de ni kuku saŋ garuḍa wahu minuṣṭi riŋ laras*

krođâmbĕk saŋ susenā saha bala sumaput kātarâsiṅhanāda,

Āpan pakṣy-âhĕlaṙ sañjata kadi garuḍâneka seww-aṙwwudâhöm*

perat sok raḥnya saṅkêŋ ḍaḍa nika kawutaḥ mrĕm tibâdoḥ gumĕntĕṙ*

saŋ pāṇḍya soṙ titih alaḥ malayū tinaṅkis,

śīǥrânurumbunuh amūk ri narendraputra,
Atyadƀutâlimunan iŋ gaganāntarāla,
mĕttâṅuliŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukūs umaṇḍĕm,

kāla nrĕpātmaja n inambulan iŋ gajendra,

meww-îwu hĕnti mati śīǥra parĕŋ tumĕmpĕk,

prodƀūta kātara dahat patĕmunya kāliḥ,

sāmpun byakta kacakrawaṙttyan i nrĕpātmaja ri huwus irâmarājaya,

meḥ meḥ rwaŋ puluhaŋ kulĕm lawas irâṅhinĕp i huwus irâpraṅ iŋ hĕnū,

<wikrĕti>

tĕwĕknya n inalap ni rena nika tan tahu katĕmu gĕnĕp tigaŋ tahun,

nāhan wastu ni de nirâṅikĕt ikĕt winĕkasakĕn irêrikaŋ yaśa,
prajñā śrîndumatī sirâmaca kapintiga tama tumurun sirâduluṙ,

sāmpun rakwa gĕnĕp salek lawas irêŋ hawan asuꝁa suꝁan dudū gawe,

Aśrī denya mawâmbĕk abwat atĕrĕḥ tumiru tiru manaḥ suputrikā*

Akweḥ rājasutā ry-ayođyanagarī mada makapaṅayāya rūm nikā,

mrĕm tan löŋ kadi wintaṅ iŋ wĕṅi katon akucĕm i kĕñar iŋ niśākara*

Āpan kādƀuta siŋ sapolah ira kāƀinawa ri haliwat nirêŋ lĕbuḥ,
sakweḥ kweḥ para taṇḍa söḥ parĕṅ anuṅsuṅ i sira paḍa haṙṣa gaṙjjita,
Abyūṅan kumisik garantuṅ ira rāmya kadi papagut iŋ ṙyyak iŋ pasiṙ*

ṅhiŋ dewînalĕm iŋ mulat syapa ta taṇḍiṅa nira liṅ ikânulus dahat,
yadyan sewu purī pametana mamaṙppatana hajĕṅ ira ndatan hana,

byakta śrîndumatī pakapraƀu nirêŋ śayana pisaniṅū katampika*

nā liŋnya n paṅalĕm katuhwan apa tan hana kadi sira ratnakanyakā,
Āpan saṙwwa sĕkaṙ suganđa makanāyaka pĕnĕd i raras ni rūm nira,

linolya rinasan manisnya winiweka winaca waca de nareśwarī*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rakryan riŋ lĕpihan taṅisku k aṅaraŋ waca lĕburĕn i luḥta yan tama,
rĕsku n kawruhana n siliḥ kirim ujaṙ tinĕkakĕn i huwusta medĕman,
maṅke n prāpta muwaḥ suwalta sipi wiṣṭi nika katĕṅĕrâmabak puḍak,
yadyastun ṅwaṅ apaṅgihâwaka palambaṅ ibu kadi wuruŋ hana ŋ ƀaya*

rakryan yan priya rakryan aṅluruga māsku tumuta kita muṅgwa riŋ raŧa,
tan wismrĕtya kitêŋ tĕgal pacaru luḥ yat atutur i kasiṅhan i ṅhulun,
pañjiṅkw-iŋ kakawin taṅis taṅisananta ri hati yak araryan iŋ yaśa,
lambaṅkw-îbu wunin rasanya hiḍĕpĕn ṅhulun aṅisapu maṅruwat prĕman*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

nahan rasa nikaŋ palambaṅ alabuḥ saṅ ahayu sira moǥa kasrĕpan,
prapañca hiḍĕpan sirê carita niŋ kakawin inayu rāgawādaka,
sumaṅśaya ri budđi saŋ praƀu makolah iṅ ulah ika hetu niŋ wiwal,
miṅe musapi luḥ nirâṅisĕk isĕk tinañan api kapĕñcir iŋ kuku*

prahāsana narendra rakwa wihikan ri karaṇa ni wuyuŋ nareśwarī,
sumatya ri laṅö nira n paṅikĕta ry-awak ira nĕhĕr aṅdilat pupuṙ,
Amaṅkwakĕn ameri luḥ tuhu tuhu n kawi siṅ ulah ira n tĕkâmanis,
raras raras i kapriyambadan irâṅhari hari saha luḥ mawoṙ taṅis*

yayī mapa panĕmwanaṅkwa kadi māsku hayu saꝑala rājaputrikā,
yadin susupanêŋ sahasranagara triƀuwana kapana n kapaṅgiha,
hyaṅ iŋ kusuma sūkṣma tan wĕnaṅ aṅiṇḍarat awĕdi tumon kitêŋ taman,
tulis kanaka tan kĕḍap kadi kapūhan aṅaraṅ alara n sinorakĕn*

tĕwĕk niṅ akurĕn lawan kita kakanta karakĕtan amaṅkwakĕn laṅö,
hirĕŋ siṅ ulah iŋ karas kapana yan paṅalapana rarasta riŋ prĕman,
lulutkw-i jarijinta riŋ kapana yan kawaśa taruhĕn iŋ tanaḥ garuŋ,
sĕkaṙ pisaniṅūn panampikakĕna n hana kita ri kisapwan i ṅhulun*

ṅhulun ratu niraṙŧa kady-usaṅ amak ri papaḍa nika sūṙyyawaṅśaja,
sih iŋ hyaṅ aṅiriŋ ri siḥta riṅ anāśraya pinupu ri laywan iŋ puḍak,
manaḥta kapalaŋ tuhun siha ni māsku pamuhun i kakanta tiṅhali,
Unĕṅku ri raras rarasta yayi saṅwa niṅ ajar ajarêŋ wanāśrama*

Ujaṙ saṅ aja mātra maṙmma rinasan tuna tuna mamĕlas mĕlas harĕp,
nimitta ni manaḥ narendramahiṣī wĕdi kaluputanê nareśwara,
hilaŋ taṅis irâtĕmaḥ gĕrĕh arūm luh ira sumĕmu riŋ hudan muliḥ,
Aminta sĕpah esi de nira mulat kadi mawarah i hĕnti niŋ lara*

<śiꝁariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ = 17

lipuṙ suṅsut saŋ lwiṙ śaśađara lumiṅsiṙ karĕrĕban,
parĕŋ mantuk hinrĕt ni pakusikan iŋ cāmara mure,
I siṅgroŋ siṅgroŋ niŋ watu hawan irâlok trĕbis arĕs,
siliḥ tuntun ṅkānêŋ juraṅ arupit awwat wwad alĕyö*

guhā lambuŋ tistis kalĕṅĕṅan ikâwaṙṇna siluman,
Asĕp ri jro lāwan sarasija pamūjā mrik awaṅi,
kukus lagy-amrĕg tawwan aliwĕran iŋ ketaka mĕkaṙ,
bañunyânūt rĕṅkā ni muꝁa nika sumyuk manutupi*

sudewī līlâpiṇḍa wayaṅ adĕgan muṅgu ri dalĕm,
manaḥ saŋ swāmi prīti maṅudaṅ udaŋ santĕn arupit,
Anāntwâṅlīlâñumbana kinĕliran wwe kadi jamaŋ,
kiduŋ lālityârūm hawan ira muliḥ rāmya tumurun*

huwus prāptêŋ kalpadruma pinarigîŋ ratna kinaraŋ,
turuŋ mampĕḥ sub niŋ hariṅĕt aṅĕbun tūsnya ri jaja,
Aganty-aṅdĕmwan dĕmwani muꝁa tan imbā silih usap,
gĕluŋ mury-âtöb lāgi pinĕpĕkakĕn mwaŋ karatala*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

An kāmīrasa saṅgamênulahakĕn narapati kalawan nareśwarī,
wwantĕn paṙwwata riŋ pasiṙ tĕpi kidul hinĕmukan i kukus niṅ ampuhan,
riŋ gokaṙṇna ṅaranya rāmya kahujuŋ saray i suku nikâmĕgat harus,
ṅkā n līlâmĕṅ amĕŋ ƀaṭāra mihat iŋ timi wijah aṅalūŋ hanêŋ tasik*

kāla dyaḥ hariṇī śināpa ri pamiǥna nika tapa madadya mānuṣa,
mogâsiḥ wĕkasan dwijaṙṣi trĕṇawindu ri panaṅis ikâmaṅun wĕlas,
ndan rakwânta ni śāpa saŋ rĕṣi sĕkaṙ sumanasa hawananya mantuka,
ndaḥ yêkī ginawe ƀaṭāra paramāṙŧa karaṇa nika don ikêŋ jagat*

saŋ saptaṙṣi sulakṣaṇâhalĕp asewa satata sira śuśruṣâguru,
ndān aṅhiŋ rĕṣi nāradâṅgupit inuttama tuwi kawi gīta suswara,
winwītan lalitâmanis tinĕṅahan raras inapi tinuṅtuṅan laṅö,
kālap citta ƀaṭāra mūṙcꞓita saśoka hati nira kalĕswan aṅrĕṅö*

lwiṙ strī stry-aṙjja kawîṅgitajña para gīta pawulatan i piṇḍa niŋ gupit,
ṅkānê tuṅgul ikā sĕkaṙ sumanasênikĕt asĕmu sadak hanêŋ gĕluŋ,
kady-ânumpiṅakĕn tanaḥ ri sĕḍĕṅ iŋ tabĕh inĕnah i tambaṅ iŋ waluḥ,
mwaŋ kady-âsidĕhâṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅih i pĕs ni lĕṅĕn ika lanā katiṇḍihan*

srĕṣṭi hyaŋ madanâtikaŋ sumanasa mrik inalap iṅ aṅin huwus lĕwas,
kāry-âśâlara piṇḍa niŋ gupit arūm sawaṅ anaṅis inambilan sĕkaṙ,
Akweḥ ṣaṭpada maṅrubuŋ milu katūt humuṅ aliwĕran iŋ naƀastala,
saŋ hyaŋ lek alaṅö lumöŋ sĕmu nikaŋ sumanasa ḍumawuḥ sakêŋ tawaŋ*

haṙṣa śrîndumatī mulat ri sĕkar iŋ sumanasa kadi tan pamatyana, 
Āpan de ni laṅönya kāṅinan amet ri sira katĕmu riŋ pasaṅgaman,
ndātan wruḥ sira yan sināđya ya ta hetu nira kahĕnĕṅan pijĕṙ maṅö,
ndaḥ yêkī karaṇanya śīǥra tumibā ri jaja nira kasuṅsaṅ iŋ susu*

ndātan wyaṙŧa ḍawuḥnya māti sira denya tuhu wĕkas i śāpa saŋ rĕṣi,
mrĕm tan sāra tibê kisapwan i wulat saṅ aja milu tibā sirâpupul,
kāliḥ māti sirêŋ tilam tuhun uđāni saṅ aja wĕkasan sirâṅliliṙ,
Akrak taŋ sakaḍatwan aṅgyat adadak taṅis ika ri pĕjaḥ nareśwarī*

göŋ niŋ duḥka kaƀukti de saṅ aja tan papaḍa wĕkas i tībra niŋ lara,
kāla śrîndumatînalap ni sĕkar iŋ sumanasa mulih iŋ surālaya,
kāry-aṅhol śawa koŋ pinakpak inamĕṙ tinañan ira tĕhĕṙ pinaṅkwakĕn,
rĕñcĕm twas nira hetu niŋ luh aṅasapta kalara lara de nirânaṅis*

rakryan saŋ lumah iŋ kisapwan ahurip karika kita mĕne n maliḥ yayi,
haywântĕnkw-asuwe pĕjaḥ yayi tutuṙ tutur ibu paṅucap kitê ṅhulun,
heman māsku śawanta tiṅgalakĕnanta sĕḍĕṅ ahayu kāsih i ṅhulun,
maṅkin rūkṣa tuhanku tan patuluṅan dudut aku ta duluṙ duluṙ pĕjaḥ*

prāṇaṅkw-indumatīṅku māsku pawuṅu ndak amalaku sĕrĕḥ lawan pucaŋ,
Aṅgy-aṅgī saha pastikêbu palakuṅkwa muwah i kita haywa tâsuwe,
Agyâweha sĕpaḥ sakê waja kakanta yayi ri kita māsku paṅliliṙ,
siḥ sihkw-î kita tan pahīṅan ibu sugyan asĕbĕla hatinta yan pĕjaḥ*

maṅke n tan pakakāraṇa ŋ lara patinta pĕjah i taṅan i ṅhulun kita,
t asy-âsiḥ pawaraḥ ri doṣa ni kakanta karaṇa niṅ atiṅgal i ṅhulun,
paṅheṙ māsku waluy muwaḥ ri śawa rakryan apa hamĕṅanaṅkw-inaryakĕn,
suŋsuŋ wāhu ḍatĕŋ kisapwakĕn anakta si daśaraŧa māsku hĕmbanĕn*

karwânakta karîŋ kaḍatwan aku denta yayi kadi linad twas i ṅhulun,
sambatnya n patañê nimitta ni patinta kawĕlas arĕp aṅgamĕl taṅan,
yâṅde syuḥ ni hatiṅku māṙ kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕṅ apĕga tan wĕnaŋ mulat,
Aṅhiŋ luḥku lawan taṅisku sahur i ṅhulun ibu ri kĕdö nikâtaña*

yêkī sambat irânaṅis kasih arĕp kaluputan i pĕjaḥ nareśwarī,
maṅgā matya matêṅ aṅölakĕna duḥka pamĕkas ira saŋ huwus pĕjaḥ,
maṅke n tiṅhal amaspadākĕn irikaŋ kusuma kasĕlaṅan taṅis nira,
de niŋ krođa lawan putĕk hati mijil paṅuman uman irêrikaŋ sĕkaṙ*

Ꜽ koŋ kĕmbaṅ apaṅkwa ko kuṭila kewala ḍumawuh amatya matyani,
denya n tan rujitĕṅkwa ko pĕjahi tâku saha bala sarājya hĕntyakĕn,
maṅke ko tumibê jajaṅku ri hatiṅkw-apa karaṇamu tan pamatyani,
sākṣāt ko wiṣapuṣpa dadyan i manaḥ niṅ aṅupĕt agawe prahelika*

lāwan deṅkw-anahā nahā ri dadimu n kusuma tĕmahan iŋ warāpsarī,
saṅkêŋ swaṙgga tĕkânurun harĕp aniwya ratu huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
ndātan haṙṣa n amaṙwwa hetumu n amatyani ri kasi kasiḥku putrikā,
riŋ śūnya n waluyâpsarī marĕka tan sah anilihana saŋ huwus pĕjaḥ*

nā de śrī naranāŧa mojar irikaŋ sumanasa sĕkar iŋ kadewatan,
sakweḥ saŋ rĕṣi śꜽwa sogata kapaṙccaya haji marĕk aṅlawad lawad,
mwaŋ ḍaŋ hyaŋ karuhun purohita nareśwara paḍa humatuṙ marê dalĕm,
niṙwiǥna ŋ rumöṅö pāwitra ni tāṅis taṅis ira paḍa wrĕdđāpaṇḍita*

<jagadnāŧa> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

sĕḍĕŋ tinaṅisan narendramahiṣī lumay awĕnĕs apan huwus pĕjaḥ,
taṅis nrĕpati rakwa mātra rinĕṅö nira tuna mamĕlas mĕlas harĕp,
nimitta nira n aṅliliṙ tutur irâmuhara wĕlas irê nareśwara,
Aṅiṅkin atalaṅkup amwit i nareśwara pĕjaha nĕhĕṙ maṅañjali*

praƀuṅku huniṅan taṅisku rasa mamwita pĕjaha ri jöŋ nareśwara,
hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥta tan tĕmu kaƀaktin ika pahalawö kita praƀu,
patikta kawĕlas harĕp syapa wiđin haji tumuta rumakṣa riŋ hĕnu,
Ahā haji waliṅku rāmya parĕṅâku pĕjaha kalawan kita praƀu*

narendra warahĕn ṅhulun ri paran iŋ mati tuduhakĕnanta riŋ hĕnū,
ndya taŋ hiḍĕpĕn i ṅhulun karaṇa niŋ maluya silih asiḥ lawan kita,
Apan kasi kasiḥta ratnawanitā juga tĕmahana ni ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,
sahasraśatajanma janma ni patikta huluna pakĕnaṅkwa de haji*

<Aṙdđasamacatuṣpadī>
– – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 11
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

trĕṣṇāṅkw-i nāŧaṅku mapôlahaṅkwa,
hilī ni luhtâkilayū hiḍĕpku,
Aṅrĕs hatiṅku n rumĕṅö taṅista,
Ay ay ṅhulun matya tuluŋ laraṅku*

swāmiṅku nāŧaṅku wĕkasku maṅke,
marĕk ri paṅkwanta cinumbananta,
Amwīta mūrâku sakê jajanta,
lalun patiṅku n lumah iŋ kisapwan*

yadyan kitâṅjanma muwaḥ dĕlāha,
tĕṅaḥku tan sāha sakê lĕṅĕnta,
haṙṣanta rokĕn kalawan lulutku,
Iruŋta sotpattya lawan pipiṅku*

nāhan taṅis śrī naranāŧapatnī,
rasâmĕlas haṙṣa tĕkap nirâmwit,
sāmpun sirâṅañjali satyaƀakti,
pĕjaḥ sirâgĕgwan i jöŋ narendra*

nitya prakampâmbĕt i mađya niŋ strī,
praƀāwa saŋ satya matî kisapwan,
truḥ truḥ luh iŋ śoka hañaṙ tinambaŋ,
kĕtug kĕtīg iŋ wahu wahw-apaṅgiḥ*

ƀakty-âtuhan dyaḥ jayaluḥ tumuṅkul,
mulat kapūhan ri pĕjaḥ sudewī,
tan samƀawā matya sirâpan anwam,
hiḍĕpnya ri twasnya nĕhĕṙ masambat*

Āḍā tuhankw-indumatīṅku māsku,
ṅhulun tuhan pun jayaluḥ kasiḥta,
yêki n humaṇḍĕm ri padadwayanta,
Asiŋ sapatyanta tumūta bela*

līlā tuhan pun kawidoṣa winwit,
maweḥ tumūtêka pĕjaḥta māsku,
Āpan katon milwa nipun dĕlāha,
namaś śiwāya n pĕjaha praƀunta*

patrĕm pabelan wulatîbu yêki,
Umigrahâtmā ni manĕḥta maṅke,
nāhan wuwusnya trus awaknya mūṙcꞓa,
pĕjaḥ tumūt satya ri jöŋ sudewī*

wahw-aṅliliṙ śrī naranāŧa meṅĕt,
Apan katuhwan lara niŋ kapatyan,
keṅĕṙ muꝁa śrîndumatī kalĕṅgak,
huwus katon līna yayan tinaṅhi*

Induŋ pawuṅw-îbu lihat kakanta,
Ikaŋ turū haywa ginöŋta māsku,
Āḍā pĕjaḥ kapwa tuhanku maṅke,
dumeḥ si tan paṅlilir an tinaṅhi*

Atyanta sihtêry-aku tan pahīṅan,
Ujaṙtta matyê kapatiṅku liŋta,
maṅke kitâniṅgalakĕn huripku,
waliṅku tuhw-âsiha miŧya māsku*

ṅhiŋ māsku māṙggaṅku suꝁêŋ kaḍatwan,
huripku tuṅgal kalawan huripta,
luṅhā pwa jīwanta sakê śawanta,
hilaŋ pwa jīwaṅku sakê hatiṅku*

nāhan śawa dyaḥ jayawaspa māsku,
tumūt awās bela tĕlas mapatrĕm,
swāminya lāwan tanayanya kāri,
laranya tuṅgal kalawan laraṅku*

nā de narendrâṅucap asrĕt ahrĕk,
mawoṙ taṅis luḥ nira maṅkin adrĕs,
ndan soca dewîndumatî tibānya,
paḍânaṅis rūpa nira n paḍâṅluḥ*

sāmpun śawa śrîndumatī pinuṇḍut,
sakê kisapwan saṅ ajâlupâwak,
mūṙcꞓā pĕjaḥ sakṣaṇa śīǥra meṅĕt,
tuhun sira glāna masū masambat*

Induṅku māskw-indumatīṅku paṅheṙ,
Ah aḥ yayi ndī parananta maṅko,
Āḍâlalis tan panahā laraṅku,
tuhanku toliḥ kawĕlas harĕpku*

nāhan taṅis saŋ praƀu māṙ rasanya,
tamuy nira prāpta mahāṙṣi wrĕdđa,
ndan rakwa saṅkêŋ ƀagawān wasiṣṫa,
narendra maswāgata sāṙjjawâtwaŋ*

kṣāntabya rānak mapa don mahāṙṣi,
ḍatĕŋ sĕḍĕŋ niŋ lara tan patambān,
saŋ paṇḍitâtaḥ karaṇanya marya,
prasidđa śudđāmrĕta saŋ munīndra*

<bramitākṣara> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏓ = 12

kṣama yogya de saṅ ahulun mataña,
ri ḍatĕŋ ƀujaṅga haji riŋ nagara,
ƀagawān wasiṣṫa maṅutus marĕka,
tumĕkākĕnôcapan irê nrĕpati*

haji rakwa haywa kalaran dahatĕn,
purih iŋ dadi n dadi kalotakĕna,
lara duḥka moǥa tumuwuḥ riṅ awak,
ya tikā prihĕn saṅ ahulun paḍĕmĕn*

suraputrikā kĕta saṅ indumatī,
suƀagêŋ triloka maṅaran hariṇī,
śuci rakwa janma nira śudđy-anulus,
sira dewatī niṅ araras pinuji*

ri sĕḍĕŋ dwijaṙṣi trĕṇawindw-atapa,
hana saṅśayê hyaṅ amarendra mulat,
I mahāpraƀāwa nira riŋ patapan,
tinahā nirâṅadĕha kendran ira*

Irikā ta rakwa sira saŋ hariṇī,
katuduḥ mamiǥnana tapâṅĕnĕsa,
I ḍataŋ nirêŋ patapan epw-aputĕk,
ƀagawān sirâsĕgĕ sĕgĕḥ ya masiḥ*

suraputrikâṅucapakĕn hyun ira,
marĕk iŋ dwijaṙṣi sĕḍĕṅ iŋ majapa,
Amahaywa kĕmbaṅ ira tan kasaha,
Atĕhĕṙ manaṅhuluha riŋ śayana*

<krĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏓ = 20

mawuyuŋ dwijaṙṣi wĕkasan rumasa rasani de nirâṅucap,
tumuluy śināpa nira tan waluya muwah i jöŋ surāđipa,
jĕnĕkêŋ manuṣyapada kewala matĕmaha janma mānuṣa,
Ujar iŋ wiśeṣapuruṣa pratiniyata tĕtĕpnya tan wuruŋ*

I ḍawuḥ ni śāpa ƀagawān sira kapĕgan ikêpu keraṅan,
Anaṅis nĕhĕṙ marĕk aminta tinurunan anugrahâṅĕdö,
ƀagawān mulat ri kawĕlas harĕp ira wĕkasan sirâwĕlas,
Ikaṅ antaśāpa sĕkar iŋ sumanasa paṅanugrahêrika*

<bramitākṣara> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏓ = 12

Irikā n pĕjaḥ ta sira riŋ patapan,
tumuluy prakāśa dadi rājasutā,
I widaṙbƀa maṙttyapada rājya nira,
kraŧakeśikendra makawīja sira*

pira taŋ tahun lawas irêŋ nagara,
mĕtu dewatī nira n arūm rumara,
sĕḍĕṅ iŋ swayĕmbara kināṙyya nira,
naranāŧa kahyun ira nora muwaḥ*

matutuṙ sirê sĕḍĕṅ ira n paniwi,
I narendra riŋ surapada n patĕmu,
dumadak pwa saŋ praƀu hilaŋ rumuhun,
dadi rājaputra sira rājasutā*

Akurĕn muwaḥ suꝁa tĕkêŋ karatun,
tĕka ṅ antaśāpa maṅutus muliha,
maluyê swajāti nira dewasutā,
tumibā ŋ sĕkaṙ sumanasâmĕjahi*

kaliṅanya saŋ praƀu hade kalarā,
kĕna saŋ pĕjaḥ mulih iṅ indrapada,
Apa tan wuruŋ haji matĕmwa muwaḥ,
kalawan sirêṅ amaraloka hĕlĕm*

nya wuwus mahaṙṣy-apitutuṙ I haji,
Ahĕbaŋ hĕbaŋ lara nirâtĕlasan,
Umuliḥ mahāṙṣi tumuluy kalaran,
pitutuṙ nirê saṅ aja rakwa tumūt*

<Aṙdđasamacatuṣpadī>
– – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ­⏓ = 11
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

sāmpun śawa śrîndumatī ƀinasmi,
murub siluŋluŋ nira ratnacetya,
maṅkin prapañca nrĕpati wyamoha,
wwaluŋ tahun kāla nira n katiṅgal*

<Udgatawisama>
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 20
– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ = 11
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏓ = 13

Irikā ta saŋ daśaraŧâṅadĕg anilihi kapraƀun haji,
budđi saṅ aja suꝁa haṙṣa mulat,
I kasiṅha siṅhan ira digjayêŋ jagat*

tadanantarêrika ta budđi saṅ aja siwuhĕn sirâlara,
monĕṅ i hayu saṅ aniṅgalakĕn,
mulih iŋ surālaya maluy surāpsarī*

<Atiśakwarī> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑­⏓ = 15

hana tīṙŧa niṙmmala wĕkas niṅ anindyaśuci,
I patĕmwan iŋ suranadī kalawan sarayū,
naranāŧa karwa kawidoṣa pĕjaḥ lumabuḥ,
mulih iŋ surālayapadântya pinaṅgih ira*

jayaluḥ dadi hyaṅ aṅaraŋ rumuhun katĕmu,
tumuluy kataṅgamaṅ anĕmbah i jöŋ saṅ aja,
Anaṅis nĕhĕṙ mulat i saŋ kawidoṣa marĕk,
Umucap lawasnya mapasaḥ mataṅis taṅisan*

parameśwarī haji sirâṅdadi dewasutā,
surarājya nandanawanāꝁya katĕmwan ira,
pinĕkul pinaṅkwakĕn aweḥ pipi wet niṅ unĕŋ,
Asalin śarīra paḍa māṙddawa rūpa nira*

saṅ apiṇḍa puṣpa tamuyan ƀramarâṅarĕki,
kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn sira mulat ri papaṅgih ira,
kadi tan patĕmwa muwah iŋ paḍa sūkṣma pĕjaḥ,
maduluṙ taṅis wara waraḥ nira maṙmma dahat*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

saŋ sākṣāt hurip i ṅhulun kawĕkas iŋ nagara ri sĕḍĕṅ i ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,
duḥkantê ruhun i ṅhulun mulih iṅ indrapada karaṇa niŋ lanânaṅis,
maṅke n prāpta paran tĕmunta kaka de ni kawĕlas arĕp i ṅhulun maṅö,
Aṅhiŋ luḥku panuṅsuṅaṅkwa tarimanta kaka wijil i rāga ni ṅhulun*

Induŋ tan sipi kapwa göṅ i lara niŋ huwus atĕmu rinudđa niŋ wiđi,
saṅsāraṅkw-aṅajap tawaŋ karaṇa niŋ ḍatĕṅ i kita katalyan iŋ hayu,
ndan maṅke n tĕka śūnyahasta yayi kewala ḍatĕṅ aṅisapw-aṅolakĕn,
Aṅhiŋ kūṅ ulih i ṅhulun saha taṅiskw-asĕkĕl i hati māsku sanmatan*

tonton ku n rumuhun pĕjaḥ karika hetu niṅ anĕmu larônĕṅ antya ya,
tontonĕn taṅan i ṅhulun ri kita yan panipati nĕhĕr aṅdĕlö mata,
mwaŋ tan kram waja ni ṅhulun kadi humeṙ kita masuṅa sĕpaḥ sakê waja,
milw-âkuŋ tĕṅah i ṅhulun kaka paṅawruhana lagi kaluṅsuran tapiḥ*

hāḥ swāmiṅkw-alawas dahat kita tan antuk iṅ amarapadâparan hineṙ,
mūṙcꞓâpriḥ ṅwaṅ aṅantyakĕn ri ḍatĕṅanta tumutura ri līna ni ṅhulun,
trĕṣṇantê suꝁa niŋ hanêŋ kabinihajyan amuhara lalista ri ṅhulun,
deṅkw-ânaṙkka ri tan tĕkanta tumuluy pilih aharĕp i patya ni ṅhulun*

Aṅkĕn rātri ri tambwaṅ iŋ wulan awā ṅhulun aṅaraṅ anaṅhulun puḍak,
de ny-ûnĕṅkw-i kitâṅutus taḍahasiḥ tumĕkakĕna taṅisku riŋ kulĕm,
kālaṅkyaŋ jarumankwa riŋ masa kapat ḍatĕṅa ri kita kāla niŋ rĕmĕŋ,
heṙ herĕn ri tĕkanta kewala kitâtiśaya kadi hinundaṅ iŋ patĕṙ*

lwaḥ luḥ wāđaka ni ṅhulun drĕs i hilī nika kadi minahâmĕgat hawan,
wwat goṅgaŋnya gaḍuŋ mure sĕkar ika mrik awaṅi sinaluṇḍiṅ iŋ puḍak,
luṅgaḥ niŋ katiraḥ lumuŋ pinakagĕgwan i tĕka niṅ aṅin kadînayun,
Aṅlaṅwākĕn ululnya puṣpa winaṅun hinĕduk i hĕlar iŋ mađubrata*

ṅkâku n ton kakawinta riŋ wĕla wĕlaḥ paḍa paḍa tinatā limaŋ wiji,
wwantĕn ṣaṭpada kanyakânaṅis i saṇḍiṅ ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun mulat,
haṙṣaṅkw-ânuculî talinya tumuluy kinisapu hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp kita,
tan pātmâkw-amacânaṅis katitisan luh araras ikaṅ akṣarâmanis*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ = 19

saṅ apiṇḍa mađubrata taruṇa manĕḥta sawaŋ salaga,
winaraŋ waraṅ iŋ masa kapat alaṅö kararas rarasan,
Irikā ta tuwuhkw-asana wawaṅ alum kita kāry-anaṅis,
maluyā sahanêŋ katiga kaka maran ṅwaṅ atĕmwa muwaḥ*

kaka yan kita lūha niṅ amaca wilāpa suwal piniṅit,
tĕmahaṅkwa taṅisnya winuni sinamaṙ samar iŋ kakawin,
yan adadyana ketaka kita tĕmahaṅkwa tulisnya ṭikā,
kaka de ni laraṅkwa pinasahakĕn iŋ wiđi niṣkaraṇa*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

wruḥ kw-î tan wĕnaṅanta đāraka kumölakĕna lulut unĕŋta ri ṅhulun,
wwat niŋ lwaḥ luh ariṅguṅan hawana saŋ praƀu tumutur i līna ni ṅhulun,
tiṅhaltê lara ni ṅhulun winaṅun akṣara rasa kakawin pralāpita,
byaktâdadyana luḥ tutuṙtta ri hatinta yak amaca ri lambaṅ i ṅhulun*

saŋ kārî nagari ndi siḥta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,
ry-antuk ni ṅhulun iŋ surālaya tĕwĕk niṅ anaṅis apasaḥ lawan kita,
kālanta n panulis karas mwaṅ aṅikiṙ tanah i kuku ya konĕṅ i ṅhulun,
kāpan swāmi muwaḥ ṅhulun warahananta kakawin anĕhĕṙ pinaṅkwakĕn*

lāwan pājara ni ṅhulun hana gaḍuŋ lumuṅ awarah i tiṅkah iŋ hĕnū,
makweḥ luŋnya hanan paṅulwan aṅaloṙ hana lumuṅ aṅidul ya tan tutĕn,
wwantĕn luṅgah ikâṅawetan amĕnĕṙ sĕkar ika kadi kĕmbaṅ iŋ laṅit,
Aṅhiŋ tūtakĕnanta riŋ gagana nandanawana tinujunya nora len*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 16

yayi rasa ni palambaṅtêkī māṙ ṅhulun amaca,
muwah inĕnahakĕnku ry-uṅgwanyâlawas alaṅö,
lumaku laku tumoliḥ rākantêbu karakĕtan,
pawarah ika tinūtkw-induŋ maṅke n tĕka ri kita*

tarima yayi paṅolkw-î rakryan kuṅkw-amarĕpĕhi,
syapa parana ni rāgaṅku n haṙṣaṅku katulaka,
hĕnĕṅakĕna taṅankw-âmet met moǥa kajĕnĕkan,
sapamalaku niṅ onĕŋ rakryan haywa pinihĕran*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

rakryan haywa kitâṅhĕmū guyu nĕhĕṙ miṅay amiru mirū tapiḥ lukaṙ,
rĕñcĕm twasku mulat raras paran ikā ṅaran ika lĕṅĕṅ aṅligā tĕṅaḥ,
ndan mogârĕṅu tan tulus waśa kita n paṅutu taṅan inambilan tapiḥ,
māskw-akras karikā manis manis i denta lumiriṅ anamaṙ linurwakĕn*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ = 22

nāhan paṅucap ucap irêŋ taman sinĕlaṅan prĕman uwat iṅ akuŋ,
saswaṙgga paḍa suꝁa tumon i rāmya ni papaṅgih ira silih asiḥ,
ṅūnî sĕḍĕṅ ira ratu cakrawaṙtti suꝁa niŋ ratu tinĕmu nira,
maṅke n suꝁa riṅ amaraloka maṅdaśaguṇê suꝁa nira mawa rāt*

riŋ nandanawana sira karwa raśmi niṅ asaṅgama hinarĕp ira,
riŋ pūṙṇnama mijil amaḍaŋ wulan sira marêŋ taman aṭika ṭikan,
riŋ swapna tuwi sira yayâmanĕḥ manĕhi rāga nira tan awanĕḥ,
kiṅkiŋ ni hati nira miniśra kāraṇa ni tuṅgal i turida nira*

riŋ nandanawana wĕkas iŋ kaŧā sumanasāntaka riṅ aji raǥu,
pinrākrĕta rasa kakawin tinīṙŧakĕn i jöŋ nrĕpati rasa laṅö,
siḥ kāraṇa nira n anumāna mājara rikaŋ paṅikĕt amanisa,
śudđāmrĕta warah ira hetu niŋ kadi gaḍuŋ lumuṅ anĕmu kapat*

<jagadđita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ = 23

sāmpun kekĕtan iŋ kaŧā sumanasāntaka winaṅun ahĕmbanan laṅö,
kāla śrîndumatī lawan saṅ aja mantuk iṅ amarapadâkurĕn muwaḥ,
yêkī tambay ira mpu monaguṇa milw-aṅikĕt ikĕt amaṙṇnana ŋ kaŧā,
ṅhiŋ śrī waṙṣajaya prasidđa guru niŋ guru laǥu sira hantusâmuruk*

dīṙgǥāyuṣya janapriyā saṅ amacâmahiḍĕpakĕna saŋ harĕp wruha,
niṙwiǥnâstu saŋ Aṅröṅö sakahārĕp nira katĕkanā moǥā sanmatan,
salwiṙ saŋ makapustaka ŋ sumanasāntaka kasihana de nareśwara,
sidđi mpuṅkw-i garuŋ tirun saṅ anulis katĕkana sasināđya saŋ wiku*
